Debt expenses: All repayment expenses of legitimate domestic and foreign debts borne by the central government that do not belong to official business operations belong to this category. Britain Actively Building Ships 55

Navy Budget Sharply Increased

Reuters reported from London on the 9th that the British naval budget for this fiscal year is more than 3 million British pounds higher than last year, totaling 53.57 million British pounds. Most of the increased funds are for normal construction costs, including four cruisers, one squadron flagship, eight destroyers, three submarines, and five small warships. These four cruisers are the last batch to be completed in 1936 in accordance with the compensatory procedures stipulated in the London Naval Treaty. The naval personnel will be reduced by more than a thousand people, but will still be around 90,000 people.

The Disarmament Conference Is Dying 56

Japan Drops a Huge Bomb 57

Openly Notifies Chairman Henderson

Changes Will Be Made to the National Defense Plan

The National News Agency reported from Geneva on the 8th that the disarmament conference, a ridiculous farce that is half-dead here, suffered another major fatal blow today, and the main culprit is Japan, which has not awakened from its militaristic dream. The Japanese delegation today openly notified Chairman Henderson that Japan feels compelled to expand its military equipment due to recent events in the Far East.

At the same time, the Japanese delegation also notified the League of Nations Secretariat that Japan and the League of Nations have different views on the Manchurian Incident. Japan fears that it will withdraw from the League of Nations, but Japan is still willing to cooperate with the Disarmament Conference, but Japan really needs to reorganize its army. After the announcement of this declaration, the League of Nations was as frightened as if struck by lightning. This move will also have a significant impact on the Anglo-French talks to be held in Paris tomorrow.

Havas reported from Geneva on the 8th that Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, recently received a declaration from the Japanese government, stating that with regard to the Far East issue, Japan's views are incompatible with those of the League of Nations, which has led Japan to order its representatives to withdraw from the League of Nations, which is deeply regrettable. As for the Disarmament Conference, Japan will continue to participate, but Japan's national defense must be fundamentally changed due to certain obvious circumstances. This should be considered by the Disarmament Conference.

MacDonald Goes to Paris: Britain and France First Make Behind-the-Scenes Contacts 58

Havas reported from London on the 9th that Prime Minister MacDonald, accompanied by his daughter Miss Hepburn, and Foreign Secretary Simon, took a train from Victoria Station to Paris at 11:00 AM. The Prime Minister met with French Ambassador Faroliio on the platform and declared, "We must seek a result at the Disarmament Conference. This result may not be entirely what we want, but it will definitely be helpful for world peace."

The National News Agency reported from Paris on the 8th that French Prime Minister Daladier and British Prime Minister MacDonald will meet here tomorrow. It is heard that French Foreign Minister Pong and British Foreign Secretary Simon will also participate in this matter, which is of great importance to the future of the Disarmament Conference and is the most important matter in political circles today. As for the newspapers, they are very uneasy and worried about the British proposal to indefinitely postpone the Disarmament Conference and conclude a preliminary treaty with the meager results that have already been achieved. Newspapers such as the Morning Post believe that the Anglo-French meeting will determine the fate of the Disarmament Conference, while the News newspaper advocates Anglo-French cooperation and hopes that the United States will also join the Anglo-French group.

Obstacles to Disarmament: Germany Insists on Equal Status 59

Reuter, Paris, 8th – Discussions between Britain and France regarding the difficult disarmament issue will commence this Friday. British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon will first have lunch with French Premier Daladier for a brief discussion before proceeding to Geneva. The French government has yet to express its attitude towards the British Prime Minister's proposal to halt the arms race for five years. The main obstacle in the disarmament process for France remains Germany's demand for immediate equality in armaments. However, France is likely to agree to a temporary convention, incorporating the points already agreed upon and acknowledging Germany's demand in principle. Judging from the general opinion in French circles, the British authorities may not receive a warm welcome, as public opinion believes that the disarmament conference is on its deathbed and Geneva can no longer achieve anything. *Le Liberté* claims that Germany, Italy, Austria, and Hungary all oppose France, and France should stay at home and guard its own web rather than go to Geneva to be caught in the spiderweb woven by Italy and Germany. *Le Débat* does not approve of the British proposal for a five-year arms truce, saying that it would only allow France and other peaceful nations to retreat, allowing the Hitler government to replenish its national defense forces and Italy to continue supplying Hungary with armaments.

National News Agency, Berlin, 8th – German newspapers, while not placing much emphasis on the Five-Power Conference and the preceding Anglo-French talks, still feel that France's attitude is too uncompromising and shows no willingness to concede on Germany's demand for unconditional equality of status. Therefore, the future of the Anglo-French conference is predicted to be without any achievements. Currently, both government and opposition parties unanimously state that Germany must refuse to sign any treaty that does not recognize this fundamental principle. *Lokalanzeiger* goes further, stating that if the disarmament conference fails and the powerful nations with sufficient armaments fail to fulfill their promise to reduce armaments, then Germany has ample reason to freely exercise its sovereign right to protect its national defense.

White House Drafts Emergency Plan to Resolve Financial Crisis 60

Submitted to Special Congressional Session Yesterday

Abandoning the Issuance of Scrip

Issuing New Currency to Aid the Currency Shortage

Fundamentally Reforming the Banking System

Reducing Government Spending to Balance the Budget

Reuter, Washington, 9th – President Roosevelt issued a statement regarding his consultation with congressional leaders, saying that he had discussed a carefully drafted plan that could save the situation and allow the nation's banking industry to resume operations. This legislation, once proposed, is assured of passage, and he is very pleased with the current situation.

Reuter, Washington, 9th – President Roosevelt, in consultation with congressional leaders at the White House last night, reportedly proposed a managed inflation plan to extend the payment moratorium until Congress enacts emergency legislation.

Reuter, New York, 9th – New York Governor Lehman announced today that the U.S. Treasury Department has rescinded the order to issue scrip.

National News Agency, Washington, 8th – After the U.S. Congress convenes in a special session tomorrow, the first step will be to establish a stable banking procedure to overcome this financial crisis. The second step will be to provide a more solid foundation for the entire banking structure. This was heard at President Roosevelt's meeting with congressional leaders tonight. Roosevelt's detailed plan has not yet been released. Only Democratic Senate Leader Robinson told reporters after the meeting that Congress would swiftly pass all emergency legislation without delay. According to information gathered from congressional leaders regarding the President's plan, it is expected that Roosevelt will ask Congress to temporarily grant him dictatorial powers to deal with the financial crisis, which may be even broader than the powers granted during wartime. He will also ask Congress to authorize the federal government to provide limited guarantees for bank deposits. The guaranteed amount will likely be equal to the percentage of withdrawals allowed to depositors by each bank before the President's moratorium announcement. It is said that this guarantee can reassure depositors and encourage them to return their hoarded money to the banks. In addition, it is expected that the President will ask Congress to authorize the continued embargo on currency exports, especially gold or gold certificates, until the President and the Treasury Department deem it safe to lift the embargo. After passing this emergency legislation, Congress will freely consider reforming the banking system. As for the best medium of exchange during this emergency period, the Treasury Department, on behalf of Congress, has decided to abandon the scrip clearinghouse plan and issue more banknotes.

National News Agency, Washington, 8th – Today, the U.S. government formally abandoned the use of scrip clearinghouse tickets or other money ticket plans and will use legal tender to deal with the current crisis. Treasury Secretary Woodin announced that the department is currently discussing detailed measures to issue more Federal Reserve banknotes, secured by gold and the liquid assets of member banks. He said, "We have now emerged from the clouds and see the light of day. The situation has largely stabilized and is no longer on the verge of collapse." However, Woodin did not mention when these additional banknotes could be issued, only saying that it would take several days to complete the government's plan to restore the banks to normalcy. He said that the events of the past forty-eight hours have proven that money tickets are not necessary to deal with the current situation and that existing currency can still be used to supply the banks. According to Treasury Department statistics, the elasticity of the Federal Reserve System has not reached its limit, and an additional 3 billion yuan of banknotes can still be issued without exceeding the legal ratio of gold reserves. The Treasury Department has instructed the Federal Reserve Banks to allow all 6,000 member banks to withdraw cash for wages and other regular business, provided that they submit all their gold certificates to the Federal Reserve Banks. The banking industry views this order as an indication that the government is determined to collect hoarded gold from the public on a large scale. In the past forty-eight hours, the Treasury Department has conducted a detailed investigation of the nation's financial reserves to determine where the currency shortage is most severe (i.e., lacking currency) so that it can be alleviated with the assistance of banks. It has also been found that the total amount of banknotes currently issued by the Federal Reserve Banks is far less than the allowable amount based on the legal cash reserve rate. The government can safely issue more banknotes without fear of danger, as Federal Reserve Bank notes are legally required to maintain only a 40% cash reserve, while the current cash reserve rate is 62%. On March 2nd, the total amount issued was 3,579,522,000 yuan, and the cash reserve was 2,268,462,000 yuan. Therefore, an additional 2 billion yuan can still be issued. In addition to the shortfall in issuance from the Federal Reserve Banks, there are other shortfalls that can be secured to provide sufficient currency to alleviate the current currency shortage.

Reuter, New York, 9th – This afternoon, Congress will hold a special session, and Roosevelt will present a straightforward and concise emergency legislative bill regarding the banking crisis. The gist of the bill is to use new currency to aid solvent banks while allowing insolvent banks to die of currency shortage. President Roosevelt will also propose actively reducing government spending to match revenue and put the government on a non-deficit footing. It is expected that Congress will pass a bill stipulating that banking for various commercial deposits is the responsibility of the federal government and that the government has the authority to charter and supervise banks. Judging from the current situation, Congress will definitely pass emergency procedures. It is believed that Congress's current actions are also closely related to future war debt negotiations. The attitude of Congress [Let Roosevelt do it] is encouraging. The printing bureau has been working day and night since Saturday to rush-print new banknotes in accordance with Roosevelt's currency expansion plan. These will be Federal Reserve banknotes, which are different from Federal Reserve notes that require a 40% cash reserve. According to Senator Glass, the new banknotes will have the same status as Treasury notes, backed by government bonds. Reuter, Washington, 8th – After consulting with representatives of grain exchanges in Chicago and other places, Bureau of Agricultural Economics Director Morganthau stated today that the meeting failed to agree on a method to reopen the grain exchanges. During the meeting, it was proposed that the Bureau of Agricultural Economics should release 30 million bushels of futures wheat to stabilize the operation of flour mills and the sale of flour, as flour mills are currently experiencing difficulties due to the lack of futures market hedging convenience. Morganthau also said that he believes a solution can be found in the future. Before the exchanges reopen, the Bureau of Agricultural Economics' 30,391,000 bushels of futures wheat cannot be sold in fact or in law. Today, efforts to reopen the grain exchanges before the banks resume operations have been abandoned, but meetings will still be held tomorrow to find an emergency solution to release the Bureau of Agricultural Economics' mostly May futures wheat so that flour mills can hedge their flour. It is reported that several flour mills have jointly purchased wheat stored by the Grain Stabilization Corporation from the Bureau of Agricultural Economics, totaling approximately 30 million bushels, but no official news about this matter has been heard yet.

=Currency Circulation Situation=

National News Agency, Washington, 8th – When the Federal Reserve Board submitted a report on the nation's financial reserves to the Treasury Department, it also included a report on the circulation of various currencies, including: (A) Gold certificates (i.e., gold notes), fully backed by gold coins stored in the Treasury; (B) Silver certificates (i.e., silver notes), fully backed by standard silver dollars stored in the Treasury; (C) United States Notes, backed by 156,039,088 yuan of gold stored in the Treasury; (D) Treasury notes of 1890, some backed by the aforementioned gold stored in the Treasury, and some backed by standard silver dollars stored in the Treasury. These Treasury notes will be recalled and cancelled after being collected and will no longer be circulated, but some still remain in circulation; (E) Federal Reserve Bank notes, for which the nation has an obligation to redeem, are preferentially guaranteed by all assets of the issuing Reserve Bank. Borrowers must deposit an equivalent amount of cash or a portion of securities of equivalent value with the Federal Reserve Bank, and the Federal Reserve Bank must maintain a gold reserve of at least 40%. The Treasury Department stores legal tender within the Treasury to redeem all of these banknotes; (F) National bank (large banks with operations nationwide) circulation notes, which are backed by government bonds unless legal tender is stored in the Treasury for redemption. However, 5% of the legal tender must still be stored in the Treasury. When borrowing Federal Reserve Bank notes, member banks must deposit all their gold certificates with the Federal Reserve Bank. In peacetime, all banknotes are indistinguishable and circulate equally. Since the emergency order prohibiting cash flow was announced, there is no issue with national banknotes. In addition, there is very little difference in the actual use of various banknotes. The Treasury Department only accepts gold coins for tariffs, which can usually be paid from ordinary bank deposits. It is not yet known how this will be handled in the future. It is expected that various customs offices will accept Federal Reserve Bank notes, and some believe that the government will follow the old rules and force the public to withdraw their hoarded gold coins or gold certificates.

Heavy Taxes on Hoarded Money 61

Reuter, New York, 9th – The Federal Reserve Bank of Richmond (Virginia) and other Federal Reserve Banks have been ordered by the Federal Reserve Board in Washington to report the names of those who withdrew cash after February 1st and failed to deposit it back by March 13th. It is expected that the authorities will force hoarders to redeposit their money in banks, otherwise they will be subject to heavy taxes and their names will be published.

Chronic Disease Becomes Acute Illness 62

9,000 U.S. Banks Closed in Three Years

The American financial panic is a chronic illness of the past three years. During this period, although there have been periods of temporary stability, the severity of the illness has only increased. In three years, as many as 5,096 banks have closed, with deposits exceeding 32,866,510,000 U.S. dollars, averaging 6.44 million U.S. dollars per bank. Details are as follows:

Year Number of Banks Monthly Average Total Deposits

Closed

1930 1,345 22 864,715 [thousands]

1931 2,298 192 1,691,510

1932 1,453 121 730,426

Total 5,096 3,286,651

From the above analysis, most of the closed banks are small banks, but the public has suffered losses of 320 billion yuan. Although not all deposits are lost due to closure, the public has felt very uneasy and has withdrawn their deposits, either hoarding them at home or transferring them to large banks or remitting them to foreign banks. Therefore, in December of last year, 153 banks closed, and in January of this year, the number exceeded 200. Moreover, it is widely rumored abroad that Roosevelt will adopt a gold ban policy after taking office, which has further prompted the public to transfer funds and deposit them in British and French banks. (United News Agency)

Rich Man Begs on the Street 68

Reuter, Marseille – A 60-year-old man here was arrested for repeatedly begging on the street. After a police investigation, it was found that the old man was not poor and owned a four-story building and many gumball machines in various hotels. During the interrogation, he said that although he was nominally a rich man, he was actually very distressed because the tenants owed him a lot of rent, while the property tax could not be delayed. Therefore, for the sake of paying taxes, he had no choice but to beg. After the trial, the judge sentenced the old man to eight months in prison and said, "You can have no worries for these eight months." The old man replied, "No, no, my tenants will take the opportunity to not pay rent for eight months."

The Strategic Significance of the Japanese Navy's Grand Maneuvers in the Eyes of the Japanese (By Masanori Ito) 69

One: The Origin of the Grand Maneuvers

The atmospheric pressure on both sides of the Pacific Ocean has deviated from the norm. Although it has not yet reached the level of a "storm," a strong wind continues to stir the emotions of the people on both shores. At this very moment, the US Navy's grand maneuvers have begun. Is this preparation for war against Japan? Most people harbor such doubts and feel a sense of agitation toward the Atlantic fleet stationed in the Pacific. On the other hand, Japan's naval grand maneuvers this year have also expanded in scope. This news of expansion has been interpreted as preparation for war against the League of Nations and a demonstration against the United States, causing agitation among people on the other shore.

Formally, both sides are suspicious of each other because the confrontation of the maneuvers is a fact. And this fact is the object of doubt. Originally, it is appropriate for fleets to come together through maneuvers. To suspect each other because of this is rather absurd. Coming together symbolizes peace, while suspicion is the seed of preparation for war. Although humanity loves peace, the current situation seems to be unconsciously tilting toward war preparations. This is a reality in the relationship between Japan and the United States. The following is a reflection of the international political situation, such as the United States' suspicion that Japan intended to occupy China during the Manchurian and Shanghai incidents. Stimson's diplomacy was based on this suspicion. As a result, Japan also deeply suspected that the United States was preparing for war against Japan. International discourse also became tense. And the suspicion of the United States deepened even further. This reciprocal suspicion is the reality on both sides of the Pacific. Just as this unconscious atmosphere had calmed down, the grand maneuvers of Japan and the United States were held one after the other. This naturally added fuel to the fire of suspicion before the ashes had even cooled. Ultimately, is the US Navy's exercise worthy of vigilance? Is Japan's naval exercise worthy of suspicion?

Two: Strategy and Tactics

Ignorance often leads to misunderstanding, and misunderstanding often leads to war. Unconscious judgment of international affairs or half-understood commentary on such matters often contain dangerous elements. Misunderstandings between the people of both countries regarding the naval relationship between Japan and the United States will at least lead to danger in the fact of the arms race.

If the purpose of the US maneuvers is clearly preparation for war against Japan, then we must certainly make thorough preparations. If Japan's maneuvers are truly a hypothetical battle against... then the suspicions of the United States are naturally not unreasonable. If Japan's maneuvers are held because it is planning to withdraw from the League of Nations, planning to refuse to return..., and planning to fight alone when allied forces use force to seize it, then the suspicion has some reason. However, Japanese naval commanders, in fact, are not currently thinking of going to war with the world. Therefore, there are no such maneuvers as mentioned above at present. However, should our perspective on the US naval maneuvers be sharp or dull? Naturally, neither a sharp nor a dull one-sided observation will reveal its truth. Therefore, here, the author first offers two concepts:

(1) The political significance of the US Navy's grand maneuvers. (2) Its tactical significance.

The above two points are derived from observing the horizontal plane. If we look further, we can also derive two concepts:

Page 8

(A) A test of the existing power of the US Navy maneuvers and a strategic indication.

(B) Demands for the future.

Three: The Grand Maneuvers

The duration of this exercise is approximately seventy days, from January 23, when the scouting force/Atlantic Fleet (Scouting Force, US Fleet) departed from San Pedro, California, to March 31, the day the US Fleet's entire combined tactical exercise concludes. However, the scouting force and the battle force (Battle Force) had already begun preparations at their bases on January 1. Therefore, starting from January 1, it can also be said to be ninety days. Participants are almost all of the US Navy. The exercise is divided into three phases:

Exercise Objective Period Participating Forces

Phase 1: Hawaii Attack and Defense Exercise (Joint Exercise) From January 23 to February 5 Attacking: Scouting Force, Defending: Hawaii Land and Sea Forces

Phase 2: Occupation of Base Exercise (Fleet Problem) From February 6 to February 17 Attacking: Scouting Force, Defending: Battle Force

Phase 3: Combined Training of the Grand Fleet (Fleet Concentration) From February 18 to March 31 Entire US Fleet

From the above table, the battlefields for attack and defense in the exercises are all islands and bases. Compared with ordinary exercises that focus solely on naval gunfire and torpedo tactics on the sea surface, this is not only more diverse in style but also very interesting. This will be described in detail below. This type of exercise has extremely important tactical significance for the air force. Not only naval authorities of various countries around the world but also people who care about the navy should pay serious attention.

What kind of tactical lessons will be learned from this? We can see its record in April. However, some of the more interesting tactics can be guessed at now. For example, the commonly reported use of "colored water columns" from the main guns to test the mutual distance of various ships, which can be considered an interesting thing in the third phase of the exercise. In addition, new tactics such as firing "long-range illuminating shells" during night battles to observe enemy ships and shield oneself while attacking the enemy are also interesting. And the battle for the attack and defense of Hawaii is a reflection and realistic portrayal of the Shanghai battle, making it even more interesting. The above points will be discussed in the following. Now, let's first study the so-called political and strategic significances.

Four: Testing Offensive and Defensive Capabilities

The first question that people generally have about this exercise is whether it is offensive or defensive. What I call "political significance" mainly refers to this point. The so-called political significance refers to strategy. The strategy of peacetime exercises can greatly reflect political or diplomatic actions. Because strategy is an integral part of national policy. Policy going left and strategy going right is not only theoretically unacceptable but also clumsy and useless in practice. Therefore, the direction of policy and the trend of diplomacy can be tested to a certain extent from the methods adopted in the naval grand maneuvers.

Of course, the goal of the exercise is indefinite, and it is not possible to conduct hypothetical battles with the same force on the same sea surface every year. Although the battle tactics are only slightly different, the strategic background is definitely not the same. Assuming that the strategy is changed every year, it is something that should naturally be done in exercises. The impact on the assumed enemy country is also definitely not the same. In other words, a subjective, unintentional strategy can be objectively recognized as an intentional strategic goal.

However, this subtle psychology, because of the different background of the times, is sometimes激昂, but sometimes it will also be calm. Therefore, the observation of the offensive and defensive issue of the purpose of the exercise and the judgment of the trend of national policy naturally shift according to the development of the situation. Therefore, after Stimson revised his diplomatic policy, the relationship between Japan and the United States gradually eased. Compared with this time last year, the degree of cold and heat is no longer the same. The feelings of the people have also relaxed a lot. However, the clouds of suspicion are still shrouding the area. It has not yet reached the point of clearing up after the rain. The increasing number of people who want to hear a detailed discussion of the US grand maneuvers proves that people's hearts are still floating.

In fact, as in the previous exercise around Panama, taking Japan as a hypothetical enemy country and assuming that the canal was bombed by the Japanese air force, so that the US main fleet and cruiser fleet could not take care of each other and were trapped in an isolated and helpless state, they did feel this kind of exercise was interesting. But Japan had to pay attention to this exercise to speculate on the urgency of the situation.

Five: Speculation on the Defensive

First, let's calmly observe this exercise. We seem to feel that the US exercise is defensive. First, assuming that Hawaii has been occupied by the enemy, the US Navy starts its offensive from Hawaii. How passively does this kind of strategy indicate? Second, the warships that counterattack Hawaii do not use the main fleet but the cruiser fleet. Compared with previous exercises, this is also a passive indication. Third, the second phase of the exercise is exclusively aimed at defending the country's base. This is a manifestation of defensiveness. Fourth, the defense force of the base is the main battleship fleet, which is an even more obvious manifestation of "defensiveness."

Originally, attack and defense are like two sides of a shield, which cannot be separated. One must attack to defend, and one must defend to attack. Therefore, the two words attack and defense, apart from being distinguishable in concept, cannot be separated strategically. The famous general Mahan once said that even if a strategy is defensive, the fleet must always take the offensive.

If these two sentences are observed from within, then sometimes the fleet takes offensive operations, but the strategy is defensive. However, the exercise is a peacetime strategy and a peacetime tactic. If we look at the purpose of the exercise as described above, then we might as well say that the US peacetime outlook and tactics are defensive. This strategy is contrary to the traditional policy of the United States, that is, avoiding stimulating expressions in the relationship between Japan and the United States and considering it from a far-reaching conscious perspective. We know that the US military is intensifying the practice of free attacks, but this kind of guerrilla-style free attack is more than enough to guard against the enemy, but it is insufficient for formal combat.

The author has good feelings about the US naval maneuvers. Apart from Secretary of State Stimson, the author also respects Admiral Pratt. I respect his wisdom and brilliance. If it is a fact that Stimson wanted to start a war with Japan, then Pratt's prevention was an even greater fact. The scale of the 1932 grand maneuvers was all a realistic portrayal of Admiral Pratt's concept.

Six: The Naval Balance between Japan and the United States

Stimson initially understood Japan a little, but after the Jinzhou incident, he changed his mentality, and his anti-Japanese feelings deepened. Finally, he raised the "question of whether it is possible to wage war against Japan" and immediately answered "no." This was Admiral Pratt.

Regarding the so-called judgment of the situation—a strategic element that the US Navy has recently attached great importance to, Estimation of Situation—Pratt has surpassed American politicians. The admiral once said that whether strategically or in terms of military strength, naval battles between Japan and the United States are unfavorable, at least useless. Now, he wants to avoid war as much as possible and discover the value of the navy outside of war.

The scale and purpose of this exercise are almost the same as described above. The deployment and selection of offensive and defensive forces everywhere make it clear at a glance that it comes from a "defensive" perspective. Some people may doubt that this is a smokescreen to appease Japan. Those who doubt can continue to doubt. The author believes in it extremely. There is only one thing we must know. The Japanese Navy is able to exist because it possesses its current strength. If the Japanese Navy's strength were half of what it is now, perhaps the war between Japan and the United States would have started long ago. And Japan's Far East policy might be subject to restraint and suppression. Japan might have surrendered long before the war started.

Americans will naturally not shed blood for the Far East issue, but if Admiral Pratt answered Stimson's question with "victory is possible" (the ratio of strength between Japan and the United States is four to ten), then the fact would be either a war between Japan and the United States or Japan's surrender.

The current power of the United States is more than enough to defend its own country, but not enough to attack Japan. The current strength of the Japanese Navy is sufficient to resist the attack of any country. In other words, in terms of the position of the United States attacking and Japan defending, the naval forces of Japan and the United States are evenly matched. They cannot invade each other. The essence and value of armaments are all here.

If Japan did not have this kind of strength, it would naturally be difficult to recognize Manchuria and to claim to be the master of upholding peace in the Far East. Because it has this kind of power, it maintains the peace between Japan and the United States. Soldiers may be willing to fight, but our people have already recognized the value of the navy winning without fighting. The US exercise is also recognized as defensive, and the atmospheric pressure in diplomatic relations has gradually calmed down.

(To be continued)

Hunan Raises National Salvation Loan 70

Five million yuan to be raised according to property grade

To be used for relief from national crisis and to maintain provincial defense costs

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan's Party, Government, Military, and Civilian Jointly Organized National Salvation and Communist Suppression General Mobilization Propaganda Week was held on the 6th. Leaders of the Party, Government, Military, and Civilians also held a joint meeting at the headquarters of the 4th Route Army at 2 PM on the afternoon of the 6th and resolved to adopt (1) the Regulations for Raising the Hunan National Salvation Loan, (2) the Regulations for the Hunan National Salvation Loan Supervision Committee, and (3) the Methods for National Salvation Donations. These were sent to the Provincial Government for approval at the 350th Provincial Affairs Meeting on the 7th and will be promulgated and implemented immediately. The regulations and methods are as follows:

Article 1 of the Regulations for Raising the National Salvation Loan states that the Hunan National Salvation Loan is specifically for relieving the national crisis and maintaining the province's defense expenditures. It is to be raised upon resolution by the joint meeting of the province's Party, Government, and Military. Article 2: The fixed amount of the loan is five million yuan, with an annual interest rate of four percent. The land tax of the entire province of Hunan will be used as the repayment fund. The Provincial Government will first issue bonds, and the repayment period will be from the Republic of China year 24, with principal and interest to be repaid in installments over 20 years. The custody and repayment methods of the fund will be determined separately. Article 3: The face value of the loan bonds will be divided into six denominations: five yuan, ten yuan, fifty yuan, one hundred yuan, five hundred yuan, and one thousand yuan. They will be allowed to be used as guarantees and deposits in administrative, judicial, and various business matters. Article 4: The raising of the loan and the issuance of the bonds will be handled by the Hunan Finance Committee. The methods will be determined by the Committee and submitted to the Provincial Government for record. Article 5: The National Salvation Loan will be subscribed to by all sectors of society in the province. The amount of subscription will be based on the grade of property, as shown in the attached table:

Property Grade Property Value Subscription Amount for National Salvation Loan

Grade A: 300,000 yuan or more: Subscribe at 5% starting from 15,000 yuan

Grade B: 200,000 yuan or more: Subscribe at 4% starting from 8,000 yuan

Grade C: 100,000 yuan or more: Subscribe at 3% starting from 3,000 yuan

Grade D: 50,000 yuan or more: Subscribe at 2.5% starting from 1,250 yuan

Grade E: 20,000 yuan or more: Subscribe at 2% starting from 400 yuan

Grade F: 10,000 yuan or more: Subscribe at 1.5% starting from 150 yuan

Grade G: 5,000 yuan or more: Subscribe at 1% starting from 50 yuan

Grade H: 2,000 yuan or more: Subscribe at 0.5% starting from 10 yuan

(Explanation): The calculation of the property value in the table: movable property is based on the actual surveyed amount, and immovable property is based on the local market value or income. If it is more than 300,000 yuan, it is estimated in increments of 100,000 yuan, but it must not exceed 10%. Article 6: In addition to the provisions of the preceding article, if there are enthusiastic subscribers, they may subscribe freely and submit the amount to the local fundraising agency for verification and receipt. Article 7: The amount of the loan to be subscribed by each county shall be determined by the Finance Committee, which shall instruct the county magistrate and the director of the Provincial Tax Collection Bureau to organize a fundraising committee to handle it. Article 8: If the loan subscriber resides outside the province but has property in various counties of the province, or resides in various counties of the province but has property outside the province, or resides in County A but has property in County B, they shall all subscribe to the loan uniformly. Article 9: If a loan subscriber moves and avoids subscription, the resident neighborhood shall be responsible for investigating the actual amount of all property, and the county magistrate shall strictly order them to pay. Article 10: After receiving the notice of the fixed subscription amount verified by the county bureau, the loan subscriber must pay the full amount of the subscription within ten days. If the payment is delayed beyond the deadline, the county bureau may send personnel to urge payment. If they refuse to comply, the county magistrate may order them to pay. Article 11: The loan business of each county shall be completed within three months from the date of the order. Article 12: If the personnel handling the loan business demand or embezzle funds, they will be dealt with by military law once the evidence is verified. Article 13: The raised loan shall be kept by the Hunan National Salvation Loan Supervision Committee, which shall supervise its use. The regulations of the Supervision Committee shall be determined separately. Article 14: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time by the joint meeting of the Party, Government, and Military. Article 15: These regulations shall be resolved by the joint meeting of the Party, Government, and Military and submitted to the Hunan Provincial Government for promulgation and implementation.

Article 1 of the Regulations of the National Salvation Loan Supervision Committee states that these regulations are formulated in accordance with Article 13 of the Regulations for Raising the Hunan National Salvation Loan. Article 2: The Hunan National Salvation Loan shall be kept by this committee, which shall supervise its use. The supervision methods shall be determined by this committee. Article 3: This committee shall be composed of the following personnel, determined by the joint meeting of the Party, Government, and Military. All are unpaid positions: 1. Two members of the Provincial Party Committee; 2. Two members of the Provincial Government; 3. One person from the Headquarters of the Fourth Route Army; 4. One member of the Audit Committee; 5. Nine impartial people from the province. Article 4: This committee shall have five standing committee members, who shall be elected by all the committee members. Article 5: This committee shall have several staff members, handling matters, and secretaries, who may be transferred from various agencies to handle the affairs of the committee under the command of the standing committee members. Article 6: The supervisory committee members may inspect the amount of the loan raised and the issuance of the bonds at any time and may also inspect all books and records. Article 7: The National Salvation Loan shall not be used for any purpose other than relieving the national crisis and maintaining the province's defense unless signed by a majority of the standing committee members of this committee. Article 8: This committee shall meet once a week. The detailed rules of procedure shall be determined separately. Article 9: The expenses of this committee shall be resolved and paid by the Hunan Finance Committee. Article 10: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time by the joint meeting of the Party, Government, and Military. Article 11: These regulations shall be resolved by the joint meeting of the Party, Government, and Military and submitted to the Provincial Government for promulgation and implementation.

Methods for National Salvation Donations: (1) Elementary school students: donate or raise 10 cents per person; (2) Middle school students: donate 50 cents per person; (3) University and vocational students: donate 1 yuan per person; (4) Workers in all provincial groups and public and private businesses: donate 10 cents per person; (5) People with salaries in the province: those with a monthly salary between 12 yuan and 20 yuan donate 50 cents per person, and those with more than 20 yuan donate 1 yuan; (6) Public officials and teachers in the province (including provincial and county expenditures) shall donate according to the central government's standards; (7) People in the province are free to donate more; (8) These methods were resolved by the joint meeting of the Party, Government, and Military. All other donations related to the national salvation movement are stopped. (March 7)

Imperial Tang Emperor Ming's Mountain Sacrifice Jade Tablets 72

Discovered at the Foot of Mount Tai

An Unprecedented and Unique Treasure

Tai'an Dispatch: Mount Tai in Tai'an, Shandong, is the most revered of the Five Sacred Mountains. Emperors of all dynasties performed Feng and Shan sacrifices there. All the gold, stone, and ritual implements used are of great significance to Chinese history and culture. However, after use, they were often carefully and secretly stored to show respect for Mount Tai. Since the Tang Dynasty, no such sacrificial items have been discovered. Recently, it was rumored that Jade Tablets with sacrificial text and other jade objects used by Emperor Ming of the Tang Dynasty during his Feng sacrifice at Mount Tai were discovered in Tai'an. It is said that when the discovery was made, Tai'an was garrisoned by a certain army, so everything was taken by that army. Later, when that army withdrew from Shandong, the treasures were also transported to Beiping (Beijing). A special investigation into the situation is detailed below:

Location of the Treasure: At the foot of Mount Tai, north of Tai'an Railway Station on the Jinpu Railway, there is a small mountain called Songli Mountain. On the mountain, there is a Temple of the King of Hell (阎王庙), and in front of the temple, there is a pagoda. The construction date of the pagoda cannot be determined, but it is known to be from the Tang Dynasty. During the Northern Expedition of the Revolutionary Army in the 17th year of the Republic (1928), both the temple and the pagoda on the mountain were destroyed by artillery fire. When a certain army garrisoned Tai'an, they sent soldiers to clear away the remaining bricks and tiles on the mountain and build a memorial碑 on the original site of the pagoda. It now stands tall and majestic. Passengers traveling on the Jinpu Railway can see it from a dozen miles away. Unsuspecting observers would never imagine that precious treasures were discovered beneath this pagoda.

Discovery Process: When the army was clearing the pagoda, intending to rebuild the memorial碑, they first dug up the remaining bricks of the pagoda's foundation. Unexpectedly, under the base of the pagoda, they discovered five-color earth, similar to the form of the Temple of Heaven (天地坛) in Beiping. The soil was in the shape of a square, with red, white, blue, and black colors on the four sides and yellow in the center (as shown in the diagram).

White Digging soldiers, seeing that the soil

Red Yellow Black was of a special nature, immediately reported it to their

Blue highest officer. Upon hearing the report, the officer knew that there must be treasures buried beneath. He ordered further excavation, with soldiers rotated daily to prevent the news from leaking out. During the excavation within the red, white, blue, and black soils, a large number of jade objects were unearthed. Upon examination of the inscriptions, all were sacrificial items used by Emperor Ming (Xuanzong) of the Tang Dynasty during the Feng sacrifice at Mount Tai.

Exquisite Jade Tablets: Later, within the yellow soil, a stone box, five feet square, was unearthed. The carvings on the outside of the box were extremely intricate. Upon opening the stone box, another gold box was found inside. The floral engravings on the gold box were even more mysterious and beyond description with words. Inside the gold box, there were fifteen white jade plates, arranged side by side. Each plate was about one foot long and two inches wide, connected by gold threads. Each plate was engraved with the script form of the Tang Emperor Ming's inscription placed at Mount Tai. By reading the text on the fifteen plates together, it was discovered to be the sacrificial text of Emperor Ming of the Tang Dynasty's Feng sacrifice at Mount Tai. The words and phrases of the sacrificial text were particularly exquisite. Thus, it was proven to be the sacrificial items buried after the Feng sacrifice of Emperor Ming of the Tang Dynasty. The army commander ordered strict secrecy, collected and stored the items. Now that the army has withdrawn from Shandong for a long time, these antiques have long been transported to Beiping. Some of the soldiers who dug the earth at that time did not leave with the army, and recently, when they talked about this matter, the outside world learned the details.

(Value of the Antiquities): According to archaeologists in Tai'an, this ancient artifact is an unprecedented discovery. The plates inside the gold box on which the sacrificial text is engraved are the ancient jade tablets. Although the existence of jade tablets has been known in modern times, no one has ever seen them. Its importance lies in that, on one hand, it can be used to study the ancient Feng and Shan sacrificial rituals at Mount Tai, and on the other hand, it can reveal the form of ancient writing slips. It is extremely related to Chinese history and culture, and its value is far beyond any ancient artifact discovered in the past. (March 7th)

The county borders Guilin on three sides, and the Yao people are numerous and have little knowledge, making them easily incited. Recently, rumors have been circulating daily. In Yongming, the rumor is that the Yao bandits of Guanyang will arrive in Yongming soon. In Guanyang, the rumor is that there are two or three thousand Yao bandits in Yongming who will attack Guanyang soon. In addition to ordering the teams to defend key areas and instructing the local militia in the border areas to inform the Yao people not to believe the rumors and to investigate and guard against them at any time, we should earnestly request the dispatch of troops to the county to assist in defense and suppression, and await further instructions. County Magistrate Huang Kunshan, Republican Commander, heard that there are over two thousand Yao bandits in Yongming County, and they threaten to disrupt Daoxian and Guanyang County. Please clarify the actual situation and respond accordingly. We have already telegraphed the County Magistrate of Yongming and requested the local security to send officers for close investigation and teams for suppression. Now, we enclose the copies of reports from all parties as follows: (1) The Yao bandits in Guanyang, Xing'an and Quanan counties have agreed to rise up, incited by communists who are trying to communize the Yao people. (2) There are many Yao bandits in Xing'an, but few have guns, most wielding knives and clubs. They have already engaged with the local militia. The bandits are organized into teams of ten or more, brandishing knives and spears, charging one after another. Improving Security Corps Organization and Training in Jiangsu Province 73

First-class counties must draw up at least three companies of security forces. Zhenjiang Dispatch: The Jiangsu Provincial Government's 567th Commission meeting passed the following measures to improve the organization and training of the province's security corps: (1) Establish a Houserolder (户长) under the current existing Qu (區), Tuan (圑), Jia (甲) and Pai (牌) levels of the security corps. (2) If the county has completed its autonomy and the Qu, Xiang (鄉), Zhen (鎮) and Lu (閭) can be responsible, the heads of Qu, Tuan, Jia and Pai should also serve concurrently. Otherwise, they should be elected in order, but this is not limited to those with military knowledge. (3) The responsibilities of the Qu, Xiang, Zhen, Lu and the Qu, Jia and Pai should be clearly divided. All matters that should be handled by the autonomous organs but are the responsibility of the Baojia (保甲) should be handled by the Security Corps. The original tasks of the Security Corps remain unchanged. (4) The mutual security pledge should be based on the Lu unit. The old mutual security pledge for each household of the same Jia is abolished. (5) Universal training should be based on the Jia unit and held once a year during the agricultural slack season. The training period is limited to three months. (6) Centralized training: The head of the General Corps should draw up strong men from each Jia to be trained in the county for six months. After their discharge, they will be responsible for the universal training of their original Jia. (7) Strong men registered in the registers should be called Strong Men's Teams (壯丁隊), strong men in the universal training should be called Regular Teams (常備隊), and strong men in the centralized training should be called Security Teams (保衛隊). (8) First-class counties must draw up at least three companies of security forces every six months, second-class counties two companies, and third-class counties one company. Each company should have ninety soldiers. (9) The funds required for universal training and centralized training should be budgeted by each county and submitted to the province for approval. (March 9th)

Songjiang

Fierce Battle Between Police and Bandits in Jiaodiaowan

Jiaodiaowan Township in the county has many rivers and harbors, making it an area where bandits frequent. The night before last, a bandit boat was discovered there, sailing from the west. It contained three bandits, each carrying a Mauser pistol. It was rumored that there was also a hostage on board. Fan Shaolin, an investigator from the Second Squad of the First District of the Provincial Public Security Team stationed there, spotted the boat and led the police to pursue it. When they reached the Yang Bridge at number thirty-eight, the bandit boat opened fire to resist arrest. Outnumbered, the bandits quickly sailed away. The police boat was unable to pursue due to the darkness and returned empty-handed.

Suzhou

Accomplices of Taibao Ashu Arrested

Qi Xingxiong, Qi Xingyou, Wu Shaoquan, accomplices of Taibao Ashu, the leader of the Pudong gang, as well as suspects Yang Jinsong, Wang Awu, Sun Aliu, Yang Shoumei, etc., were recently arrested by Xu Pucheng, the district chief of the First District of the Water Police, at Hujiaqiao in Songjiang. They were escorted to Suzhou on the 8th and handed over to the Suzhou-Songjiang Bandit Suppression Command for interrogation. That evening, they were interrogated by the Inspector General. According to Qi Xingxiong's confession, when Taibao Ashu started his gang in Hujiaqiao, I, along with my brothers Qi Xingyou, Arong, and Achang, joined the gang. Later, when Taibao Ashu was executed, the gang disbanded. On December 22nd of last year, Arong led Qi Ayou, Afu Lin, Wu Shaoquan, Hobbling Azhao, Pockmarked Afu, etc., to rob the families of Lu and Lu Xunyan in Changbang Village, Songjiang, and kidnapped two men. When the boat arrived at the temple, the hostage was taken away by Little Arong, and later the hostage was released. They stole 300 yuan in silver, which was used for food. Each of the brothers received five yuan, etc. After interrogating Ma Xingyou and Wu Shaoquan once, they were ordered to be returned to custody pending verification. However, Yang Jinsong, etc., denied communicating with the bandits.

Tomb-Sweeping Boat Robbed in Shihu

The Zhu family, residing in Hulongdai, hired a boat to go to Zhangjiaqiao in Suzhou County to sweep tombs on the morning of the 9th. Unexpectedly, when the boat passed near Shihu, it was suddenly encountered by a bandit boat with four bandits who boarded the boat and robbed them. They were robbed of jewelry and clothing worth about 200 yuan. Also, the Wang Zhaofu family in Fengjiaqiao, Hengtang, was robbed by bandits on the morning of the 8th, losing clothing and silver worth about 100 yuan.

Telephone Bureau Expands Numbers and Consolidates Deposits

Since Director Deng Sixiao took office at the Suzhou Telephone Bureau, the total number of switchboard numbers has been full and materials are lacking, so registered users have not been able to add installations. To increase the expansion, there are economic difficulties. It has been found that users who install telephones should pay a deposit fee. Most have not paid enough according to regulations, and some have not paid at all. In order to ensure uniformity, a consolidation method has been drafted and the funds collected will be used for expansion projects. An order was submitted to the ministry for approval, and the ministry approved an order for the Wu County Chamber of Commerce to assist in order to facilitate the process. The county chamber of commerce, due to the decline of the market and the exhaustion of the economy, requested a delay. The original approval of the Ministry of Transportation is recorded below. It is noted that the increase in telephone rent in the 19th year (1930) was based on precise statistics by the ministry. After the full amount of salary increases for employees, the monthly rent for Suzhou telephones should have increased by an average of two yuan and eight jiao to meet the business principles. The determined increase of two yuan was originally intended to maintain the telephone business while also considering the difficulties of merchants. A notice was issued to the former Suzhou General Chamber of Commerce in Order No. 1016 of the 19th year. Later, due to the Chamber's repeated requests, the increase of two yuan was temporarily reduced by half, and Directive No. 453 of the 19th year ordered that it should be temporarily paid as such. Once the merchants' difficulties eased slightly, it should still be increased accordingly. The former General Chamber of Commerce requested that the funds from the rent increase be retained by former Director Zhao for expansion projects. Although former Director Zhao forwarded the request to the Ministry, the Ministry did not approve it because the ministry was not familiar with the status of the telephone. However, the former approval states that even if the Chamber of Commerce was notified by former Director Zhao, there is no need to follow this case because when the charter is created, the charter is terminated. Furthermore, according to the bureau's report, after the notice to collect deposits was sent out this time, many have come to the bureau to pay them. It would not be fair if for the same users in the city, the deposits collected have different weights and measures. In summary, the reason for collecting deposits this time is that the bureau's numbers are full and the telephone funds are extremely stretched. For the local population and for the important consideration of raising funds for the expansion project, it is necessary to implement the revised charter and use all the funds collected by the bureau. The funds have been ordered to be deposited in the Bank of China and a special account has been established for expansion needs. The ministry is cautious in this regard. It wants to provide convenience to the citizens of Suzhou and does not want to increase the burden on the citizens of Suzhou. Therefore, it does not collect the full two yuan increase as originally planned but only orders the deposit charter to be paid in full, so that they can be returned in full when the time comes. It is considerate of the merchants' difficulties. Furthermore, the name of the deposit has been changed to Deposit Fee according to the new charter revised in January of this year. It includes a deposit for the machine and a guarantee of rent, which is broader than the former term of Deposit only. Therefore, the addition of the deposit is of course reasonable. The previous instructions to notify the merchants to pay according to the charter shall still be followed. The previous statement to delay is difficult to approve. This batch.

Wuxi

Suspicious White Russian Actions Are Treacherous

At five o'clock in the afternoon the day before yesterday, six White Russians suddenly arrived at the railway station in this county. They were wearing crisp suits, one wearing a raincoat, and no other belongings. Two of them spoke fluent mandarin. After getting off the train, they went to the Xicheng Long-Distance Bus Company to inquire about the situation in Jiangyin. They then bought tickets and took a bus to Cheng. After arriving in Cheng, the Cheng authorities, considering the current serious situation and the tight defense of the Yangtze River, suspected that the White Russian's actions were treacherous and placed them under surveillance. Yesterday morning, they were escorted back to Xi and interrogated severely by Zhu Shou, the chief of the Sixth Branch of the County Public Security Bureau. The White Russians claimed to be a song and dance troupe. A Republic of China passport issued by the Shanghai Municipal Government in the 20th year (1931) was found on them, but it did not have the words for traveling to various ports in the interior. Later, Chief Zhu sent police officers and Qian, an official from the County Party Headquarters, to escort them onto the train and expel them from Xi.

Actively Promoting the New Weights and Measures

The county government of this county has ordered inspectors to actively promote the new weights and measures system. They will persuade various industries to use new equipment to avoid chaos in the market and to achieve uniformity. However, due to the lack of procedures, the various industries have not yet adopted it uniformly. The industries that have already switched to the new system are tea, tea leaves, oil mills, oil merchants, paint industry, coal, coal and iron, silk cloth, ready-made clothing, dried goods, lime merchants, candles, noodle restaurants, cloth factories, and vegetable markets. On the surface, the industries have been ordered to switch to the new system, but they are secretly using the old equipment. Inspectors Tang Fuqian and He Heming, in accordance with the inspection rules, led police officers to conduct inspections in various districts starting at 9:00 a.m. yesterday (the 9th). If old equipment is found, it will be confiscated. Inspections will continue daily without interruption. As for the food industry, after persuasion, they obeyed the order to switch to the new system. However, due to the new equipment not yet being manufactured and the need to wait for the implementation of rice and grain, the industry has finished manufacturing the Sheng and Dou measures and sent them to the county government for inspection. It has been decided that they will start using them on the 20th of this month. The industry association will notify the members to collect them. The mountain goods industry specially convened a meeting of urban and rural members the day before yesterday to discuss the implementation method. It was decided that the retail and wholesale scales should be switched to the new system within the shortest possible time. As for the Sheng and Dou measures used by the warehouses in the urban area and various towns and villages to collect rent rice, they should purchase new equipment from the grain industry association to avoid fraud.

Local News

Implementation of Silver Dollar Standard Begins Today 74

Money Dealers Announce Resolutions to Members

Foreign Exchange to be Calculated in Silver Dollars

Silver-Taels Exchange to Open for Business

The Ministry of Finance has decided to implement the silver dollar standard from today. Transactions in all industries will be calculated in silver dollars, with a fixed rate of seven qian, one fen and five li as the legal price. The money industry held an extraordinary meeting the day before yesterday to discuss the measures. Foreign exchange transactions in the banking industry will be calculated in silver dollars. The exchange mechanism jointly established by the Central Bank and two other banks will start business at 9:00 a.m. today. Details are as follows:

(Money Dealers' Announcement)

The Money Dealers' Association notified its members yesterday, stating, "To: All Members, This is to inform you that on the 8th of this month, an extraordinary meeting of members' representatives was held to discuss matters starting from March 10th. The following resolutions were passed by all members: (A) Regarding domestic matters: (1) The morning and afternoon markets will be held as usual. (2) The Li rate will be set at the legal price of seven qian, one fen and five li. (3) Silver discounts should be changed to discount interest. Silver and dollars will be settled with interest by transfer. (4) Bank silver dollar transfers will be calculated in fen and jiao. (5) The silver and dollar balances of all members must be settled in cash every night, except for those who wish to discount or borrow. (6) If there is a surplus of silver dollars on the day and the demand cannot be balanced, the reserve will temporarily buy and sell them, but they must be settled in cash that night. The sealed boxes of silver dollars must be sealed as usual, no later than 12:00 midnight. (B) Regarding foreign matters: (1) All bills from local industries and banks, as well as foreign banks, will be handled in the same way as silver bills. (2) Foreign banks will be charged a handling fee of one jiao per thousand yuan for banknotes or silver dollars. (3) Existing bill discounts for all correspondents will continue to be handled as before. The above items have been resolved and recorded. Please comply accordingly."

(Banking Reform Measures)

Those in the banking industry who manage foreign exchange,

such as US dollars, francs, yen, Hong Kong dollars, rupees, new dollars, marks, Dutch guilders, pounds, etc., which were originally calculated in silver taels, have decided to convert to silver dollars at the fixed rate of seven qian, one fen and five li from today. The exchange rate committee organized by the Banking Association will stop sending telegrams reporting the foreign exchange rates and exchange rates in various places from today. The method will be determined based on local market needs, as exchange rates fluctuate. However, the Central Bank's foreign exchange has already been converted to silver dollars.

(Silver-Taels Exchange Opens)

The Shanghai Silver Dollar and Silver Taels Exchange Management Committee, jointly established by the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, has been designated by the three banks to be composed of Tang Min, Li Jue, and Xi Demao from the Central Bank; Bei Songsun and Shi Jiu from the Bank of China; and Qin Zuze and Chen Jun from the Bank of Communications. The organizational outline has been promulgated by the Ministry of Finance, and the detailed rules of procedure have been discussed and approved. It will start business today. The exchange office is located in the Cashier Section of the Business Bureau on the first floor of the Central Bank. The office is located on the third floor of the Central Bank. Yang Xiaobo, the deputy director of the Issuance Bureau of the Central Bank, will serve concurrently as the secretary, and four clerks will be assigned to the exchange duties. All who wish to exchange silver taels for silver dollars or silver dollars for silver taels must fill out a request form. After the approval notice is issued, they can exchange at the designated bank. Office hours are from 9:00 a.m. to 5:00 p.m. However, the request form must be submitted before 2:00 p.m. daily, and the approval notice will be issued at 3:00 p.m. on the same day.

(Municipal Government Order to Comply)

The Municipal Government approved the Ministry of Finance's consultation and issued an order yesterday to implement the silver dollar standard, stating, "To: All to be carried out, In response to the Ministry of Finance's Qian Zi No. 5988 consultation stating, the Ministry of Finance, in preparation for the abolition of taels, will first implement it in Shanghai, and has stipulated that the commonly used silver taels and silver dollar standard coins of one yuan in the Shanghai market, or old silver coins of one yuan with the original fixed weight and fineness, will be calculated at a fixed conversion rate of seven qian, one fen and five li per standard tael, equivalent to one silver coin, which will take effect from March 10th of this year, as announced by the Ministry. All public and private payments, settlement of debts and credits, and all transactions and various taxes should be collected and paid in silver coins according to the aforementioned fixed rate, in order to unify the system. In addition to submitting a request to the Executive Yuan to submit it to the National Government for record, and issuing separate consultations, we hereby consult your Municipal Government to investigate and order all subordinates to comply accordingly. This order."

(Conversion to Dollars)

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency met with leaders of the silver money industry yesterday. According to them, after the implementation of the silver dollar standard, the funds of all correspondents that are calculated in silver taels will remain the same. All correspondents who need silver taels tickets can still open them as before. As for the delivery of goods by foreign firms and the payment of various fees, which used to be in silver taels, they can be paid in silver coins at the fixed legal price. Because in the past, those who received silver taels often arbitrarily increased or decreased the dollar rate to profit from the conversion, but now that the price of silver taels is fixed and the dollar has been abolished, there should be no problem.

(Factory Bars Replace Silver Ingots)

Since the Central Mint began minting new coins on March 1st, silver ingots are bound to be eliminated. It is heard that the Mint has decided to issue factory bars, with a fixed weight and fineness, each bar worth one thousand yuan, to replace silver ingots. In the future, the inventories of the silver money industry will all be converted to factory bars. The current number of silver ingots in this city is approximately 230 million taels.
