Jiang Zuobin Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 76

Says He Will Report Everything to the Capital in the Coming Days

For the Time Being, He Is Not Prepared to Express Anything

Whether He Returns to Japan Will Depend on the Government's Orders

The resident ambassador to Japan, Jiang Zuobin, and his wife, along with embassy secretary Ding Shaoji and two attendants, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 1:00 AM aboard the Dollar Steamship Lines' President Cleveland from Japan. The ship was moored at the Bailianjing Wharf in Pudong. Due to the late hour, the Dollar Steamship Lines' ferry only departed from the New Customs Wharf at 7:00 AM yesterday morning to pick up passengers. The municipal government specially dispatched Commissioner Wang Changchun, Councilor Yin Rugeng, and Secretary Tang Shi at 6:30 AM this morning aboard a police bureau boat to Pudong to welcome them. At 8:15 AM,

Ambassador Jiang, Who Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning (Left) (Li Zunyong) 77

Mr. and Mrs. Jiang boarded the welcoming boat and landed at the New Customs Wharf. Central Committee member Zhang Qun and Section Chief Zhao Tiezhang of the Foreign Affairs Office were also at the wharf to greet them. Mr. Jiang then returned to his residence on Lafayette Road in the same car as Zhang Qun. This newspaper's reporter went to visit him this morning. According to Mr. Jiang, regarding the Sino-Japanese issue and everything else, he is not prepared to express anything until he has gone to the capital and conferred with the government. When asked about his return to Japan, he said that he would follow the government's orders in everything and had no preconceived notions of his own. He will be resting at his residence in Shanghai for the time being. It is reported that Ambassador Jiang is scheduled to take the night train to the capital tonight to report on the diplomatic situation with Japan. In addition, Xinsheng News Agency reports that when a reporter questioned Mr. Jiang about the situation in Japan, Mr. Jiang stated that while some Chinese believe that Japan's economy is heading towards collapse, this is greatly mistaken. Economic panic is a common global phenomenon, not unique to Japan. The depreciation of the Japanese exchange rate is actually beneficial to exports because it allows exporting countries to reduce the prices of goods sold abroad. In recent years, Japanese goods have been selling very well in the Indian and Southeast Asian markets, which is evidence of this. While the suspension of foreign exchange by the United States has had some impact on Japan, it is not as severe as the impact on the countries in the Americas. The Chinese people should rise up on their own and not vainly hope that others will be in danger, while neglecting their own efforts.

Eighth Anniversary of Sun Yat-sen's Death 78

Municipal Government Holds Tree Planting Ceremony

This month on the 12th is the eighth anniversary of the death of Kuomintang leader Sun Yat-sen. The central government has stipulated that a tree planting ceremony be held on this day and that the afforestation movement be promoted. The municipal government, in accordance with the central government's regulations, will hold a tree planting ceremony at the Dongjiao Municipal Forest Farm at 10:00 AM on the morning of this day, planting 10,000 saplings. At the same time, 10,000 copies of afforestation slogans will be printed and, starting yesterday, workers have been ordered to post them throughout the city, such as "Afforestation Prevents Floods and Droughts" and "Commemorate the Premier and Complete the Afforestation Plan." The Social Affairs Bureau specially transported 3,000 pine and cypress saplings from the nursery yesterday, filling the courtyard of the bureau, in preparation for the schools to come and collect them to participate in the planting at that time. The order of the tree planting ceremony has been drafted and includes: (1) playing music, (2) all standing at attention, (3) singing the Party song, (4) saluting the Party flag and the Premier's portrait, (5) the chairman reading the Premier's will, (6) a moment of silence, (7) singing the tree planting song, (8) the chairman giving the opening remarks, (9) speeches, (10) tree planting, (11) a photograph, and (12) playing music and adjourning.

The bronze statue of Premier Sun has now been surveyed and determined to be located behind the municipal government building in the city center and in front of the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall. The groundbreaking ceremony is scheduled for March 12th, and the unveiling ceremony for the bronze statue will be held on November 12th.

Elder Ma Xiangbo, 94, Issues Important Statement on the Current Situation 79

Proposes Convening a Temporary National Assembly

To Decide on Overall Policy Toward Japan

Recently, Rehe has fallen and Tianjin and Beijing are in danger. The words and telegrams from all sides emphasize severely punishing Zhang and Tang alone. Elder Ma Xiangbo, 94, has a high-minded and far-sighted vision, and his views are different from others. According to what he said to a reporter from Xinsheng News Agency yesterday, "I once jointly issued a declaration with Mr. Zhang Taiyan, denouncing the Japanese invasion of Rehe. Now, this territory of 600,000 square li has actually been occupied by the Japanese. When I heard the news, I felt like I heard thunder in the spring, and I wanted to cry but had no tears, and I have been depressed ever since. Now that I am being interviewed, I would like to express my thoughts. The Huanggutun Incident was indeed a brutal act by the Japanese. Zhang Xueliang did not avenge his father's death, so what does he have left for loving his country and preserving his race? Avenge a private grievance is not what religious people wish to bring up, but Zhang Xueliang's father was the commander of North China at the time, and his position was inherited by Zhang Xueliang himself. The local officials of the country cannot be arbitrarily assassinated by the enemy. Therefore, Zhang Xueliang's revenge for his father should be the action of human morality and national law. Now, he is still sitting on a large army, living safely day and night, just as someone wrote in a limerick, "Hearing that the Japanese attacked Ma Zhanshan, the Japanese army did not enter Shanhaiguan. There is still a pass inside Shanhaiguan, and the pass is not as happy as inside the boudoir. There is a look of "I am happy here and do not think about Shu." Therefore, Zhang Xueliang cannot settle the case of this monstrous disaster without dismissal, punishment, or resignation.

He should stimulate his conscience, swear to avenge his father, and recover the Northeast, and then he can hope to redeem his past sins and still be worthy of a good man with blood. Otherwise, it will be difficult to escape the judgment of heaven and national law. As for Tang Yulin, he is currently the so-called true colors of the warlords, internally imposing heavy taxes and forcing opium cultivation, and externally fleeing upon hearing the wind, retreating without a fight. There are many like this. However, it is better than the puppets of the old Northeast warlords who refuse to surrender to the Japanese. Moreover, the current problem is definitely not the personal responsibility of Tang and Zhang, but rather our

The problem of national defense and saving the country. I still remember that Ming worthy Shi Kefa said, "In the turmoil of the northern capital, all subjects are guilty. Those in the north should die, but are those in the south not subjects? The generals are able to defeat the enemy because of their courage. The rulers are able to control their generals because of their will. If the will of the court is not courageous, then the courage of the army will not be encouraged. There are not many officials in the south who died for their country, and there are few officials in the north who attacked. This is a disgrace for all ages. " The old man's citation of Shi Gong's words is not intentionally excessive, but to awaken the sense of responsibility of the whole people. In fact, the current crisis is surrounded on all sides. Tianjin and Beijing are difficult to defend. Therefore, the so-called ancient objects are ordered to be transported south, and the National University of Peking is also discussing moving to a better place. Since North China is not consolidated, enemy ships are densely deployed along the coastal ports of the Yangtze River, and the capital is in danger again. Moreover, the Japanese so-called lifeline on the water extends to Southeast Asia, and their navy can invade various ports in South China at any time. Therefore, in such a situation, our people can only support the country and resist the enemy as a whole. We must use the strength of the whole country to commit crimes against us, and we

Only partial resistance will not work. It is a pity that the current national policy is extremely confusing. Not only is the foreign enemy invading on a large scale, as if the thief has already entered the house, but the brothers in the family do not love each other, such as the internal turmoil in Sichuan and Guizhou. We must wait for the thief to use a knife on everyone's body before we will be willing to defend ourselves. Of course, it is too late. The Battle of Shanghai and the recent events in Rehe were all initiated by the enemy, and we counterattacked. And we must wait for the enemy to complete their defenses before we start to fight in different places, and we flee without a fight.

It is really outrageous. At the same time, the violent enemy freely dispatches naval, land, and air forces, hoping for more after gaining something, gaining an inch and wanting a foot, and now they declare that they will take Chahar. I don't know if General Feng Yuxiang, who is currently singing anti-Japanese sentiments in that area, is also actively uniting his people to prepare to resist the enemy. Moreover, our country recently recalled its ambassador to Japan, while Japanese diplomats are very active in our country, exhausting all important Chinese and foreign figures to lobby, implementing a "sweet-mouthed and vicious-hearted" diplomatic policy. They also set up intelligence bureaus in major cities, openly acting as national military spies. As for our citizens who enter Japan, they are often illegally detained or monitored. There are news reports every day. Under such a distorted phenomenon, it is no wonder that our representatives to the League of Nations have jointly resigned. Since the September 18th Incident, our country

What exactly is the overall policy towards Japan? The country is in such danger that the government urgently needs the support of the people. I propose that a national assembly be convened immediately, and the government and the people will jointly plan the national policy. The necessary reasons for the national assembly and the way to adopt it will be briefly stated. I remember the Franco-Prussian War. France was invaded, and in a very critical period, a "daddy" came out and proposed convening a national assembly, which laid the foundation for the dangerous situation at that time. Our country's national crisis is now the same, so we should convene representatives of the whole people. The attending representatives should be publicly elected by the people's autonomous groups in each county. The purpose of holding this kind of national assembly is to address important national issues.

Submit it to a national referendum. (1) The issue of war or peace with Japan. In today's situation, we are neither at war nor at peace, and the violent enemy is implementing a policy of gradual encroachment. Today they take a city, and tomorrow they clear a village, so that the officials who do not fight flee upon hearing the wind, and the people's volunteer army loses its base. At the same time, we neither declare a break in relations nor declare that we will not sign a peace treaty, missing the opportunity and losing the country. Therefore, the general will of the people must be given the opportunity to a public vote. As in the previous National Crisis Conference, it was only a so-called advisory body, and the important decisions it made, such as unanimous resistance to insults, were all filed for future reference. Only the resolutions of this kind of national assembly must be implemented by our national government, so that the future of the country will be determined in one fell swoop. (2) The issue of overall national defense. The national military and political affairs must be unified for the sake of national defense. Those who are only loyal to the country and the national government, even a dictatorship is acceptable. We must use the will of the whole people to break the current situation of division and segregation. All military leaders lead their troops back to the country, so that the national army can be used for national defense. As for those who privately raise troops and engage in internal turmoil, the people will publicly judge them, and the crime is unforgivable. (3) The issue of overall financial planning. Because of foreign defense, large expenses are required. The people will publicly decide whether to borrow foreign debt or issue public debt, so that the soldiers defending against insults will have a constant supply of funds and do not need to raise funds in a scattered manner. Because a drop in the bucket is difficult to help. Other internal affairs to be resolved should be decided by the public will of the people. In short, the way to save the country in the future is only the method of "national defense against insults." The revival of the Republic of China depends on this move.

Rice Merchants' Strike Case Discussed by the Social Affairs Bureau Yesterday 83

The discussion did not result in a good solution. A second instrument inspection will be held today.

The rice merchants in southern Shanghai have been on strike in protest against the heavy official measure, and this has been going on for two weeks. The rice industry of the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce, because the merchants have blocked rice boats and affected people's food, have submitted to the Municipal Government's Social Affairs Bureau to find a way to solve the problem as soon as possible. The Social Affairs Bureau specially convened various groups yesterday to discuss the method, and decided to re-measure the instruments today to determine the method. The details are recorded below.

The Party and government organs have determined a method of consultation, and have not yet resolved the problem of dispute of measuring instruments, affecting the people's food. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the Social Affairs Bureau convened various rice industry groups to discuss methods. Those who attended included Jiang Huaisu and He Yuanming from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Wu Huanru, Zhang Binghui, and Zhou Minggang from the Social Affairs Bureau, Zhou Zanming from the Bureau of Weights and Measures, Lu Wenshao from the Rice Industry Trade Association, Gu Xinyi from the Bean and Rice Industry Trade Association, Zhang Songtao from the Grains and Rice Trade Association, Cai Yukun from the Miscellaneous Grain and Cake Industry Association, Zhu Zixiang from the Rice Milling Industry Trade Association, Jiang Shizhi from the Shanghai North Transport Rice Merchants Union, Chen Zhiqiang from the Shanghai South Transport Rice Merchants Union, Lu Gongquan, Jin Weixiang, and Lu Junwen from the various Rice Firms, and Lu Quanlin and Cai Mingwang from the Instrument Measurement Union. More than 20 people were present. The meeting was chaired by Zhang Binghui. As a result of the discussion, the two sides had different opinions and could not be decided.

The various masters involved in the second meter inspection and Party and government organs failed to reach an agreement. The Liangyi Association required the implementation of the level measure and funnel, and the Rice Company number requested the abolition of the volume and the change of weight. Party and government representatives believed that the use of funnels was too time-consuming, and the abolition of volume and the change of weight did not have such a system in the mainland, so it was difficult to implement. It was decided that a second inspection of the measuring instrument will be carried out at the Rengutang on Zhonghua Road at 1:00 PM this afternoon, with a considerable amount of liters as the standard. If there is expansion and contraction, it will be calculated by light and heavy measures.

Fourth Army Deputy Commander Cheng Dejun of Ma Bu Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 86

Says His Unit Still Has 16,000 Men

Urgently Hopes Fellow Countrymen Will Continue to Help Resist the Enemy

General Cheng Dejun, Deputy Commander of the Fourth Army under General Ma Zhanshan, participated in the Jiangqiao Anti-Japanese War. He fought hard for over a year and made significant contributions. This time, due to running out of ammunition and food, he led his troops to retreat to the Xiaoxing'anling area in eastern Heilongjiang. Cheng went to the interior to seek assistance. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning from Pingnan. A reporter from the Riri News Agency interviewed him at his residence. The details of the interview are recorded below. After Su Bingwen and Zhang Dianjiu's unsuccessful battles, General Ma's troops were forced to retreat due to heavy enemy pressure. General Ma retreated to Russian territory. I led the army in early September of last year, passing through the Nenjiang Nehe from Laha Station to Dedor, intending to reorganize and replenish the troops. At that time, the armies of Deng Wen and Li Haiqing also successively moved to the Rehe border. After we arrived in western Dedor, we came into contact with the puppet state Gao group. Our army resisted strongly, and the 12th Brigade Commander Li Zuolin was martyred, but the group was ultimately disarmed by us, suffering heavy losses. The enemy, knowing our army's fierceness, had the Japanese Gao Po Brigade commander coerce two brigades of the puppet army to surrender in Gannan. At that time, Jia Bochen and Cheng Zhiyuan had already surrendered and sent letters urging us. Since I could not guarantee the integrity of the army, and retreat was difficult, I convened a meeting of officers above the brigade commander level to resolve the situation. They all advocated ["Better to be a Ningzuo rebel than a slave of a fallen nation."] Without surrendering to the puppet state, after being presided over by the Japanese Gao Po Commander and negotiating with me for four weeks without resolution, the army's food supply was running out and there was no way to replenish it. Fortunately, Xu Jingde, the acting Deputy Commander stationed in Jiang, allocated food, and we retreated to the Xiaoxing'anling area in eastern Heilongjiang, conscripting food from the people as temporary relief. About 1,800 soldiers returned to their hometowns, but they all left their weapons behind, now buried in the soil. The remaining troops still number over 16,000, occupying dangerous mountain areas, determined not to surrender to the enemy. However, both bullets and food are lacking. The weather in the northern border region is extremely cold, and we are still wearing single-layered clothing. As the commander, I am truly filled with grief and indignation. Moreover, since our army commander Xu Haiting has already gone to Shanghai, and Chairman Ma Xiufang will also return from Russia, I specifically went to the interior to request assistance from fellow countrymen across the nation, so that we can continue to resist the enemy. Commanders Pu Bingshan and Cai Hongyou, as well as the three army commanders Nan Tingfang and Zhang Xiwu, have 60,000 men hiding in various locations. If they can receive active assistance, they can rise up again immediately and fight against the enemy. As for the puppet state of Manchuria's Zhang Haipeng, Cheng Guorui, and Zi Zhishan, they can also be persuaded to understand the greater righteousness and revolt against the Japanese. Moreover, with the arrival of spring, the soil in Heilongjiang is thawing, and the muddy and rugged terrain renders enemy tanks ineffective, allowing our side to seize the opportunity to launch a major offensive and recover lost territory. Since the September 18th Incident, I have long disregarded life and death, only seeking that the soldiers have bullets and food. I will then return to Heilongjiang to lead troops to kill the enemy, restraining the Japanese army's rear. If the Japanese advance into North China and the Jiangnan region, it cannot be averted without a unified national resistance.

China National Products Introduction Center Officially Established Today Branch Offices to Be Established in Various Locations 88

The China National Products Production and Sales Cooperative Association, organized by Shanghai's national product manufacturers, has been preparing to establish a China National Products Introduction Center in Shanghai since its establishment, and plans to set up branch offices in various locations in order to awaken the nation's unified adoption of national products. It is reported that the China National Products Introduction Center has been fully prepared, and the address has been selected at No. 1 Yuemingyuan Road. Xie Yunting has been appointed as the manager, and Shi Qichen and Lu Qianting as the deputy managers. The official establishment will be held today. Here is the opening declaration of the China National Products Production and Sales Cooperative Association, Shanghai General Office of the China National Products Introduction Center. At this time of global economic panic, people from all countries are doing their utmost to increase and expand production and stabilize and balance consumption. How can our backward country, trapped in dire straits, not rise up and quickly seek countermeasures, recognize the direction, and determine the most effective and practical method to save the country? What is the method? It is to promote national products. Promoting national products is the fundamental work to solve the people's livelihood problem, the only way to strive for material construction, the supreme weapon to prevent international oppression and establish national defense, and the goal that people across the country should strive for together. However, promoting national products has been talked about repeatedly. Instead of empty talk, it is better to ask for implementation. In seeking implementation, the most effective and powerful work should be adopted first. Today, compatriots across the country all have the hope of using national products. With this keen need, there must be a sufficient supply. Therefore, thorough research must be conducted on the quantity, quality, and price of national products, so that the items supplied by the producers can meet the standards needed by the people of the country, and consumers can have the convenience of identifying and purchasing national products. Only then can supply and demand be met, and goods be fully utilized and smoothly circulated. With China's vast territory and abundant production, if we want to correct the mistakes of the past and determine the direction of the future, it will not be possible without the joint efforts of producers and sellers to implement thorough cooperation. In order to complete this mission of cooperation, it is even more necessary to have a sound organizational structure and unified national assistance. Adhering to this purpose, this association has gathered national product manufacturers in Shanghai to organize the China National Products Production and Sales Cooperative Association, which has been registered with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and has received strong support from the government. On the one hand, it is responsible for promoting the products of national product factories and improving publicity. On the other hand, it is responsible for introducing the production and industrial raw materials of various places to domestic and foreign markets. In order to further promote its effectiveness and usefulness in the interior, national product introduction branch offices are set up in various places to introduce goods from various places to domestic and foreign markets, report consumption situations, display national product samples, and accept wholesale orders, so that the people of the country can recognize the advantages of national products and distinguish the standards for selection and purchase, so that producers have no worries about not being able to sell and consumers are spared the trouble of selecting and seeking. The National Product Introduction Center is established at No. 1 Yuemingyuan Road, Shanghai, to serve as the hub for promoting national products to the interior, receiving orders, and investigating consumption. This association will also engage in research on improving [quality], increasing [quantity], balancing [prices], and [market] conditions, with the aim of establishing a close relationship between producers and sellers and achieving the effect of division of labor and cooperation. As the General Office is now completed and officially opened, this association has something to tell the people of society. The organization of the National Product Introduction Center is an organic body with a cellular function. In the future, it should do its best to promote and exercise its functions and strive to be the vanguard of society. However, supply arises from needs, and sales are valued for their universality. How to purchase and use as much as possible, and how to provide as much assistance and guidance as possible, depends on the people of the country to provide a strong backing in order to achieve success. It is also hoped that entrepreneurs will take it as their duty to research products and reduce costs, laborers will take it as their responsibility to refine technology and increase production, women will take purchasing national products as a prerequisite for consumption, and children will take using national products as a great honor. In this way, with the same steps and the same goal, each fulfilling their national responsibility and working hard in their respective positions, the total mobilization of the national product movement will be realized. The smooth sales of national products can be expected soon, and the opportunity for this association to serve will also be increased. The revitalization of China's economy will be realized, which is not only the honor of this association. However, at the beginning of the creation, there are many shortcomings. We hope that people from all walks of life will not hesitate to give us instructions. Furthermore, the China National Products Introduction Center

Annual Work of the International Chamber of Commerce 89

Thomas, the Commander of the International Chamber of Commerce in the Public Concession, has prepared a report on the activities of the Chamber of Commerce in 1932 and submitted it to the Public Works Department. The summary is as follows:

Annual Inspection

The annual inspection of the Chamber of Commerce last year was conducted by Major General Fleming, the British Commander in Shanghai. His inspection report has been published in the Public Works Department Gazette in July.

Mobilization Work

On January 28th of last year, the Chamber of Commerce mobilized the Russian Volunteer Corps to guard the defense line with four hours' notice. Within six hours, all corps were mobilized and concentrated. At that time, there were many personnel shortages, and the infantry had only 50% of its personnel. Within ten days of mobilization, recruitment was continuously increased, and the total number increased from 1,500 to 2,300. However, most of the newly recruited members lacked training, and military uniforms and boots were also incomplete, which was extremely difficult. However, the general spirit was very good. Several corps members who lived in the vicinity of Distsheng suffered robbery of all their belongings at home because they were eager to go to the call. This is especially memorable.

Personnel Replenishment

Due to the experience of mobilization, personnel have been replenished. However, the infantry still has a shortage of 27%, which is about 400 people. New teams have been organized to increase the number of people. Efforts have been made to list former military personnel and other experienced personnel as reserve members of each team, and they will be called up with their respective teams when necessary.

Clothing and Provisions

Military boots are essential. Many of those who were called up last year only wore cloth shoes, which were not suitable. If military boots were provided completely free of charge, it would not only be very expensive, but the team members would often leave after a few months. Therefore, the current method is to prepare a certain number of military boots, which team members can purchase at cost price. In the future, new team members will be required to prepare their own boots. In addition, the overcoats used by the team members cannot protect against rain. Waterproof jackets have now been prepared for distribution during the call-up. As for the food for the team members when they depart, it has been customary to issue money for them to purchase themselves. This is inconvenient during active operations. Now the headquarters has prepared a method of providing food itself, so that the team members serving in the first place can be transferred at will without having to worry about food.

Transportation and Engineering

During the mobilization of the Chamber of Commerce, transportation was handled by the Public Works Department, which was very satisfactory. However, in view of the need for transporting supplies, a transportation team has been formed for command. Most of the officers in the team are employees of the Public Works Department. As for the engineering team, it was being reorganized at the time of mobilization. Currently, the team is entirely composed of Public Works Department personnel. During the deployment, the Public Works Department personnel worked extremely hard, adding barbed wire and creating several miles in a very short time.

Names of Each Team

In addition to the General Headquarters, the Chamber of Commerce has the following organizations: Shanghai Light Cavalry, Volunteer Corps, Shanghai Land Artillery, Shanghai Light Artillery, Engineering Team, Armored Vehicle Team, A Team, B Team, American Volunteer Team, Portuguese Team, Japanese Volunteer Team, Chinese Team, Scottish Volunteer Team, H Team, Philippine Team, American Volunteer Machine Gun Team, American Volunteer Reserve Team, Transportation Team, Internal Transportation Team, Interpreter Team, Air Defense Team, Russian Volunteer Team (composed of four squads, the first, second, and fourth squads are regular corps members, and the third squad are volunteer corps members), and Public School Trainee Team. In addition, there are military musicians, drivers, medical staff, chaplains, reserve officers, and reserve corps members, totaling 191 officers and 1,943 corps members.

French Concession Police Uncover a Large Gang of Taihu Bandits 91

Rescuing a Kidnapped Farmer from Dangshan Bay, Jiaxing

Yesterday, the French Concession police uncovered a large gang of Taihu bandits who had come to Shanghai from Jiaxing. They rescued a kidnapped victim from Jiaxing on the spot, and arrested a total of eleven male and female bandits. The details are described below.

(Farmer's Life)

In Dangshan Bay, outside the South Gate of Jiaxing, there lived a farmer named Chen Tianyou, aged 48, who was relatively well-off. He had a wife, Nee, and only one son and one daughter. His eldest daughter was already engaged, and his son, named Zurong (nicknamed Amao), was 14 years old. He was intelligent by nature and had a dignified appearance, unlike most farm children. Therefore, the elderly couple loved him like the apple of their eye. At the age of seven, he began studying at a local private school. The family lived in harmony, enjoying their rural life. Unexpectedly, disaster struck from within.

(Taihu Bandits)

Because Chen's family was relatively well-off, they had long been noticed by bandits. It happened that in the middle of the first lunar month of this year, at dusk, more than ten Taihu bandits suddenly arrived. They first looted all of Chen's property and then kidnapped Chen's beloved son, Zurong. Afterwards, the bandits transferred the hostage to Shanghai by waterway and hid him in a bandit den at No. 3 Ping'anfang, Lane 155, Xuehuali Road, in the French Concession.

(Negotiations in Shanghai)

After losing his beloved son, Chen was distraught. Before long, he received a letter from the bandits demanding a ransom of 4,000 yuan. After repeated negotiations, because the amounts were too far apart, it was impossible to reach an agreement. Recently, they sent another letter inviting Chen to Shanghai, stating that they would meet him at the entrance of Baoyuli, Caishi Street, in the French Concession at around 8:00 am yesterday. After receiving the letter, Chen immediately sent someone to Shanghai to negotiate everything.

(Bandits' Extravagant Desires)

After Chen's representative arrived in Shanghai, he knew that the bandits' desires were too extravagant and feared that there would be no satisfactory outcome. Therefore, he resolutely entrusted someone to secretly report to Jin Jiulin, Inspector of the French Concession Police. At around 8:00 am yesterday, Inspector Jin notified Detective Henry of the Western Branch, who immediately led detectives Zhang Ziying, Zhou Yaoting, Zhou Bingcheng, Qin Youyu, detective Cai Jinzhang, Ma Yizhi, Zhang Chunsheng, and Xu Guilin, disguised themselves and secretly carried weapons, and first ambushed themselves at the entrance of Baoyuli.

(Lowest Ransom Price)

First, Chen's representative, according to the bandits' letter, made a mark and stood waiting at the entrance of Baoyuli. At around 8:00 am, he saw a person greet him and then led him to Room 4 of the Huhai Inn in the lane to talk secretly. At this time, the detectives rushed in and arrested two bandits on the spot. They also found a ransom letter addressed to Chen in the crotch of the bandit leader Shen Yuyun's pants. The envelope was marked "To be handed over in person [Received by Mr. Chen Tianyou]." The sender was named [Shen Chuanjun]. The content stated that 3,500 yuan was the lowest ransom price.

(Hostage Rescued)

After the two bandits were arrested, three more people were arrested in Room 32 of the Changxing Hotel at the intersection of Xinxiao Street, Caishi Street. They confessed the location of the hostage, and the hostage was rescued by address. Finally, three men and one woman were intercepted in Room 12 of the Huadong Apartment on Malong Road, and one man and one woman were arrested on Fulilou Road. A total of eleven people were arrested. All of them were interrogated by the police chief and ordered to be detained separately, pending transfer to the court for strict investigation. As of the reporter's deadline, the police are still continuing their investigation.

News of the Long-Missing Yurong Ship Sinking 92

Searched for Without Success by Customs Offices Everywhere

Rumored to Have Sunk Near Qiongzhou

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Yurong, a ship represented by the Tongyu Shipping Company, set sail from Hongji on December 8th of last year, loaded with coal, heading for Shanghai. It suddenly disappeared. The company offered a reward for its search, but there was no trace. According to reliable sources, the ship encountered a hurricane and sank near Hainan Island. The details are as follows:

(Searched Everywhere Without Success)

After the Yurong ship disappeared, customs offices everywhere used radio to search for it without success. The crew members' families were extremely frightened and requested assistance from the company. Although the company offered a large reward, there was still no news. The company sent three people, including the brother of the ship's first mate, to Hong Kong to search along the way. The company received a telegram from Hong Kong yesterday reporting that they were also unable to find it. According to company personnel, the Yurong ship must have had an accident and sunk. If it had been stolen, there would not have been no news until now. The shipping industry generally believes that it encountered a hurricane and sank.

(Encountered a Hurricane and Sank)

Yesterday, a Xin Sheng News Agency reporter learned from a seaman from Hongji who was familiar with navigation (i.e., the pilot who took the ship out) that the Yurong ship sank near Hainan Island after leaving port. As for the reason for the sinking, the Yurong ship was overloaded with coal, and the waterline was more than one foot over. It was very dangerous when leaving the port. Encountering a hurricane near Hainan Island, an overloaded ship could not resist the strong winds and waves, so it sank in an instant. The crew members were unable to escape. It is learned that the ship's load capacity was only 2,700 tons, but this time it was loaded with 2,400 tons of coal.

Xu Peikun Discusses the American Financial Crisis 93

Xu Peikun, President of the National Shanghai College of Commerce, is a veteran of economic studies. When the reporter asked him about the American financial crisis yesterday, Xu shared the following views: The American financial crisis has been going on for more than four years. The reason why we are paying attention to it today is because the recent turmoil seems to be more serious. It is like a fire in a house that has broken through the roof. The thick smoke and flames are frightening. Today, we learned that American banks have gradually resumed business, and the Shanghai Gold Standard Market is still active, soaring by more than ten taels, as if the American financial crisis has been resolved and the fire in the house has been extinguished.

Mr. Zhu Sues Daughter-in-Law and In-Laws for Abandonment After the Untimely Death of His Beloved Son 94

Not living together in life, not attending his side in illness, not relying on his coffin in death.

Mr. Zhu Sui laments the premature death of his son, expressing his feelings in words, unable to bear it in his heart.

The daughter-in-law, supporting herself despite illness, arrived in court, tears streaming down her face; her situation is also pitiful.

| The judge, with good intentions, hopes that both parties will reconcile |

Zhu Junsui, from Yin County, Zhejiang, is currently sixty-three years old. He lives at No. 63, Sen Yi Lane, Shanhaiguan Road, Meibai Ge Road, and works at the Nanyang Advertising Company on Fuzhou Road. Recently, he hired a lawyer to file a criminal complaint with the First Special District Court against his daughter-in-law, Wu Huilian (age 26, from Suzhou), and her parents, Wu Xunqing and his daughter, for abandonment.

The complaint roughly states that his son was abandoned by his daughter-in-law while ill, leading to his death. He requests severe punishment according to the law. It reads: "I, the plaintiff, am nearing seventy years old and approaching the end of my life. The world is bustling and chaotic, and I have tasted all the bitterness of life. The only comfort in my old age is my children. My second son, Zhongkan, was intelligent from a young age. When he grew up, I arranged a marriage for him to fulfill my long-cherished wish. On October 18th of the twentieth year of the Republic of China, he married Wu Huilian. I thought that as a young couple, their love would be steadfast, sharing clothes and food, bringing comfort in my twilight years. Unexpectedly, Huilian was naturally strong and independent and did not maintain proper behavior, leaving our home to build her own nest. Out of deep love for my son, I did not dare to completely disregard her wishes, only hoping that she would have a good home and that they would maintain a harmonious relationship. This single thought was enough to comfort me. Unexpectedly, in the late spring of last year, Zhongkan fell ill. After treatment by both Chinese and Western doctors, his condition seemed manageable. However, because his wife was restless and her whereabouts were vague, and not long after their marriage, she repeatedly used excuses to return to her parents' home. In August, she left and never returned. There was no one to prepare medicine or tea, no one to care for him, and his illness worsened, increasing his loneliness. Like grass in late autumn, how could he withstand the frost? Like a flower subjected to torment, how could he endure the heavy rain? As a result, his illness lingered, and even doctors were helpless. His youthful vigor was completely depleted. Seeing him tossing and turning in bed, moaning on his pillow, calling out with no one to answer, leaving his feelings to whom? The pitiful state was unbearable to witness. I am old and frail, unable to care for myself, let alone provide for him. Zhongkan was alone and could not bear to be alone. Although I tried many ways to persuade her to return, hoping that someone would care for him and his illness would improve, she repeatedly refused with various excuses, claiming to be ill. Zhongkan was heartbroken upon hearing this, losing all interest in life, and his illness worsened, becoming incurable. No one could be found to take on the responsibility of caring for him. Like Bo Dao, who had no descendants, there was no one to bring joy to his face. Material support was nonexistent, and spiritual pain was profound. Who is without feelings, who can endure this? His illness was incurable for this reason. Thus, less than a year after the marriage, Zhongkan passed away on November 25th of last year. Alas, how painful! Counting the days since Huilian returned to her parents' home until Zhongkan's death, there were over a hundred days. During this period, Huilian neither appeared nor inquired about him. Her intentions are incomprehensible. As his legal wife, she abruptly abandoned her sick husband. Her cruel behavior is despised by humanity. Therefore, although Huilian did not kill Zhongkan directly, Zhongkan died because of Huilian. I still remember my deceased son's final moments, tears welling up in his eyes, calling out his wife's name, as if wanting to see her one last time to express his heart full of sorrow. The scene was so desolate that everyone present shed tears and felt heartbroken. Yet, the defendant remained indifferent, so heartless that it was beyond normal. Now, two months have passed since Zhongkan's death. Despite repeated notifications of his death and invitations for the seventh-day ceremony, she has disappeared without a trace. I am an old man in my twilight years, suffering such misfortune, grieving over the premature death of my beloved son, and filled with unbearable anger. As husband and wife, they did not live together in life, she did not attend his side in illness, she did not rely on his coffin in death, and she did not weep at his funeral. The facts are clear and cannot be concealed. Her malicious abandonment is undeniable. Zhongkan was originally self-sufficient, but when his illness became incurable, he had no ability to save himself. Wu Huilian, as Zhongkan's wife, was legally obligated to provide support and protection. Now, Huilian not only failed to fulfill this obligation but also suddenly returned to her parents' home when Zhongkan was seriously ill and never returned, leading to Zhongkan's death. Her actions violate Article 310 and the second clause of the Criminal Law. Wu Xunqing instigated his daughter's actions and should be punished equally according to Article 43 of the same law. If justice is served and my grievance is redressed, I will be eternally grateful, whether in life or in death." The court accepted the complaint and issued a warrant to summon the defendants. On October 18th, both parties were summoned for questioning. As the plaintiff did not appear, the court dismissed the complaint. Upon hearing this, Zhu Junsui entrusted his lawyer to submit a justification and appeal for reinstatement. The collegial panel approved the request, and the case was scheduled for a hearing yesterday afternoon. A summons was issued to the defendants, and Chinese constable Guo Xiang was dispatched to notify them. After receiving the summons, Wu Huilian also hired lawyer Zhu Sifu to submit a response.

The defense roughly states, regarding the abandonment case brought by Zhu Junsui, that she is responding according to the law. She states that in the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, she was betrothed to the deceased Zhu Zhongkan through parental arrangement. Due to Zhongkan's illness, the marriage was postponed until November 1st of the twentieth year of the Republic of China. At that time, he was still coughing up blood, and his lung disease worsened after the marriage. He received medical treatment for years, with varying degrees of improvement, but never fully recovered. Later, the defendant also became ill, and medical treatment was ineffective. On August 18th of the twenty-first year of the Republic of China, she returned to her parents' home, and her illness worsened. On November 17th of the same year, she went to Hangzhou for medical treatment. Her body, weakened by prolonged illness, was further strained by the journey, and she was bedridden. Zhongkan passed away while the defendant was seriously ill. She is still receiving medical treatment, and any significant movement causes dizziness. This is the factual situation of the defendant's condition after marriage and her current state of illness. Now, the plaintiff is suing for abandonment. In a family where father, son, and brothers live together and share property, suing the daughter-in-law for abandonment after the son's death, whether the defendant, as a wife, receives no financial support from the plaintiff for food, clothing, and medicine, constitutes abandonment should be determined first according to law and considering the circumstances. The complaint states that October 18th of the twentieth year of the Republic of China was the date of the defendant's marriage to Zhongkan, which is inconsistent with the facts. The complaint also claims that she was restless and her whereabouts were vague. Considering that the defendant was a wife of a sick husband at the beginning of the marriage, constantly providing medicine and filled with sorrow, how could she be restless and her whereabouts vague in just ten months? These are baseless accusations and arbitrary defamation. The plaintiff has no pity for his daughter-in-law, how can he comfort his deceased son in the afterlife? A lawsuit between the paternal grandfather and daughter-in-law after the son's death is a family tragedy that the defendant cannot bear to speak of. Therefore, she has submitted this statement to express her grief and earnestly requests a judgment according to the law. Wu Xunqing, in addition to hiring lawyer Pei to respond, also filed a countersuit against Zhu Junsui for false accusation. Judge Qian Wen of the Second Criminal Division of the court presided over the hearing.

Both parties, along with their lawyers, appeared in court. The defendant, Wu Huilian, dressed in plain clothes and appearing ill, was supported by a female relative. Her lawyer, Zhu Sifu, stated that Wu Huilian was summoned to court despite her illness and requested permission for her to remain seated during the hearing due to her frailty, which was granted by the court. The plaintiff, Zhu Junsui, stated that he had two sons. The elder son, currently thirty-two years old, works at the Minghua Bank. The younger son, Zhongkan, was twenty-three years old and worked in the gauze exchange with the defendant, Wu Xunqing. Zhongkan was originally very healthy. On October 18th of the twentieth year of the Republic of China, he married Wu Huilian. Within two months, Zhongkan became ill, and Huilian frequently returned to her parents' home. On January 28th of last year, she left and never returned. This was at the time when Zhongkan was seriously ill. When people were sent to call her, she ignored them and went to Hangzhou for leisure. Wu Xunqing, as her father, should have advised her to return to her husband's home. Not only did he fail to advise her, but he also did not visit his son-in-law when he was seriously ill. Therefore, they are jointly accused. The judge stated that according to Zhu Junsui's statement, the only accusation against Wu Xunqing was his failure to visit his sick son-in-law, which is a matter of morality and human relations and cannot be considered a crime. Wu Huilian testified that she married Zhongkan on October 1st of the lunar calendar of the previous year. Within three or four days of the marriage, she saw Zhongkan coughing up blood and asked him about it. He said it was nothing and that he had been coughing up blood for two years. She also had an illness and agreed with her husband to return to her parents' home. At that time, her husband was as usual. Later, her husband also often visited her. Because her illness has lingered until now, she has not returned. Her relationship with her husband was very close in ordinary times. Tears streamed down her face, overwhelmed with sadness. Lawyer Zhu presented medical prescriptions and doctor's diagnoses to the court. The judge persuaded Zhu Junsui, saying that he and the defendants were all relatives, one being his in-laws and the other being his daughter-in-law. Moreover, Zhongkan died of illness and not because the defendants had any malicious intent. As for Wu Xunqing, his failure to visit his sick son-in-law is a matter of human relations and morality and not related to the law. Therefore, it would be better to attempt reconciliation outside of court to avoid a prolonged lawsuit that would harm both sides. If the feelings between them cannot be restored in the future, and if this case is pursued further, the outcome is difficult to predict. Zhu Junsui did not heed this advice. The witnesses Shao Yefu and Chai Zhixian were questioned. The court ordered the commencement of arguments. The lawyers for both parties stood up in turn and argued for a long time. The judge still adhered to the principle of settling matters peacefully and advised Zhu Junsui. He also said that the lawyers for both parties have already argued. According to the rules, a conclusion can be announced, a judgment can be rendered in court, or a judgment can be scheduled for a later date. However, if a judgment is rendered, one party will inevitably lose. To maintain the future relationship between the two parties and avoid a split, a chance will be given. The case will not be concluded today but will be reviewed again in seven days. It is hoped that a reconciliation can be reached and the case can be withdrawn. Otherwise, a judgment will be rendered at that time. Both parties agreed and withdrew. It is unknown what the outcome of this case involving the daughter-in-law and her parents will be.

Looking at the actual content, the American financial turmoil today is like the financial turmoil of four years ago. The current turmoil has not subsided and remains the same. The fire in the room, although extinguished, can easily be rekindled. The causes of the American financial turmoil are extremely complex, but I have spoken of them four years ago and have not changed my position. The events of the past four years have conformed to what I said. When the Kemmerer Commission was in Shanghai, it advocated for China to adopt the gold standard. I repeatedly refuted this in numerous articles. At that time, there were various opinions among the Chinese people, with some supporting and some opposing, and no consensus was reached. In less than a year, countries abandoned the gold standard one after another, and the Chinese people began to believe that what I said was not wrong and had meaning. Several months ago, representatives from the United Kingdom, the United States, and France attending the International Economic Conference declared that these three countries were determined to maintain the gold standard and that they firmly believed that only by restoring the gold standard could the world's commercial decline be remedied. When this statement came out, those in China who advocated for the gold standard cited it as a good thing, believing that China should also follow the example of major countries. At that time, I deeply feared that the Chinese people would change their position again. Fortunately, in recent weeks, the Legislative Yuan has passed and implemented the silver standard law, which is truly a blessing for our country. The gold standard system that I mentioned is the fundamental and primary cause of the current American financial turmoil and the world's commercial decline. If the United States does not abandon the gold standard, the turmoil in the United States will not subside. Furthermore, if countries do not abandon the gold standard, there is no hope for the world's commercial decline to recover. In addition to the gold standard, the Sino-Japanese War, the increase in the number of unemployed people in the world, and the economic activities of Russia are all related causes of the American financial turmoil. The Sino-Japanese War is a particularly significant underlying cause. The trade relations between China and Japan with various countries are extremely important. Now, due to the war, they have withdrawn from the international market, and the industrial and commercial enterprises and laborers of various countries have been greatly affected, which in turn affects the finances of the United States. It is particularly noteworthy that the Sino-Japanese War will likely trigger a second world war and will plunge the world's economic decline into an unrecoverable state. If the Sino-Japanese War is not resolved, the world's economic decline will inevitably become more severe, with no possibility of escaping it. Some economists have stated that excessive speculation and overproduction are the causes of today's economic decline. If "excessive speculation" refers to the speculation caused by the gold-silver price ratio, it may be reasonable. In reality, it exposes the ills of the gold standard. As for "overproduction," it is a ridiculous argument. World production is not excessive. Regarding the impact of the current American financial turmoil on China, both positive and negative, I will list the most noteworthy points as follows: (1) Since China is on the silver standard, when gold becomes cheap, silver will inevitably become expensive. China's wealth will increase significantly, and its purchasing power will also increase significantly. Goods that cannot be produced domestically can be easily exchanged with a small number of silver coins. This is the first benefit for our country. (2) When silver becomes expensive in our country, our wealth will increase, and our international credit will naturally increase. The status of international public debt will naturally increase. This is the second benefit for our country. (3) When silver becomes expensive in our country, international trade is expected to become active, and tax revenue will increase accordingly. This is the third benefit. However, there is also a negative aspect, which is not insignificant. When silver becomes expensive, imports will increase. Our country's industry is still in its early stages, and due to fierce competition, the sales of domestic goods will inevitably be hit. It is necessary to increase import tariffs to counteract this. There are many other related issues, which I will discuss in detail when I have the opportunity.

Shouts of Kidnapping on Luban Road 95

But the car sped away

The identity of the hostage is unknown

Yesterday at 5:45 PM, passersby on Luban Road, at the entrance of Xingxing Lane in the Second District of Nanshi, suddenly heard shouts of kidnapping. Soon, someone reported it to the Yulin Road Police Station under its jurisdiction, claiming that a black car without license plates had been parked near the entrance of Xingxing Lane. Case of Vietnamese Constable Shooting a Chinese Person 96

External Instruction Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 97

Various parties are actively engaging in negotiations

The United Association will continue its meeting today

The case of a Vietnamese constable shooting a Chinese person on Dongxinqiao Street in the French Concession has been ongoing for two weeks. Although various sectors are very indignant, the French authorities have not yet made a concrete statement. The United Association for the Tragedy, organized by various hometown associations and groups, is actively engaging in negotiations. The external instruction arrived in Shanghai yesterday, with details as follows:

External Instruction

After receiving the telegram from the Ningbo Association in Shanghai, the Diplomatic Bureau instructed the association yesterday, with document number Zhengzi 10164, regarding the telegram submitted by the Ningbo Association in Shanghai concerning the case of the Vietnamese constable shooting Liu Fugao in the French Concession, requesting negotiations. The telegram was noted. The Shanghai Municipal Government has been instructed to promptly investigate and initiate negotiations. You are hereby informed. Upon receiving this instruction, the association immediately recorded it and distributed it to various groups for reference.

Legal Deliberations

Regarding the legal issues of this case, the lawyers met at the Ningbo Association the day before yesterday to discuss and decide on a plan. It was generally agreed that the public prosecution portion of this case falls under the jurisdiction of the French police. According to lawyer Wu Kaisheng's report, the French police have already appointed a French lawyer as their litigation agent. He can appear in court to assist with everything during the public hearing. Since it is a public trial, anyone concerned can attend and observe. As for the private prosecution portion, there are still studies to be done due to extraterritoriality. After discussion among various legal experts, it was deemed more appropriate to request Du Yuesheng to mediate.

Compensation Issues

Regarding the request for compensation from the families of the victims, the lawyers hired by the relevant Ningbo, Chaozhou, Pudong, and Changzhou hometown associations are conducting a detailed investigation of the circumstances of the victims' families and the amount of funds needed for post-mortem care and support. After the collection is completed, the case will be submitted to the mediator, Du Yuesheng, for consultation with the French authorities. However, the exact amount is currently undetermined. The numbers circulating outside are all inaccurate.

Continuing the Meeting

The Shanghai Aid French Concession Tragedy United Association, to discuss the direction of negotiations, notified the committee members of seventeen groups yesterday that the third committee meeting will be held at 5:00 PM today, still on the fourth floor of the Ningbo Association on Xizang Road, to continue the proceedings based on the resolutions passed at the last general meeting.

Postponing the Petition

Regarding the recommendation of representatives to petition party and government organs, requesting serious negotiations with the French authorities, it was decided to temporarily postpone the negotiations because the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has instructed the municipal government to negotiate, and the compensation issue has also been entrusted to Du Yuesheng for negotiation.

Greyhound Association's Lawsuit Continues 103

| Jurors' Opinions Not Entirely the Same |

The Greyhound Association's lawsuit regarding the closure of the Xinfeng Mingyuan Greyhound Track continued its hearing yesterday at the British Assize Court. The part of the lawsuit concerning current Extra Chief Inspector of the Shanghai Municipal Council, Martin, was heard. After the plaintiff's lawyer presented his final arguments to the jurors, Judge Grain addressed the jurors, analyzing the circumstances of the case. The jurors then retired to the deliberation room at 11:50 AM to discuss the case. However, the five jurors' opinions were not entirely the same, and a decision had not been reached by 12:30 PM. Judge Grain clearly stated in his instructions that he believed the Shanghai Municipal Council's closure of this large gambling establishment, deemed to be obstructing the public, was within its power. The Council's power is to maintain good governance and good order within the International Settlement. Judge Grain's instructions stated that this case had taken up a lot of time for the jurors and himself. Under normal circumstances, there would not have been a lawsuit. The first issue in this case is whether the Shanghai Municipal Council has the power to close the greyhound track. There has been much dispute over this point, but there is little basis for determining the true power of the Shanghai Municipal Council. This undoubtedly falls under the jurisdiction of the Consular Court. This case is the plaintiff accusing the defendant Martin and the Shanghai Municipal Council of violating civil law, but no evidence has been presented. We must rely on common sense as the basis for our judgment regarding the power of the Shanghai Municipal Council. Grain then discussed the powers of the Shanghai Municipal Council as outlined in the Yangjingbang Regulations and the Council's bylaws, stating that the police have great power in managing traffic and can close roads. What the authorities did was send police to the road to prevent the public from entering Mingyuan, but there is no evidence to constitute the crime of trespassing on private land. He also stated that the Shanghai Municipal Council had notified the plaintiff that the sale of dog racing tickets was illegal and had given them some time to hesitate. At that time, there was some correspondence between the parties. The plaintiff could not stop dog racing due to a contract related to electricity supply, as if they wanted to ask the Shanghai Municipal Council to order them to stop. The Shanghai Municipal Council is responsible for maintaining good governance and order within the settlement and for preventing anything that obstructs the public, given that this large gambling business is opposed by the Chinese government, opposed by the Japanese Consul-General, and opposed by the British authorities. Based on all the evidence in this case, he felt unable to find that the Shanghai Municipal Council did not have the right to close the greyhound track. Judging by common sense, he felt that the Shanghai Municipal Council had the right to do what it did.

Married Women May Also Participate in Shanghai Queen Election 107

According to Mr. Duncan, Secretary of the Shanghai Queen Election Preparatory Committee, prominent Shanghai figures such as Mr. Li Ming, Sassoon, Da Lai, and others have joined as honorary patrons. Consequently, women in Shanghai have enthusiastically participated, submitting over four hundred photographs. It is said that due to the support of various philanthropists, the Committee has decided to relax the qualifications for participating women, extending the registration deadline. For the sake of convenience, aside from actresses, married women are also allowed to participate. The original number of finalists was eleven, but it has now been increased to twenty-six: thirteen Chinese women and eleven European and American women. Among these twenty-six, the one who sells the most tickets will be elected as the Shanghai Queen. A grand coronation ceremony will be held soon at a renowned dance hall, followed by a large-scale cinematic masquerade ball. All proceeds from ticket sales and other sources will be used for charitable purposes. The elected Queen will receive a free trip to Hollywood in the United States, a radio set, and various other gifts. Applicants should submit their photographs (6 or 8 inches), with their name, age, and occupation written on the back, to the Queen Election Department at the Feige Company, No. 98 Nanjing Road. Those without photographs can have them taken for free at the following photography studios: Shanshi Ti at No. 72 Nanjing Road, Shanfu at No. 106, Zhaofang at No. 647, Guangyi at No. 104 Jing'an Temple Road, and Datong at No. 242.

Reader's Consultation

Free Love and Forced Marriage 108

[Letter from Ms. Zhu, Ying, of this city]

Editor:

I am a lonely, weak woman with new ideas, living in an old-fashioned family and being forced [into marriage]. I am eighteen years old and have received a considerable education. I am very clear about the new wisdom of society. My father is a chief employee in a large merchant store of the propertied class, and his annual income is also considerable. He has a very gentle temperament, but he is a bit stubborn in his thinking. I am his only child from his first wife. He has not had any children since, and although my mother urged him to take a concubine, he always refused. Therefore, he loves me like a pearl in his palm. At the age of five, I was sent to elementary school. Because of my affinity for school, I was promoted to the second grade of junior high school, but now I have dropped out. Unfortunately, my beloved mother passed away from tuberculosis a year ago. I was very distressed at the time. Perhaps [being dead makes for an official father, don't forget begging for food]! However, my marriage problem was resolved early on. It was my late mother who made the decision. It was the [family] of a [person]. Since then, my father, because of the issue of descendants, married a young and beautiful maiden as his second wife. I was also happy to welcome her. At the beginning of my stepmother's marriage, things were still good, but gradually her temperament and personality changed completely, as if she had become a different person. Her treatment of me was also unfair. Coincidentally, near my old school, a certain student from a certain university often passed by my old school. He was a [youthful] young man. [After] [encountering] each other, because we were very compatible in [interests], it was as if we regretted meeting so late. From then on, we made mutual appointments on Sundays to visit parks and movie theaters. Over time, we developed a love that was difficult to break, and we had intimate relations. Feeling the spring breeze several times, I became pregnant. We made mutual promises to carry out a marriage revolution. His marriage was also decided by his parents, who betrothed him to a certain woman. For my sake, he is now trying to persuade his father. However, my stepmother has a nephew who is a fashionable young man. He often visits my home, and as the mistress of the house, I offer him a bit of hospitality. However, my stepmother often [spouts] words [alluding to], how [free] love should be, how men and women are equal, how her nephew is promising, etc. At first, I [resented] her for [doing this], but [unexpectedly], she [actually] betrothed me to her nephew. Because I already have a lover, I naturally refused with stern words. She [tried to persuade me], but from then on, we became alienated, and she even made false accusations to my father, gossiping about me in bed. My father, believing her words, began to mistreat me day and night. From then on, [communication was] [cut off]. Fortunately, due to my relationship with a certain student, my stepmother did not find out. We still exchanged love letters. Once, my stepmother intercepted them and showed the letters to my father, and I suffered physical pain as a result. He doesn't even know about the thing in my belly. My enemy-like fiancé sent me a letter asking me to marry him, and after opening it, I was of course ashamed and did not reply. A week later, my father and stepmother talked about preparing for the wedding. Hearing this news was heartbreaking. At this critical moment, I can't think of a solution. On the one hand, the wedding day is approaching. On the other hand, my pregnancy is gradually becoming apparent and is about to [be revealed]. Proposing a divorce is out of the question because the other party is a gentleman and my parents would not agree. Remaining in the original marriage would harm a certain student, and I have the secret of my pregnancy. Abortion poses a life-threatening risk, and I am also under the control of my parents, leaving me in a dilemma. The only option is suicide to fulfill my wishes. The above [situations] are all subject to legal constraints. I am a weak woman and have no [experience]. The situation is critical. Please, sir, provide a good solution, a proper method that is not restricted by current laws, so that I can [escape]. Fortunately, my family also reads your newspaper. Every day, I see that the difficult problems in the Reader's Consultation are properly instructed by you, benefiting [many people]. Regarding the reply, because my stepmother [is] [watchful] and it involves the issue of reputation, it is best to disclose it in the newspaper, otherwise, I am afraid things will get worse.

Answer: Madam, under the current social family and etiquette constraints, there is really no perfect solution to your problem. There is no choice but to (1) immediately claim illness, stay in the hospital, and firmly refuse to marry. This requires a determination to fight; (2) ask your lover, the university student, to simultaneously write home to resolutely cancel the engagement, and declare that he is already freely engaged to you in Shanghai, asking his family to acknowledge it. If the university student has this courage and determination, then the matter will be easy to handle. In any case, consensual love is unlikely to be strongly interfered with by the law. At most, your father will, based on your stepmother's words, drive you out. Then, as long as your lover does not abandon you, the two of you might as well live together. After you give birth, find some work to slowly move forward. The difficult thing is that you are both too inexperienced and did not know how to prevent pregnancy, so you have produced a third party. Your future may have fewer days of joy and more days of suffering. Moreover, for university students in Shanghai, we dare not say there are no good ones, but truly gentle and kind people who are not unfaithful are probably rare. This requires you to observe him carefully.

Results Announced for Recruitment of Copyists for Two Railways 110

Two people out of more than two thousand eight hundred and thirty people

Fifteen officially selected, twenty-two alternates

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration recently recruited 15 copyists to be assigned to various departments. Since the advertisement for recruitment was published, up to 2,832 people have applied (with about 300 more applications arriving after the deadline, which were not counted). The personnel department was assigned to carefully select the handwriting samples submitted by each applicant, selecting 300 people with the most beautiful handwriting. The deputy director of the general affairs office, the secretary, and the head of the document section then jointly selected the 50 people with the best handwriting and asked them to come to the bureau for an interview. March 8th was the date of the interview. After the applicants registered, a doctor examined their physical condition one by one. Only those who passed the physical examination were allowed to take the exam. After the examination was completed, the director of the bureau personally gave the exam question: [Discuss the professional ethics that civil servants should have], with 40 minutes allotted for the essay and 20 minutes for the calligraphy test. Once the time was up, all papers had to be submitted, regardless of whether they were completed. It is said that the essays and calligraphy of the candidates in this exam were all excellent, and even those who did not make it in the first round were not without talent. However, due to the limited number of places, only 15 particularly outstanding people were selected. It is also said that everything in this recruitment was transparent. All the candidates' handwriting and exam papers, whether accepted or not, were [numbered] and preserved. If those who were not selected felt wronged, they could [go] to inspect [the papers] to demonstrate fairness. Those who were selected will also have a three-month probationary period. If their character or work is unsatisfactory, they will be eliminated at any time. The names of those admitted are listed below. Fifteen officially selected: Shen [Name], Mao [Name], Lu Zonghai, Zhi [Name], He Shouqin, Jiang Sisi, Shao Xiyao, [Name] Zi [Name], Ding [Name] San, Zhou Renshan, Zhu Yu [Name], Song Qimin, Su Ji, Xu Zonggan, Hong [Name] Xian. Conviction of Robbers Who Stole Guns 112

Liu Peide, a Cantonese native and younger brother of special constable Liu Xiuzhen, is a graduate of St. Francis School and is 16 years old. On the morning of the 4th of this month at around 10 a.m., he stole the pistol issued to his brother by the police station and, along with the thugs Xu Fengbin and Zhang Jinhai from Tongzhou, went to the home of Zhang Jurong from Zhenjiang at No. 2118 Hai [Name] Road to extort money. Failing, they robbed a leather [item] worth 20 yuan, pawned it, and spent the money. The case was uncovered by detectives Yang Guangqing and Wang Runhe and detective Zhang Faxiang, who arrested Liu and the other two and brought them to the First Special District Court. Zhang Jinhai was found to be the instigator and a repeat offender. The verdict was awaited. The circumstances have already been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan of the Criminal Court sentenced Zhang Jinhai to seven years in prison and Liu Peide and Xu Fengbin to one year and six months in prison each. They were escorted away and taken into custody according to the law.

The company's main factory was destroyed in the January 28th Incident, and the printing business was suspended. After resuming operations, due to limited printing capacity at the time, only business cards were printed as usual, but various sectors urged the expansion of the printing scope with increasing urgency. The company has now established another printing factory to first restore the letterpress printing section. From typesetting and plate making to printing and binding, all have considerable equipment. All kinds of Chinese and Western books, newspapers, ledgers, receipts, business cards, invitations, Chinese and Western envelopes, advertising materials, stickers, etc. can be printed. Since resuming operations, the company has been printing business cards on time every day, without fail, creating an unprecedented example in the printing industry.
