Letters to the Editor 118

To the Esteemed Editor:

Having just read the item in the "Local News" column of your esteemed newspaper of the 8th, regarding the Fook digging ticket case appeal, I was exceedingly astonished. The actual facts of the case were already described in detail in the "Local News" column of a certain newspaper on the 7th, with the headline ("[Digging and Selling Graves] Chi Lin counter-sues, Fook falsely accuses, conspires to commit perjury, accuses of extortion"). I will now refute the content published in your esteemed newspaper again: (1) The land in question is an ancestral property of Chi Lin, and all notices have been delivered by the local bailiff for many years (there are notices that can be verified). Moreover, the contract is valid, how can it be falsely claimed that it was privately printed? If there were no notices, this should be the first point of refutation. (2) Since the land is Chi Lin's ancestral property, any sale would be a sale of ancestral property. How can others interfere? Furthermore, there is no evidence of a sale. This should be the second point of refutation. (3) Regarding the so-called Zhang Sheng-tien (Zhang Guo...), Chi Lin does not know him and has never met him. How could he have requested him to mediate? This should be the third point of refutation. (4) As for the fact of destroying and digging up graves, it has already been judged by the Shanghai Special District First Court in Criminal Judgment No. 316, so there is no need for further debate. This should be the fourth point of refutation. I secretly think that Fook, disregarding his own character and fabricating facts, is merely trying to achieve his extortionist goals. Now, fearing that outsiders will not understand the truth and may mistake the false for the genuine, I hereby submit this letter of refutation, humbly requesting your chief editor to publish this letter in the news column, which would be greatly appreciated. Respectfully yours, peace. To Mr. Chief Editor of the Local News Column, respectfully, Chi Chung-lin, March 9th.

To the Esteemed Editor: Yesterday, I read in your newspaper about a tragic accident at the First Bathhouse in Minhang, stating that the victim was rushed to the hospital but died due to "internal heat poisoning" and lack of effective medicine. This does not accord with the facts. Upon investigation, the deceased, Hui-sheng, sustained injuries and was immediately rushed to the hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, the injuries were too extensive, and his advanced age made it difficult for him to recover, even with good medicine. Fearing that this may affect the reputation of the hospital involved, we request a correction. Respectfully to the Editorial Department of the Local News of Shen Bao, First Bathhouse of Minhang, March 8th.

Weather Report 119

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Shandong coast will be partly cloudy with southwesterly to northwesterly winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and the East China Sea will be overcast with rain or heavy fog. Cyclones are imminent due to a passing low-pressure system moving east or east-northeast. Also, the temperature in Shanghai in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday reached a maximum of 45.3 degrees and a minimum of 38.3 degrees. On the same day last year, the maximum was 48.4 degrees and the minimum was 35.2 degrees.

Page 13

Essays

Scolding Tang is Not as Good as Scolding Ourselves 120

— Zhan Lu

Very polite to outsiders; endless internal strife. Shaw's humorous comment has come true again. Old Tang is very polite to outsiders; before the enemy arrives, he has already "politely yielded". The people of the whole country are furiously scolding Old Tang non-stop; is Old Tang afraid of being scolded? If he were afraid of being scolded, he wouldn't have shown you his bottom. You've already fallen for his big trick once, and you still want to get angry and scold him, wouldn't that make him laugh his jaw off? In the past, Chen Lin's proclamation to the Wu generals had a line: "His name is not worthy to sully the bamboo slips," we are afraid of soiling the ink, of course, we won't scold him. Any scolding must contain a kind of effect that stimulates the conscience of the one being scolded, but can we still move Old Tang's conscience? Therefore, for this Chairman Tang Yu-lin who declared "resistance to the end," we only have praise, no condemnation; praise him for what? Praise him for listening to the words of the humorous old man and practicing his great politeness to outsiders.

We don't scold Old Tang, but we should scold ourselves; we took Old Tang's solemn declaration too seriously; we believed too much in Old Tang's reports of vigorous resistance; as a result, we ate an empty soup dumpling from Old Tang. Old Tang is smart, we have all become fools, this is worth scolding ourselves for.

At this time of changing events, the generally ignorant and illiterate people still maintain their carefree attitude. We are again worthy of scolding ourselves! Why do we need to be literate? Why do we need to have knowledge? Why should we be so filled with righteous indignation when we receive the news of Chengde's fall? Su Dongpo said: "The beginning of life's worries is when one becomes literate." Why bother reading books? This is again worth scolding ourselves for.

Fellow Countrymen, No Need to Worry 121

— Zhou Jingxi

The news that has been coming in these past few days is truly terrible! Tang Yu-lin actually took his many concubines and ran away, leaving the land to the enemy. The people are all gnashing their teeth in hatred, unable to express their grief and indignation.

But wait, everyone, don't be too extreme. I advise the 400 million compatriots not to worry, and even less to be saddened. You should know that the loss of the Northeast, the fall of Shanhaiguan, and the presentation of Rehe to Japan were all marked on the world map by God long ago. Furthermore, alas! (Praise!) The few unprecedented and unsurpassed prophetic doctors in China, like Jiang Ziya, Zhuge Liang, Li Chunfeng, and Liu Bowen, couldn't bear to see later generations die of anxiety, and had already written special collections, hinting at these events to us. No matter what time or dynasty, the appearance of a world-shaking hero or a beauty who could topple a kingdom in times of chaos is all included; all that's needed is for everyone to carefully investigate!

In short, everything under heaven is predetermined, and human effort cannot change fate. Even if Japan swallows the whole of China, it is also predestined by heaven. Can humans force it?

However, if your wife is in Tianjin, or your son is in Beiping, and you're a little worried, then you can go to the Four Horses Road and buy a copy of the special collection mentioned above, take a close look at it, and then you'll have a clue as to what will happen to Tianjin and Beiping, the Yangtze River, and the Southwest. If you have a clue, you'll have a way to be at ease.

Alas! National destruction is predestined by heaven! Why bother shouting and fighting so hard, my compatriots!

Let's sing while drinking, how much is life? Spring has arrived, let us enjoy ourselves in time!

Big Pancake Movement 122

— Fei Ming

According to reports, the workers of Yenching University, in view of the shortage of food at the front lines, have spontaneously launched a big pancake movement. The pancakes are as big as woks, about two feet in diameter and three inches thick, each weighing about ten pounds. They are requesting people from all walks of life to imitate and donate them (see the Shen Bao education column). Big pancakes are a staple food in the north. Recently, after listening to the wonderful melodies of the storytelling drums, I realized that storytelling drums are truly wonderful folk literature. They are both better than Peking opera in terms of superficiality and not as obscure as Kun opera. The emotions and writing are vivid, the descriptions are satisfying, and the structure is well-organized. The art of landscape painting makes good use of reduplicative words, vividly capturing the quiet, soft, affectionate, miserable, and dark atmosphere. The "blood stained sleeves, fragrant lips cold, moonlight shines on palace shoes showing red" in the Long Ban Slope section can be placed in the prose of the Six Dynasties without any awkwardness.

Xiao Hei's songs are like the Yangtze River, flowing a thousand miles at a stretch, and are sometimes interspersed with exclamatory interjections. The sound of ripping silk startles the entire audience. Her voice is extremely beautiful and can convey emotions subtly and silently. In the blink of an eye, everyone understands her feelings of joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness, and they change their expressions and lean forward to listen.

Truly, the storytelling drums are not an easy task. Without a stage, they use scenery to enhance their art, and they also lack brocade costumes to enhance their color. With just one drum and one string, they wander in a confined space and try to captivate the audience with great magic. Aside from Xiao Hei, I have rarely seen such talent. When she raises her eyebrows, waves her sleeves, and sings at the top of her voice, she is boundless and sees no one else. She is one with her art, and her spirit is sent into the song. She is truly a heroine of our time and no longer just an ordinary drum girl. (Ti Gong)

As for food, in the South, "big pancakes" and "fried dough sticks" are considered sisters. But the big pancakes that we usually see, although called big, actually weigh no more than two or three pounds. Now, the big pancakes specially made by the workers of Yenching University have actually broken all big pancake records and weigh up to ten pounds. I don't know what to call them, so I'll call them "Big Big Pancakes." If we were to translate it into foreign languages, it should be: BiggestBigCake, right?

Recently, we have seen many national salvation movements in the country, such as the aviation salvation movement, tea dance salvation movement, domestic goods movement, flower country election movement, and the Guangdong jade face salvation movement. Truly, they are abundant and beautiful beyond description. However, I have not seen any that embody the meaning of proletarian salvation in the movement. If there are any, it probably started with the big pancake movement. Song for the Big Pancake Movement (regardless of old poetic rhyme):

Big pancake, big pancake, big big pancake, made with domestic wheat flour, two feet in diameter and weighing ten pounds, the best among big pancakes. The northern wind blows snow, the mountains are cold, the brave soldiers are fighting, hungry and cold, having this big pancake to fill their bellies, chewing and pouring out their hatred. Suddenly, it is reported that the enemy has captured the city of Rehe, and the commander-in-chief has fled without a trace. High officials have delicacies to eat, how could they be willing to eat big pancakes on the battlefield! The big pancake is given to brave soldiers, eat it and aim well with the gun. Comrades of the same big pancake, soldiers and workers hold hands tightly, let the rich stink with wine and meat, big pancakes and fried dough sticks are eternal! The proletariat knows hunger and cold, resisting the enemy starts with food.

Ghost Money 123

— Xu Xiaoting

The same colorful pieces of paper, some are real, some are fake, and there is also a kind of "ghost money" for use in the underworld. There are so many kinds of banknotes, we can't count them all at once, no matter what bank issued them. Counterfeit banknotes circulate into our hands without us knowing, and the impact we suffer is great. But in this society where education is not widespread and illiterate people fill the entire society, ghost money – paper used by ghosts – has a great impact on the average, foolish masses, especially the women in the countryside and farmers in our inland areas, who are not easily acquainted with banknotes. The losses they suffer from ghost money being confused with real money are truly not uncommon.

Chinese people are used to mystification. They don't vigorously do practical work in the real society, but they are very authentic in planning the economic problems of the ghosts in the illusory and strange underworld. In the past, the people burned paper money and silver ingots for their ancestors. Now there are paper silver dollars and banknotes issued by underworld banks. Their shape and color are no different from real ones. Paper silver dollars are light in weight, and we know at a glance that they are for ghost use. Underworld banknotes and real banknotes – the only difference is in the writing – do not distinguish between above and below. Illiterate friends are deceived and receive them in their hands, and they really can't tell the difference between real and fake.

The place where the underworld bank is established is in Java. The paper money it issues is of a non-convertible nature. This kind of paper money circulates in Chinese society, specifically for the silly guys who can't read to have fun. Speaking of which, there are so many kinds of money used by Chinese ghosts, no wonder some mischievous ghosts say that although the Chinese people are poor, the ancestors of the Chinese people are not poor. Alas! Due to the superstition of theocracy, things that are popular for a while are poisonous to society. Instead of watching this ghost money harm ignorant men and women, we might as well prohibit its issuance.

Long Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 124

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 1: Pushing Food with Earnest Hospitality, Inviting Poor Women, Remembering Entering the Gate, Generously Leaving, Possessing a Military Man's Valor

Old Miss had always been a Beijing girl who came and went freely, but now she was suddenly told that she was not allowed to leave the house, how could this be done. So on this day, the Jiang family kept a straight face, and Old Miss was embarrassed to go out. But the next morning, she still went to the Haihong Street to buy things. When she left the house, the Jiang family was thinking that it would be good if she came back quickly. Unexpectedly, her going out today was exactly the opposite of her mother's intentions. She had been gone for a long time and had not yet returned. The Jiang family became anxious and restless in the house, and ran to the gate to look around. After waiting for a long time, her own daughter had not returned, but a military officer rode a sorrel high horse and walked to the gate. This place was not far from the Xiyuan barracks, and there were soldiers coming and going every day, so a riding military officer passing by was not unusual, and she did not pay much attention to it. Unexpectedly, the tall sorrel horse stopped suddenly in front of her, and the officer got off the horse, holding a horse whip in his hand, and stood straight in front of the Jiang family. The Jiang family was caught off guard and startled, and holding the door, she took two steps back. The officer was not the kind of person she expected. The horse whip in his hand drooped down, and with that hand, he took off his hat and nodded at her with a smile, saying: Old lady, do you also live in this house? Seeing that he was very polite and did not have any rude habits, the Jiang family also put on a smile and replied: That's right, we live here. What are you looking for, sir? The officer smiled and said: I'm not looking for anyone. My name is Zhao Ziqiang, a company commander, currently stationed in the Xiyuan camp. My old man wants to bring a servant and move into the backyard. I've rented your backyard house, and we'll be neighbors from now on. Please take care of me if anything happens. As soon as the Jiang family heard that a military officer had rented the backyard, an unpleasant impression had already been left in her mind. Now seeing that Zhao Ziqiang was not the unreasonable type, she was halfway reconciled. She smiled and said: We are poor people, just a mother and daughter. We'll have to ask you to take care of us in everything. Zhao Ziqiang tied the horse to the stone pillar outside the gate and walked in, asking: Old lady, what is your honorable surname? The Jiang family smiled and said: Why are you calling me that? I don't deserve it; my surname is Yang. (7)

World Oddities

— Chu Yu

The Queen of England is Not Free 125

At the end of last year, the National Union of Women's Institutes in London held an exhibition, and the women of England all put out their own handicrafts to compete for novelty and beauty. Among them, there was a beautifully decorated shoebox. The Queen of England repeatedly attended the exhibition to view it, and she loved this shoebox very much, wanting to buy it at a high price. However, the items displayed in the exhibition were all not for sale, and it was never allowed for the exhibitors to sell them as an exception. The Queen tried every means to ask the exhibitor to intercede, but she could not get her permission. Later, the Women's Institute held several review meetings specifically for this matter. As a result, they could not force the exhibitor to sell it because of the Queen's fondness, and the Queen had no way to obtain the shoebox.

Exquisite Prison 126

The state of Pennsylvania in the United States has built an extremely luxurious prison in Roswell, with various facilities modeled after the best hotels. The exterior looks like a palace, and the construction cost as much as seven million dollars. The interior rooms are more beautifully decorated than high-end hotels, with sofas, lounge chairs, wardrobes, hot and cold water, etc., all complete. Outside there are also large living rooms, dining rooms, entertainment venues, reading rooms, libraries, and sports fields. Therefore, it is called a hotel-style prison. The intention is to allow prisoners to improve their minds in this exquisite prison. When they are released, they are treated the same as graduates from specialized schools. Therefore, many prisoners dare not commit crimes again after being released.

Inventor Colludes with the Enemy 127

A German technician recently invented a new type of gas mask that can prevent any kind of poison gas. He wanted to sell the exclusive rights to this newly invented gas mask to a domestic military supplies factory, but because he was not given preferential treatment, he was very unwilling. He then sold it to his enemy, France. French military officials saw this new type of gas mask and were willing to pay a huge amount of royalties. Later, this news was detected by the German military authorities, and they all regretted it.

Great War Babies of England 128

The British army uses a volunteer soldier system. Currently, most of the British army are Great War babies. What are Great War babies? It refers to infants who were born or breastfed during the European War era. We recall that it has been nineteen years since the Great War began in 1914. The children who were born at that time are now young people around twenty years old. Therefore, in the current British army, Great War babies account for about eighty-five percent.

Pearls from Nine Million Years Ago 129

There is a barbershop in London whose owner's ancestors were collectors. Among the antiques they collected, there were four pearls that were identified by British geologists as rare antiques from nine million years ago. Legend has it that these pearls were the treasures of an Irish tycoon. Experts have now made a detailed assessment of the special features of the pearls: first, the pearl shape is very small, less than one-tenth of an ordinary pearl. The inside and outside both have the same mother-of-pearl. From the outside, it belongs to a species of true pearl shell that has already become extinct in ancient times. These pearls have a history. At first, they were tribute from the Spanish allied countries to King Ayutle of Denagor. Later, they were passed down from the king to his descendants, but it is no longer possible to find out when they fell into the hands of the barbershop owner's ancestors. Therefore, its value is truly priceless.

Buttons on Dress Uniforms 130

Gentlemen, have you seen why there are two buttons on the back of the buttocks of a suit dress uniform? This is because in the past, when there were no trains, cars, or trams, people mostly traveled by horse. However, when riding on horseback, you should roll up the two lapels of your coat and fasten them with the buttons on the side of your buttocks, so that you can avoid various obstacles. Therefore, the buttons on the back of the buttocks of dress uniforms are still left over to this day.

Leningrad Holds Arctic Exhibition 132

(TASS Leningrad Dispatch) An Arctic exhibition is currently being held here. The exhibits are mostly documents collected by Arctic exploration teams, all of which are of historical value, such as the "New Voyages of Novaya Zemlya" by the famous Dutch explorer. This book is in Latin and was published in 1611. It has become a rare book in the world. There is also a copy of Laff's diary, which is rich in textual research materials. In addition, there is also a branch inserted into the soil of Spitsbergen, the remains of the Arctic traveler Louis.

Disaster Area Students' Free Tuition Has Restrictions 133

Ministry of Education Orders Provinces and Cities

(Nanjing, 9th dispatch) The Ministry of Education issued a circular to various provincial and city departments, stating that the previous order for free tuition for students in disaster areas was intended for specific facts that could be verified as evidence of suffering from disasters. Recently, it has been found that many students in various schools are using the current general disaster situation in various parts of our country as a basis. The county government prepares a letter of proof, and many county government officials add a unified annotation, which is generally forwarded, which is inconsistent with the original order. The original order should be explained separately, so that the various schools are aware of it, and announce it to the students, so that everyone is aware of it.

School Aircraft Donations Must Not Be Used for Other Purposes 134

Nanjing, 9th dispatch) Various schools in Beiping and Tianjin telegraphed the Ministry of Education, stating that Beiping and Tianjin are close to the war zone, and all sectors are actively raising funds to aid the front lines. Fearing that it would be too late, they proposed to allocate aircraft donations to provide assistance nearby. On the 9th, the Ministry of Education replied that the aircraft donation was designated by the Central Government for purchasing aircraft and could not be allocated for other purposes.

In the Soviet Union's First Five-Year Plan 135

Four-Year Compulsory Education System Has Been Completed

Literacy Rate Increased from 33% to 90%

Thousands of Universities, Industrial Schools, and Holiday Remedial Schools Added

(TASS Moscow Dispatch) When the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union held its third congress, Bubnov, the People's Commissar of Education, reported to the public on the progress of culture and education in the Soviet Union during the first five-year plan. According to him, during this period, the development of various cultural and educational undertakings in the Soviet Union has exceeded the plan's expectations. For example, according to the plan, the educational expenses were 762.8 million rubles, but as a result, 155 billion rubles have been spent in four years and three months. Among them, 703.2 million rubles were used to train cadres, 700.4 million rubles were used for mass education, and 146.3 million rubles were used for scientific and research work. In the national cultural and educational expenses, the expenditure used to train cadres has increased year by year. In 1928, this expenditure accounted for 30.6%, and in 1932, it increased to 50.6%. The gradual increase in cultural work expenses in various republics is sufficient to prove the improvement of the cultural standards of general "backward" ethnic groups. The following is a table showing the increase in cultural and educational expenses in various republics in four years (1928 to 1932) (taking 1928 as 100 points):

Percentage

Russian Republic 239

Belarus Republic 331

Uzbek Republic 426

Tajikistan Republic 696

Turkmenistan Republic 710

In the past four years, thousands of new schools, industrial schools, colleges, and holiday remedial schools have been added. At the beginning of 1933, there were 485,000 male and female students studying in universities and industrial schools, and 1.5 million students studying in holiday industrial remedial schools. In 1922, there were only 57,000 engineers and technicians with university education in the entire Soviet Union. In 1932, it had increased to 216,000. As for mass education, the Soviet Union has made significant progress in implementing compulsory primary education. According to the original plan, the deadline for completing the compulsory education system in the Ukrainian Republic was 1934, the Belarus Republic was 1935, the Transcaucasian Republic was 1936, the Russian Republic was 1937, and the Central Asian Republics were 1940. But according to the facts, the four-year compulsory education system has been completed in 1932, and the seven-year compulsory education system has also been implemented. Moreover, the Soviet Union has achieved exceptional success in eliminating illiteracy. According to the first five-year plan, eliminating illiteracy could reach 17 million people, but in four years and three months, 29 million illiterate people became literate, and 17.7 million semi-literate people received supplementary education. In 1913, the literacy rate in the entire Russia was 35%. In 1932, it increased to 90%. Other "backward" ethnic groups also had the same increase in literacy. During the same period, the literacy rate in Uzbekistan increased from 2% to 72%, in Tajikistan from 1.5% to 52%, and in Turkmenistan from 2% to 61%. Also, according to the original plan, by the end of the five-year plan, the number of children entering kindergartens and "children's homes" could reach 900,000, but the actual number has now reached 5.2 million.

Educational Institutions in Jiangsu Province Promote Livelihood Education (Part 2) 136

丨Jiangsu Education Department Issues Concrete Plans for County Governments to Implement丨

B. For specially contracted farmland, the selection of seeds, fertilization, planting, use of agricultural tools, and pest control must all be carried out according to the guidance of the various institutions. The required seeds must also be selected and supplied by the institutions.

C. The establishment of specially contracted farmland should strive for distribution throughout the district and be clearly marked as such.

D. If a specially contracted farmland, due to special circumstances, fails to achieve the originally planned harvest results, resulting in losses for the landowner, the institution may provide an appropriate subsidy.

E. If a specially contracted farmland achieves excellent results, the landowner should be given appropriate rewards.

F. If a specially contracted farmland has achieved considerable success, the contract may be appropriately terminated, and other farmland may be contracted as specially contracted farmland.

3. In addition to establishing model farms and specially contracted farms, if county-level farmers' education centers have larger-scale farmland, they should also designate experimental farmland. The regulations for this are as follows:

A. Divide the experimental farmland into several zones, each zone measuring three to five mu.

B. Distribute the experimental farmland in each zone to farmers in the district for trial cultivation, with each household cultivating one zone.

C. When experimental farmland is given to the public for trial cultivation, no land price or any fees shall be charged. The institutions shall select and lend seeds, and the cultivators shall provide fertilizers, agricultural tools, and labor themselves.

D. All farming methods used during the trial cultivation of experimental farmland must be guided by the staff of the institutions. Otherwise, the qualification for trial cultivation will be revoked.

E. The agricultural products harvested from the experimental farmland, after repaying the original amount of seeds, shall belong to the cultivator.

F. The trial cultivation period is set for one year (extendable by one year in special circumstances). Upon expiration, the institution shall reclaim the land and allocate it to other farmers in the district for trial cultivation.

G. Farmers who have cultivated experimental farmland must continue to manage their private farmland according to the farming methods guided by the institutions and bear the responsibility of encouraging other farmers to imitate them.

H. Each institution must establish a rural improvement association. All farmers who cultivate experimental farmland must join the association as members to facilitate the implementation of various educational programs.

4. County-level farmers' education centers must convene all farmers in the district (at least one person per household) to organize the following associations:

A. Agricultural Improvement Association: Discusses various agricultural improvement matters.

B. Agricultural Study Group: During the agricultural off-season, studies general agricultural knowledge.

C. Agricultural Communication Agency: Transmits and reports various news related to agriculture, as well as agricultural improvement or relief methods.

5. County-level farmers' education centers must hold the following competitions or exhibitions on a regular or irregular basis:

A. Agricultural Tools and Crop Exhibition: A mobile exhibition must be held at least once a year, and all farmers in the district must participate with their products.

B. Plowing Cattle Competition: Must be held at least once every two years, and all plowing cattle in the district must participate. However, it may be held by village or district.

6. If more than two-thirds of the population in the social education district under the jurisdiction of the county-level public education center are farmers, agricultural guidance must be carried out in accordance with the above five regulations.

5. Promoting Subsidiary Occupations

1. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers must earnestly promote and provide guidance on subsidiary occupations for the public.

2. Every urban household must have at least one type of subsidiary occupation, such as household handicrafts, women's handicrafts, etc.

3. Rural farmers must make a living by raising livestock, chickens, pigs, fish, bees, and various handicrafts as subsidiary occupations, and must engage in at least one type.

4. In order to promote subsidiary occupations and for the sake of convenience, county-level public education centers and farmers' education centers must, in addition to establishing special training classes when necessary, also send personnel to conduct door-to-door guidance within the district.

5. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers must have accurate statistics and reports on the types of subsidiary occupations, the distribution of subsidiary occupations, and the exact annual income of each household for the public and farmers in the district, and submit them to the county government or education bureau for transmission to the education department for record.

6. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers may, when necessary, hold exhibitions of by-products, competitions of by-products, and sales offices of by-products. The methods for this shall be determined by each institution.

6. Promoting Cooperation and Savings

1. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers must earnestly promote credit cooperation, consumer cooperation, production cooperation, and marketing cooperation.

2. When county-level public education centers and farmers' education centers guide the public to organize cooperatives, they must submit the plan to the county government or education bureau for transmission to the education department for approval, and also report it to the competent authority for cooperatives for record.

3. In order to alleviate the economic difficulties of the public, county-level public education centers and farmers' education centers may establish public loan offices, farmers' warehouses, etc. before credit cooperatives are established. The methods for this shall be determined by each institution and submitted to the county government or education bureau for report to the education department for record.

4. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers must earnestly promote savings among the public.

5. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers must earnestly promote thrift and economy, organize frugality associations by village, and strongly encourage each household to participate.

7. Other Livelihood-Related Undertakings

1. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers must develop detailed plans to promote domestic goods and promote local products, implement them in stages, and hold regular exhibitions of domestic goods, introductions of domestic goods, and surveys and statistics of daily necessities for the public, striving to ensure that the public in the district uniformly use domestic goods within three years.

2. For livelihood-related work such as afforestation, dike construction, and river dredging, county-level public education centers and farmers' education centers must collaborate with local authorities through their livelihood education design committees to design and implement the projects.

3. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers shall provide assistance and guidance to private or charitable organizations that run handicraft factories and vocational training centers within the district. Those who achieve outstanding results may be recommended for awards.

4. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers may organize other livelihood-related undertakings as needed by the community.

8. Guidance and Assessment Methods

1. The provincial-level public education center and farmers' education center must earnestly provide guidance to county-level public education centers and farmers' education centers in promoting livelihood education. The work regulations are as follows:

A. Send personnel to conduct inspections and surveys of the implementation of livelihood education in various counties and provide guidance.

B. Produce and collect materials and supplies related to the implementation of livelihood education and distribute or lend them to various counties for application whenever possible. When necessary, they may also be sold at the original price.

C. Guide various counties to formulate concrete methods for implementing livelihood education.

2. County governments or education bureaus must be responsible for supervising and strictly assessing the implementation of livelihood education by county-level public education centers. The important work regulations are as follows:

A. Send personnel monthly to inspect the progress of each institution in promoting livelihood education and provide guidance at any time.

B. At the end of each year, compile a report on the assessment of livelihood education implemented by each institution and submit it to the education department for record.

C. Provide strong assistance when institutions encounter difficulties in promoting livelihood education.

3. The education department may send personnel at any time to conduct random checks or secret investigations on the implementation of livelihood education by county-level public education centers and farmers' education centers. The main points of the investigation are as follows:

A. The actual situation of each institution in carrying out livelihood education.

B. The situation of county magistrates or education bureau directors in supervising and assessing livelihood education.

C. The situation of the provincial-level public education center and farmers' education center in guiding the implementation of livelihood education in various counties.

4. Those county-level public education centers and farmers' education centers that achieve outstanding results in promoting livelihood education shall be rewarded. Those who perform poorly shall be punished. The rewards and punishments shall be determined by the county government or education bureau in accordance with the Regulations for the Assessment of Chief Personnel of Social Education Institutions in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province and submitted to the education department for approval and implementation.

9. Supplementary Provisions

1. County-level public education centers and farmers' education centers must implement each item in accordance with the regulations of this plan, unless there are special circumstances that have been submitted to the education department for approval.

2. County governments or education bureaus must formulate detailed implementation rules separately when implementing this plan and submit them to the education department for record.

3. This plan is formulated by the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department and submitted to the provincial government for promulgation and implementation. (To be continued)

Local News

### The Process of the European Education Inspection Group's Investigation (1) 137

Yang Lian and Guo Youshou Arrive in Shanghai; Remaining Members Expected to Return in Early April

European Education Has Many Advantages That China Can Learn From

### The Return Journey of Group Members 138

The European Education Inspection Group, since being commissioned by the government to go to Europe to carry out its work in August of last year, has now been working for seven months. The situation of its investigation in various countries has been reported in various newspapers. The group completed its investigation in Soviet Russia in mid-February and telegraphed the Ministry of Education to report the end of the European investigation. It immediately received an order from the Ministry to return home immediately. Group members Yang Kang and Guo Youshou took the Siberian Railway from Moscow, took a train through Vladivostok to return home. The remaining group members, Cheng Qibao and Li Ximou, went from Moscow to Geneva to wait for a boat back home. Li Jiaxiang went from Moscow to Vienna and Berlin, then took a boat from Hamburg to return home. The group still had a lot of materials and luggage stored in Vienna, Berlin, Paris, and Geneva, so they went to retrieve them separately. The two of Yang and Guo, due to domestic official duties, (Mr. Yang is a professor at Peking University, and Mr. Guo is a section chief in the Ministry of Education,) had to take the quickest route to avoid a long absence from their posts. Mr. Guo and Mr. Yang arrived in Shanghai yesterday (the 9th) on the same ship as Chiang Tso-pin, the President Cleveland. A reporter from the Da Bai News Agency immediately went to interview them. The two looked refreshed but extremely exhausted, as they had just completed seven months of work, followed by more than twenty days of trains and ships. Their hardship was extraordinary. The two will soon return to Beijing to report on their mission. The reporter from the Da Bai News Agency exchanged a few words of greeting with Mr. Yang and Mr. Guo and then raised the following questions, to which they gave detailed answers. They are recorded as follows:

### Weaknesses of Our Country's Education 139

Question: What is the mission and organization of the European Education Inspection Group?

Answer: Since the Qing Dynasty changed the school system and implemented the new education, it has been more than thirty years, which can be said to be not short. Although educational achievements have gradually increased, they have not been very significant and cannot meet the expectations of those who are enthusiastic about education. Most educators blame the poor school system. Although it has been changed many times, it is still ineffective. Some say that the teaching method is improper. Therefore, the five-stage teaching method, the heuristic teaching method, the design teaching method, and the Dalton teaching method, all the new teaching methods created in Europe and the United States have been introduced one after another. However, the educational achievements are still not obvious. Some people think that outsiders see more clearly, so it is better to invite foreign educators to China to inspect and listen to their opinions for reference. Therefore, Dr. John Dewey, Dr. Paul Monroe, Dr. Romiett Stevens, Dr. Elwood P. Cubberley, and so on from the United States came to China one after another, and we benefited a lot. However, fewer European educators have come to China to inspect education, and they have few concrete opinions on the construction of our country's education that can be used for our reference. Moreover, there are many students studying education in the United States, and few studying education in European countries. Therefore, the Chinese people are clearer about the American education system and its advantages than about the situation of European education.

### Group Member Organization Mission 140

Studying the advantages of European and American education and listening to the concrete criticisms of European and American educators on our country's education are equally important in improving our country's education. Therefore, the government authorities have long intended to send experts to Europe to investigate education and to invite European educators to China to inspect education. In the second half of the year before last, the League of Nations sent Mr. Becker, the former Prussian Minister of Education, Mr. Paul Hazard, a professor at the French National Academy, Mr. R.H. Tawney, a professor at the University of London, and Mr. Wazyk, an educational expert from the Polish Ministry of Education, to China to inspect education. Zhu Jiaji, the Minister of Education of our country, also began to select personnel to organize the European Education Inspection Group. Initially, Cheng Qibao, Yang Kang, Li Ximou, Guo Youshou, and Hang Liwu were appointed. Later, Mr. Hang could not spare the time due to other matters, so Li Jiaxiang was appointed instead. After the five of us were appointed, we gathered in Nanjing to prepare our luggage and ask the Ministry of Education to indicate the scope of the investigation and the points that should be paid special attention to. At the same time, we also sought the expectations of domestic educators for our mission. We held two meetings at the Ministry of Education and received much guidance from the Vice Minister and others. We discussed with educators in Beijing, Shanghai, Hangzhou, Jinan, and other places and obtained many opinions. However, the time between being appointed and departing was very short, so we could not listen to the opinions of domestic educators as much as we hoped, which is regrettable. In total, the most important aspects of the expectations of all parties for our mission are five points:

1. Investigate the educational system and current situation of each country.

2. Seek foreign reference materials for Chinese education problems in order to make it easier to solve them.

3. Seek to connect the Chinese education community with the education communities of European countries in order to obtain mutual benefits in academic research and enhance international friendship.

4. Collect materials for educational research.

5. Pay attention to the trends of new education in various countries.

Among these five items, the second item is the most important. Because of the burning educational situation in our country, there are many problems that are difficult to solve. Therefore, all parties submitted hundreds of questions to us. We made consistent efforts to search for and study the above five points and other points that should be paid attention to. However, in order to concentrate our efforts, we divided the work vertically. Guo Youshou paid special attention to higher education, Yang Lian paid special attention to secondary education, Cheng Qibao paid special attention to elementary education, Li Ximou paid special attention to vocational education, and Li Jiaxiang paid special attention to social education and educational administration. The five were jointly responsible. Teacher training was jointly undertaken by Yang Lian and Cheng Qibao. (End)

### Guo Jian, Leader of the Fudan Volunteer Army, Goes North to Resist Japan 141

Guo Jian, the leader of the Fudan University Student Volunteer Army in Jiangwan, was heartbroken by the loss of Chengde. He pawned all his clothes, took a boat to Tianjin, and then went to the front line to resist Japan. He went north yesterday afternoon. His classmates knew nothing about it beforehand. Only a few classmates were present to see him off. They were reluctant to part, and the whole scene was filled with a tragic atmosphere, which moved the viewers. Guo's courtesy name is Ziyuan. He is from Huaiyuan, Anhui. He is only twenty-seven years old. During the January 28 Incident, he led the Fudan Student Volunteer Army to the front line to resist the violent Japanese and served as an instructor in the training class of the 19th Route Army. He is brave and very responsible. His going north to resist the enemy this time will greatly serve our country.

### Zheng Yuxiu, President of Shanghai Political Science and Law College, Resigns Due to Illness 144

Zhang Zhongdao Elected as Acting President

Dr. Zheng Yuxiu, president of the Jin Shenfu Road Political Science and Law College, resigned from her position as the president of the college and needed to travel to a tropical region for medical treatment of her brain illness. She departed for Manila last month and is currently resting there. Fearing that she would be unable to attend to school affairs from afar, and in danger of making mistakes, she telegraphed the college's board of directors, firmly resigning from her position. After receiving the telegram, the board understood Zheng's plight and allowed her to rest temporarily and elected Zhang Zhongdao as acting president. A report was made to the entire student body at 11 a.m. on the 9th of this month in the college's auditorium. More than 700 people attended. Zhang Zhongdao, the acting president, presided over the meeting. After performing the ceremony, he read Zheng's telegram and reported the board's intentions. He then reported Zheng's various plans for the college's improvement and said he would continue to work hard to realize them in the future. At the end, he exhorted the students to abide by discipline and study hard. Next, Zhang Junmin, the college's chief of general affairs, gave a speech, recounting Zheng's hard work and achievements in maintaining and improving the college over the years. He said that all students were very sorry to hear that she had resigned due to illness and wanted to retain her unanimously. However, Zheng's intention to resign was firm, and he hoped that the students would love Zhang in the spirit of loving Zheng and that all teachers and students would cooperate to develop the school. It is reported that the students of the college were very reluctant to hear the news of Zheng's resignation due to illness. Zhang, the new president, has served in the college for many years and has always been loved by the students. Now that the board of directors has elected him as acting president, the general students are satisfied.

Organized by the Municipal Education Hall

Registration Begins Immediately

The Shanghai Municipal Public Education Hall, in order to promote children's education and enhance children's health, will hold children's jianzi and ping pong competitions on Children's Day. All preparations are underway, and registration begins immediately. The following rules have been established:

Jianzi Competition 1. Eligibility: All children in this city are eligible to participate in the competition. 2. Competition Date: April 6th, morning. 3. Number of Participants: 40. 4. Competition Location: The hall's auditorium. 5. Competition Rules: (1) The children's jianzi competition is tentatively limited to the three types designated by the hall: [ ], [jump], [ ]. Players must obey the kicking rules. (2) Small tricks must pass the face, and large tricks must pass the top of the head. (3) Latecomers at roll call may only join after the entire competition is completed; those who do not arrive will be considered to have forfeited. (4) No obstructing the competitors. (5) No shouting loudly. (6) Compete according to the number, without rushing ahead or lagging behind. (7) If the competition is illegal or irregular, the judges may stop it with a whistle. (8) Anyone who does not obey the referee's instructions may be ordered to withdraw. (9) No substitutions are allowed during the competition. 6. Competition Equipment: Provided by the hall (own equipment cannot be used). 7. Referees: Appointed by the hall. 8. Awards: The top three participants will be selected based on average scores, and the hall will award prizes accordingly. 9. Registration Dates: From now until April 1st, from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM daily. 10. Registration Location: The hall's office.

Ping Pong Competition 1. Eligibility: All children in this city are eligible to participate in the competition. 2. Competition Date: April 5th, starting at 9:00 AM. 3. Number of Participants: 40. 4. Grouping: The hall staff will be responsible for grouping participants during roll call, with two participants per group, for a total of twenty groups. 5. Competition Location: The hall's auditorium. 6. Competition Rules: A. Players who do not arrive on time or cannot continue the competition will be considered to have forfeited. B. Players must absolutely obey the referee's orders. 7. Equipment: Provided by the hall (bats may be brought by the participants themselves, but the size must comply with ping pong rules). 8. Referees: Appointed by the hall. 9. Awards: The top one, two, and three participants will be selected through elimination and round-robin systems, and the hall will award prizes accordingly. 10. Registration Dates: From now until April 1st, from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM daily. 11. Registration Location: The hall's office.

Page 16

Free Talk

Why [Liberation]! 191

— Xuan

These days, the Free Talk is debating Mr. Zeng's so-called [liberated words], which is very lively. I have not read that [Special Issue on the Liberation Movement of Words], but I have only seen the two poems quoted by various authors in the Free Talk, Mr. Zeng's [immortal works]. There are many wonderful things in the world that are [beyond expectation]. For example, a few years ago, a gentleman [discovered] that Mozi was an Indian, and made many [researches] as if it were a serious matter. And now there is Mr. Zeng's [Movement for the Liberation of Words], which is an even more advanced way of selling savages' heads.

Mr. Zeng's [immortal works] have been criticized by many gentlemen, so I will not elaborate on them here. Let's talk about what liberation is.

Generally speaking, a kind of [liberation movement] in literature and art does not arise out of thin air. First of all, there must be a conflict between old and new ideas in society. When new ideas need to be expressed in a literary and artistic way, it is felt that the old literary and artistic system is not applicable, so a new style is created. In this way, when new content produces a new form, it can be regarded as a kind of [liberation] in literature and art.

The current vernacular poetry, in relation to the old-style poetry, is a kind of liberation; because the two are not only different in form, but also completely different in the ideas and consciousness contained in them. But there are exceptions to this. Recently, many vernacular poems are actually the adopted sons of feudal thought in terms of ideological consciousness, from the groaning of poverty and resentment to the new love descriptions of talented scholars and beautiful women, all of which are the thin shadows of feudal poets; although they are ostensibly vernacular poems, selling old goods in new stores, the difference between this kind of vernacular poetry and old-style poetry is just like the difference between ancient style and rhythm in old-style poetry. Mr. Zeng's many vernacular poems are actually such adopted sons of old-style poetry. Therefore, it is a more honest way for him to fill in new words for [playing mahjong] completely according to the old rhythm of words. It is enough to remove the savage head of what [liberation] is! Wouldn't that save a lot of talk? And don't you see that another new word artist, Mr. Zhang, has already taken over the mantle of Nalan Xingde and become [immortal] without wearing the savage head of [liberation]?

Stupid Thief 192

— Jianfu

In today's smoky literary world, many people who are close to printing houses publish their books in large numbers. Although they can cheat a few coins, [play mahjong,] they cause no small harm to a group of pure young people. If this kind of automatic kaleidoscope is not exposed, the Chinese people may only sing [the peace of the false country] forever.

Since publications such as Free Talk and Analects exposed the truth about Mr. Zhang and Mr. Zeng, we have at least recognized what modern [white depiction masters] and [liberation experts] are. Mr. Zhang not only stole the entire song Lang Taosha from Nalan Xingde, but also the fourth sentence of his representative work, the first song of Yulouchun, [The most unbearable thing is to look back in the bright moon], is still stolen from the sentence [The old country is unbearable to look back in the bright moon] by the late lord. Changing the two words [old country] to [most is] is not something that any petty thief of a word artist can do, but unexpectedly it has become Mr. Zhang's swan song. This kind of [orthodox faction] is like the disciple of Liangshanbo Shiqian. If this kind of [white depiction master] is not called [word thief], what should he be called?

Mr. Zhang uses the [Huizhou] accent for the level tones of the words, but unfortunately, his master Hu Shi's Huizhou accent is different from his. We must first learn the [Huizhou] accent from Mr. Zhang to be able to read the first two sentences of his Yulouchun [The misty morning smoke shrouds the green trees, children lead calves to the stream] and the first sentence of his Bodhisattva Man [The man is floating clouds and I am catkins] smoothly. No wonder Liu Yazi scolded him [spreading errors, harming young people].

The liberation theory of the liberation master, Mr. Zeng, is even more ridiculous. He said:

(1) A word must have a score, otherwise it is no different from a poem, because a word has a musical relationship, so

(2) A word must pay attention to level tones; but there is no need to talk about yangping yinping, regardless of shang qu ru.

(3) Word sentences should be completely white depiction, or close to vernacular simple classical Chinese, and absolutely no allusions or deep and outdated classical Chinese should be used, which is (1) no liberation, (2) half liberation, (3) full liberation.

This is his [one-third five] liberation. Although we do not know how (1) no liberation and (3) full liberation can be consistent, we must use scores, have level tones, and use white depiction. In fact, it is the old technique of the Tang and Five Dynasties words, even later Dongpo and Jiaxuan are the same. When Dongpo wrote words, he sometimes changed the length of the sentences at will. In ancient times, words were a kind of popular literature. The works of the word artists of the Tang and Five Dynasties and the word saint Li Houzhu were basically white depiction. There was no need to use allusions and deep and outdated classical Chinese at all. Therefore, there is no need for the liberation of modern people. Zhang Mi's Jiangchengzi [It's good to ask him if he came, and smiled and said, don't be sentimental], Song Li Qingzhao's Ru Meng Ling [Who accompanies me to sit alone by the bright window, I and the shadow are two, when the lamp is exhausted and I want to sleep, the shadow also throws people away, helpless, helpless, what a desolate me]. Isn't this vernacular? The Yinshici and Cimaoci of Qing Nalan Xingde, and the Hualianci of Wu Pingxiang, are all excellent works. Who used allusions? Who used deep and outdated classical Chinese? Words were originally vernacular. [Wherever there is well water to drink, someone will sing Willow words]. If it is classical Chinese, how can these water carriers and villagers standing by the well drinking water understand and sing them? Only the declining word artists after the Southern Song Dynasty liked to use allusions, but this is already an inferior work. People who truly understand and love words in ancient and modern times all respect the words before the Southern Song Dynasty. Later generations abandoned the fundamentals and pursued the trivial, leaving only laughter, so the three major propositions put forward by Mr. Zeng are originally the origin of words. Why bother to do this after thousands of years? Mr. Zeng's liberation theory is not a theory at all, let alone a movement.

Mr. Zeng was originally an ignorant and incompetent thing, a petty thief like Mr. Zhang. His most proud masterpiece, and praised by the ignorant as [soul-stirring] [immortal masterpiece], Zuihuayin:

[I am too weak to relieve the long day in illness, and my loneliness is as before. I go to the flower shade alone, and I only feel the fragrance filling my sleeves in the midst of myriad purples and reds. The flowers accompany me after dusk, and my heart is first revealed when I am drunk. How can I not be bewitched, such spring light is only suitable for Jiangnan to have.]

It was copied from Li Qingzhao's Zuihuayin. How can he still have the face to publish it! Those who are good at being thieves always make it difficult for people to discover their stolen goods, but Mr. Zhang and Mr. Zeng stole other people's land to be their family gods, which is too stupid to be pitied.

Originally, Mr. Zeng wanted to continue [Hu Shi's attempt to succeed], but unfortunately, the immortal famous sentence [What does he care] can only be thrown into the toilet, rotting with excrement!

Finally, I want to advise a group of young people, if you are interested in words, you can buy Tang Wudai words, Bei Song Zhujia words, and Qing Nalan Xingde's words to read, but you must never buy the words [released] by those [word thieves] who boast about themselves, otherwise, you will be greatly deceived!

The Woman Selling Egg Slices 193

— Wang Wanrong

I have liked to eat egg slices since I was a child. They are yellow, fragrant, sweet, and crispy, which is really delicious! Every day at about two o'clock in the afternoon, there is a cry for selling egg slices in the alley: [A yao xi dan pian···A yao ji dan pian···] The tone is long, loud and clear. When I heard this cry approaching, I would stick my head out of the upstairs window and shout, [Hey, please wait a moment!] Then the Jiangbei girl selling egg slices stopped there, looked up, and revealed a plump round face under a snow-white headscarf; two bright, smiling eyes flashed in front of me. I would send a small basket from the window with a rope, and the Jiangbei girl would take two copper coins from the basket and put two slices of egg slices in it. Gradually, I got used to it. Every day when I heard the clock on the table strike twice, I would think of that girl. As long as I heard her calling from afar as she walked into the alley, I would put down what I was playing with or eating and wait at the window for her; she didn't need me to greet her anymore. When she walked past my house downstairs, she would take two slices of egg slices, look up, and wait for me to lower the small basket. I would chew the egg slices while watching her carry the basket, lift her two thin little feet, and drag her long cry out of the alley.

In recent years, all the time has been spent in a foreign land, and that girl and the sweet and delicious egg slices have gradually been forgotten.

Last year, I went home for winter vacation. One afternoon, I was lazily lying in a chair reading a novel. The sun shone on me, making me a little tired; the big tabby cat lying on the threshold was also dozing off lazily. The wintersweet on the table was exuding a faint fragrance.

From afar came the cry for selling egg slices again, the tone was sad and hoarse. I seemed to recall something, and pushed open the window foolishly. The scissor-like north wind rushed towards my face. I plucked up the courage and stretched out my neck to look down. The head that was raised up upon hearing the sound of the window was still wrapped in a white headscarf, but under the headscarf was the face of a middle-aged woman who already had wrinkles and looked haggard and thin. Those two eyes emitted a melancholy light, as if she also recalled something, and looked at me foolishly for a while. Then she dragged her sad and weak cry and walked out of the alley. I still suspect that this haggard woman is the plump girl of a few years ago.

Similarly, this woman selling egg slices may also be suspecting that this dignified girl is the little girl with braids who used to lie at the window to buy egg slices every day a few years ago!

Anatole France and Antiques 194

— Shen Qiyu

People often say that Anatole France and George Bernard Shaw can be called the two jewels of European literature, because both are good at [humor]. Among them, George Bernard Shaw's longevity is really good. At the age of seventy-seven, he can still be [old and not die], and he can still come to China to be humorous, and he can still be humorous about the [southward migration of antiques].

However, George Bernard Shaw's humor about the southward migration of antiques is nothing more than saying things like [antiques are more important than the lives of millions of people in Peiping] (see his remarks in Shen Bao). Chinese people have already said such words, so from the perspective of the humorist George Bernard Shaw, it does not seem to have much humorous meaning.

As for Anatole France, who spent his life in ancient books, antiques, ancient ..., unfortunately, he also [became ancient] a few years ago and could not come to China in person, so we have no way to hear his opinion on the southward migration of antiques. But he once wrote the following satire on the Arabs:

[The Arabs who use marble from the Palmyra temple to build a small house are more like philosophers than all the custodians of the museums in London, Paris, Munich, etc.]

Isn't this already Anatole France's indirect satire on the southward migration of antiques!

Imperialists often regard the Chinese as Arabs; since Arabs can use antiques to build small houses for themselves, why can't we use antiques? Instead of doing it secretly in Peiping, why not move it to the concession and use it happily?

In this way, amidst the opposition of the majority, antiques finally entered the concession a few days ago, and we became [very similar] to the Arabs.

The Black Woman's Quest for God (23) 195

— George Bernard Shaw, translated by Yi Xian

[I am not seeking happiness; I am seeking God,] said the black girl.

[Have you not found him yet?] said the magician.

[I have found many gods,] said the black girl. [Everyone I have come to has introduced one to me; even this image maker has a shop full of gods. But in my eyes, they are all half-dead, except for a few beast-shaped ones, like the half-goat, half-man one on the first shelf blowing a flute. That one is very natural-looking; because although I also want to be a goddess, I myself am half-goat, half-woman. Why are none of them half-woman?]

[What about pursuing this one?] said the image maker, pointing to Venus.

[Why are good bodies covered in clothes?] said the black girl. [She is neither a goddess nor a woman; half of her body is shy, and the other half is what white people call a lady. She looks like a lady, and she is beautiful, and the white governor would like her to be the head of his house; but I think she has no conscience; that makes her inhuman and ungodly. I don't need her.]

[The Way (Note) must be made with flesh and blood; white stone will not do,] said the guard. [You must not be disgusted because these gods have human bodies. If they did not bring out human forms for you, then how could you have anything in common with them? To have a link between divinity and humanity, some gods must become human.]

(Note) [The Way is God] (See the Gospel of John)

[Some women may as well become gods,] said the black girl. [That would be much better, because a god who descends to become a man is demeaning himself; a woman who becomes a god raises herself.]

[God is the refuge of all bothersome women,] (Note) said the Arab. [This is the most bothersome woman I have ever met. Making women beautiful and also bothersome is one of God's mysterious methods. The more satisfying reason he gives them, the more dissatisfied they become; this person is dissatisfied even with the very dignified and powerful God himself. Oh, young lady, if the glorious and great God cannot please you, what god or goddess can please you?]

(Note) See the Old Testament

[There is a goddess I have heard of that I want to know more about,] said the black girl. [Her name is called Maat; I feel she has something here that no other god can give us.]

China and Russia have close relations in geography, history, and politics. Guo Taiqi's Remarks 220

Japan's Ambitions Towards Us Have Not Ceased

Strengthening China's Determination to Resist Japan

(London) Guo Taiqi, the Chinese representative to the League of Nations and Minister to the United Kingdom, returned here yesterday from Geneva. This afternoon, a reporter from this agency visited him. Minister Guo said: "There is no such thing as direct negotiations between China and Japan, because they are contrary to the policy China holds, and Japan has now occupied Rehe and its ambitions have not ceased. Its intention is to conquer all of China and dominate Asia. Therefore, direct negotiations at this time are also useless. Chinese public opinion is extremely angry. Although Rehe has been lost, it must be restored. This can be predicted. Although there is no official news to confirm the death of Tang Yulin and the resignation of Zhang Xueliang, the military resistance against Japan will definitely be personally directed by Chiang Kai-shek from now on, and the people of the whole country will support him with one heart and one mind. Although Guangzhou and Nanjing had slightly different opinions on politics in the past, they have now abandoned their past grievances and are united against foreign enemies. The only thing they do not agree on is the method of national defense that should be adopted. Therefore, China is becoming unified first due to the pressure of foreign aggression. I personally am deeply disappointed with the defeat of the Chinese army, but although the war is temporarily unfavorable, the morale of the people is still available. From now on, the national self-defense psychology of the people of the whole country will be even greater than before. Therefore, the loss of Rehe has strengthened China's determination to resist to the end. The League of Nations report is obviously critical of Japan's actions. However, the Japanese government advanced into Rehe Province after the report was passed by the Extraordinary General Assembly, and staged another act of aggression. In such a situation, it is more necessary than before for the international community to exert diplomatic and economic pressure on Japan, and our people have even more right to boycott enemy goods so that they will not be dumped on our market." As Minister Guo was about to finish speaking, he mentioned that the issue of banning arms exports will be discussed in Geneva, saying, "I sincerely hope for the success of the Disarmament Conference, but I personally believe that this conference has little hope. As long as Japan does not withdraw from Chinese territory, China will not sign the Disarmament Convention for a single day. The Tokyo government will also refuse to sign it. In such a situation, how can the naval reduction demanded by the great powers be achieved? I fear that the Disarmament Conference will be shelved from now on." A certain British radio company will ask Guo Taiqi and Yosuke Matsuoka to speak on the Sino-Japanese dispute on Saturday. (9th Havas Dispatch)

U.S. Special Congress Passes Roosevelt's Emergency Bill 225

Granting the President Broad Powers to Deal with the Gold Crisis

Approving the Expansion of Currency to Assist Bank Recovery

Reuters, Washington, 9th - Both houses of Congress today passed the banking bill submitted by President Roosevelt to Congress a few hours ago, granting him the power to expand U.S. currency and continue his emergency powers to deal with banking and financial matters. The bill stipulates that national cash be concentrated in the Federal Reserve Bank and authorizes bankers to circulate Federal Reserve Bank notes to pay for U.S. government bonds, bills, drafts, and bank receipts. Such notes are issued to banks at the full value of U.S. government bonds and ninety percent of the value of all genuine bills, circulate throughout the country, are fully accepted, and can be exchanged for legal tender. The bill allows sound banks to resume operations immediately, while unsound banks must be reorganized. The bill authorizes the President, during a national emergency declared by him, to send personnel to investigate, regulate, or prohibit, in accordance with the regulations he promulgates, foreign exchange and other businesses operated by banks in the United States, as well as the export, hoarding, melting, or allocation of gold and silver coins or gold and silver bars or currency by people within the United States. Anyone who violates the provisions of this bill may be sentenced to ten years in prison and/or a fine of 10,000 yuan. The bill stipulates that the Minister of Finance may order individuals or groups or organizations to hand over all gold coins, gold bars, and gold vouchers they own to the U.S. Treasury and exchange them for any coins or currency cast or issued in accordance with U.S. law. The amount of U.S. bonds owned by all U.S. banks is currently not accurately statistically available, but according to private statistics on Wall Street, it should reach 10,000,000,000 yuan as of March 1. The amount of bank drafts and other notes that can be used as currency basis is currently impossible to determine. It is estimated that the amount currently circulating in the market is 7,250,000,000 yuan. The currency flowing in the United States in February increased by 906,000,000 yuan, totaling 6,546,000,000 yuan. The circulation of gold coins has increased from 478,837,000 yuan to 571,338,000 yuan. The nationwide per capita circulation has jumped from 45.06 yuan to 52.23 yuan. This is the highest per capita circulation since the end of October 1920, and the total circulation has reached the highest level on record.

Reuters, Washington, 9th - President Roosevelt today proposed in his address to Congress to immediately begin the operation of sound banks and proposed methods for expanding currency during the bank reorganization period. The President will ask Congress to pass two other extremely important plans as soon as possible. It is said that the extremely important plans he refers to include authorizing the President to actively reduce central government expenses (including veterans' benefits) and to organize large-scale public buildings to settle the unemployed. President Roosevelt's message to Congress reads: "I believe that this banking legislation can not only immediately dispel the public's improper doubts about sound banks, but also represent the starting point of a new relationship between American banks and the people. In order to achieve the first goal, that is, the resumption of banking, I ask Congress to immediately pass legislation authorizing the government to manage banks in order to protect depositors, and to authorize the banks that are found to be sound to resume operations as soon as possible, and to reorganize the banks that are deemed necessary to reorganize and reopen them. I request that the Federal Reserve Act be amended to provide for the issuance of appropriately increased currency with sufficient collateral to meet currency needs, without increasing the unsecured debt of the U.S. government. There is no need to say that the current situation requires immediate action. It would be unthinkable if banking convenience were to stop for a long time. If this bill is passed, this situation can be eliminated. I believe that business activities can definitely be restored in a short period of time. The new members of Congress must know the great responsibility that I and the members bear. Even in a short period of five days, it is impossible to determine a complete plan that can save the day, but this should not be a reason to delay the implementation of this first step." President Roosevelt did not say that with this action, we can proceed with the consideration of a national recovery plan.

Reuters, Washington, 9th - After the banking bill was passed by both houses of Congress, President Roosevelt immediately signed it into law. Reuters, Washington, 9th - When the Treasury Department was inquired today about how foreign banks' deposits in sound banks in New York would be handled in accordance with the new banking bill, it was answered that it is not yet possible to determine whether or under what conditions the funds can be paid out. It will be possible to speak only after a thorough study of the new bill.

Reuters, New York, 10th - With President Roosevelt's swift action, sound banks are able to reopen, and bankers and people in Wall Street are all rejoicing today. Major banks in New York are now preparing to immediately resume all normal activities. It is said that the credibility of the U.S. dollar abroad has gradually recovered.

Reuters, New York, 10th - The New York Rubber Exchange, the New York Leather Exchange, the National Metal Exchange, and the National Raw Silk Exchange will merge into a commodities exchange, effective May 1. When members discussed this proposal today, almost all of them approved it. Not a single member of the Rubber, Leather, and Metal Exchanges voted against it, but 15 of the 219 members of the Raw Silk Exchange voted against it. Now, because it is necessary to wait for the authorities to approve the new plan before engaging in finding the address of the new market, each exchange will temporarily continue to trade in the existing market. However, the committee is currently considering the advantages and disadvantages of the buildings of each exchange and will determine a suitable location in the near future. The new commodities exchange will be limited to 1,015 members, and each member will pay a membership fee of 900 yuan, so that the agency will have more than 900,000 yuan of operating capital. There are various benefits after the merger, which will save expenses, employees can be reduced, the pricing machine can be changed to use one, and each person's telephone fees can also be reduced. The new market will trade in six types of goods: rubber, leather, raw silk, silver, bronze, and tin. The latter three will still follow the current method, gathering in one place. This matter has been negotiated for two and a half years, and it has only been completed now.

Reuters, New York, 9th - The Federal Reserve Bank of St. Louis and the governor today announced that the bank holiday has been extended to Saturday morning. It is said that the states of Georgia, Washington, New Jersey, and Oregon have all extended the national bank holiday to Saturday and Sunday, and the state bank to Monday.

The German Nazi Party Takes Control of Bavaria Without Bloodshed 226

Signs of the Disintegration of the Federal System

Berlin, 9th (Reuters) - Hitler's bloodless victory in Bavaria is seen here in responsible circles as a sign of the disintegration of the German federal system. It is now expected that the central government aims to build a unified Germany, establishing a parliament in Berlin and a supreme governing body, namely the central government. The acceptance of General von Epp by the Bavarian government as an administrative commissioner was a painful decision to avoid bloodshed. This is because the National Socialist Party's stormtroopers were all armed with pistols, and if the Bavarian government had refused, they would have used force to seize all public offices. Currently, all public offices, including the parliament, are guarded by armed detachments of the National Socialist Party's stormtroopers.

Shaw Departs Japan for America 227

Yokohama, 10th (Dentsu) - Since arriving in Japan, George Bernard Shaw has engaged in Zen dialogues with Minister of the Army Araki, watched Noh plays, and enthusiastically beaten a large drum at the Waseda University Theatre Museum, showcasing his signature satire. Having exceeded his planned stay, he boarded the President liner at 8 PM last night from Yokohama, bound for the United States, which he most dislikes. Many people, both domestic and foreign, came to see him off. Mr. and Mrs. Shaw frequently waved their handkerchiefs in farewell.

Pessimism Regarding the Future of the Disarmament Conference 228

Difficulties in Reconciling French and German Opinions

British and French Behind-the-Scenes Contacts Draw Criticism from Germans

Geneva, 9th (Reuters) - When British Prime Minister MacDonald arrives here in the coming days, he will find that France and Germany hold completely conflicting views on any issue in the disarmament matter. It will be extremely difficult to find a common ground for an agreement. What is most troubling is not only the absence of the US representative to the Disarmament Conference, Davis, but also the absence of any senior German officials. The Germans have been very critical of Prime Minister MacDonald's 36-hour stopover in Paris on his way to Geneva. Today, when the Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, opened the debate at the General Committee of the Conference, he asked all countries to unanimously express goodwill towards this important matter.

Paris, 9th (Havas) - British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon departed from London at 11 AM this morning and arrived in Paris at 5:40 PM this afternoon. French Prime Minister Daladier and Foreign Minister Boncour personally welcomed them at the station. They then accompanied Mr. MacDonald and Mr. Simon to the British Embassy for an hour-long meeting. Daladier is scheduled to meet with MacDonald and Simon at the State Council at 10 AM tomorrow morning.
