After the War, it Actually Increased to Over 440,000

Chongqing Correspondence: The number of troops in Sichuan, before the major war between the two Lius, was said to be 400,000, but in reality, it was only about 370,000 to 380,000. At that time, the various armies were facing a breakdown due to the excessive number of troops and the inability to maintain their salaries. Thus, war was brewing, aiming to resolve the financial difficulties of the military through war. It was not until the issuance of the telegram by 94 generals, that the 479th war was prompted. After the signing of the ceasefire agreement, not only were none of the sixteen principles for governing Sichuan mentioned in the telegram of the 94 generals implemented, but the various warlords intensified their efforts, increased the burden on the people, and greatly expanded their troops. It is estimated that the 70,000 to 80,000 soldiers who were eliminated on the battlefield have been completely replenished, and an additional 70,000 to 80,000 soldiers have been added. Strict Hair Cutting Enforcement in Shandong Province 234

A Three-Month Deadline for Complete Hair Removal

Forced Hair Cutting After the Deadline

Jinan Correspondence: Even in the twenty-second year of the Republic of China, many ignorant villagers still wear queues. The Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, Han Fuju, recently ordered his subordinates to draft measures for cutting queues, issuing a notice to all counties to strictly enforce the measure, requiring all men in the province to no longer wear queues within three months. The seven measures were presented to the provincial government meeting on the 7th and resolved to be reviewed by the Civil Affairs and Real Estate Bureaus. The measures are as follows: (1) Men in all localities who wear queues shall have them cut off in accordance with the provisions of this method. (2) This method shall be executed by the Civil Affairs Bureau in all county and city governments. (3) The competent authorities in all districts must widely publicize this method to the public and constantly promote it in order to achieve a quick and effective result. (4) All men with queues must have their queues cut off within three months of the implementation of this method. (5) Those who still have not cut off their queues after the deadline will be dealt with in accordance with the following: (1) The competent authorities will appoint special personnel to go to the villages with the police to forcibly cut off the queues. (2) In cities, the district chiefs, and in counties, the district and town chiefs, will supervise the heads of the neighborhood to cut off the queues. (6) The county and city governments shall report the progress of queue cutting to the Civil Affairs Bureau for review and submission to the provincial government for record at the end of each month. (7) This method shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

(5) Liu Hanxiong, Commander of the 5th Division, Wang Wangen, Commander of the 13th Brigade, Yang , Commander of the 14th Brigade, and Liu also serves as Commander of the 15th Brigade, totaling 6,000 soldiers. (6) Dong Zhenggui, Commander of the Independent Division, Xing Jiqing, Commander of the th Brigade, Luo Shaolin, Commander of the 2nd Brigade, and Huang also serves as Commander of the 3rd Brigade, totaling 6,000 soldiers. The Aviation Association's Appeal to the Nation 235

National Defense Can Only Be Consolidated When the National Crisis is Relieved 236

Self-Abandonment, the Disaster of Chengde, Will Spread Throughout the Country

The Country Relies on Air Defense; the Lessons of the Three Northeastern Provinces and Rehe Are Not Far Behind

The Public Should Voluntarily Organize, and Every Penny Should Be Used

Since the fall of Chengde, some people have become disillusioned with national affairs and expressed despair, while others doubt that the aviation-based national salvation movement is too slow to be of any help in the national crisis. This morning, the China Aviation Association issued a special declaration, stating the importance of air defense and urging the people to learn from the fall of Rehe and work harder. The original text is recorded below:

The Aviation Association's Letter to the People 237

Since the establishment of this association, all parties have expressed their expectations and the whole country has provided assistance. Although the solicitation of members has not lasted more than ten days, the results are remarkable, and we are deeply gratified. However, with the fall of Chengde and the danger to North China, a few passionate individuals suddenly witnessed the light commission of national territory by one or two cowardly divisional escapees, which embarrassed the international community, and then rushed into the abyss of despair, thinking that the national affairs are like this, can I alone remain pure to the end? Alas, filling the mind with a psychology of self-abandonment is enough to erode the national fabric and more than enough to do so. Do we mean that our patriotic people are willing to perish from this point onward? How did Rehe fall? It is said that it was due to the cowardice of the commanding general, the complete lack of preparation, the inconvenience of transportation, and the obstruction of communication. This argument is correct, but if we think about it calmly, we will know that the military strength of the enemy and us is too far apart. We only rely on the ancient organization, while the enemy is rich in modern weapons. We only rely on the bravery of the army, while the enemy uses the power of the air force to control the fate of our army. Other things aside, those who gallop and gallop over mountains and ridges to detect military situations, destroy our positions, slaughter our compatriots, and demoralize our morale are the enemy planes ravaging them, which is enough to make our loyal and brave soldiers run around in vain and end up with regret? Alas, if our people learn from the fall of Chengde and from now on, they will be indifferent as if they have lost something, and no longer enthusiastically contribute to the flourishing of our aviation national defense, then the disaster of Chengde will follow and spread throughout the country. Thinking about this, how can we not shudder? It is not just about dealing with the national crisis at the moment. We live in this world, and since we cannot live without a country, the country cannot be without defense, and air defense is the newest and most effective weapon of national defense and the most effective means of self-defense. We cannot live without a country for a day, so we cannot live without air defense for a day. The lack of organization in air defense in the past has caused us to lose three provinces and trap Rehe. If, even today, we are still a nation that has long been without aerial resistance, can we ask whether our people's lives and our national fabric can be permanently secure from this point onward? This is a serious question that we hope our compatriots across the country will think about deeply and carefully. This association was organized to witness the special pain of the Songhu Incident and to urgently save the country, and now the solicitation of members coincides with the autumn when the area outside Guan fell into the hands of the enemy and Chengde was announced to have fallen. Recalling the national crisis, we feel even more inspired. Now the whole country is filled with grief and indignation, and the army has done its best to fight. If we can unite as one and save the country through aviation, and everyone joins this association as a member, then the day when the foundation of aviation national defense is consolidated will also be the autumn when our unprecedented national crisis is suddenly relieved. Time waits for no one, let us rise together. Finally, this association has something that cannot be left unsaid. This association is an organization voluntarily organized by the people. Although the government appreciates its aspirations and hires directors to supervise it, the association's affairs are conducted on the basis of the association's autonomy, and the membership fees collected are based on the association's receipts. After collection, the association's management committee is responsible for safekeeping, and the management committee is composed of the association's directors and celebrities from all walks of life. In the future, how this association will use the funds, how to develop its事业, and how to contribute to the government, will all be decided by this association based on the public's opinion. The government has no intention of helping to plan and all the funds will be used for public benefit. People from all walks of life are kindly requested to take note of this.

Various Industries Implemented the Silver Dollar Standard This Morning 238

Silver Exchange Houses Abolish the Silver Taels and Cash Market

Silver Dollar and Silver Taels Exchange Market Opened at 9 AM

Starting today, the city's various industries will implement the silver dollar standard and calculate in silver currency. Silver exchange houses have abolished the silver taels and cash market. The exchange management committee, jointly formed by the three industries, has begun operations.

Abolition of the Silver Taels and Cash Market 239

In accordance with the notice issued by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, all transactions and foreign goods will be calculated in silver currency starting today. The bank notes issued by the Northern and Southern City Exchange Houses will be based on silver currency as the main currency. The Ningbo Road Money Industry Market announced the resolution of the Money Industry Public Conference to stop operating the silver taels and cash market. Silver swaps have been changed to swap interest, but the morning gathering transactions will continue as usual. The market committee of the Banking Industry Association has stopped reporting the silver taels and cash market this morning and only handles remittance matters from various places.

Silver Dollar and Silver Taels Exchange 240

The Central, China, and Communications Banks, in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Finance, have jointly formed the Shanghai Silver Yuan and Silver Taels Exchange Management Committee, which began operations at 9 AM this morning at the cashier's department of the Central Bank's business bureau. This morning, money changers went to exchange silver taels and silver dollars. The Money Changers United Reserve Bank and other money changers all followed the regulations, first filling out a request form, stating the purpose, and after approval, they began transferring accounts at 3 PM in the afternoon.

Customs Notice 241

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Berlot, Tax Commissioner, jointly issued Notice No. 1282 yesterday regarding the calculation of various import and export taxes and transit surcharges in the new silver currency. The notice stated that, according to the government's order, the use of customs silver taels will be abolished from March 10 of this year, and the newly minted silver currency will be used instead. The fineness of this silver currency is 88, containing 23.493448 grams of pure silver. The conversion rate for customs silver taels is set at 7 mace, 1 candareen, and 9 cash. Therefore, 100 customs silver taels are equivalent to 155.80 yuan of the newly minted silver standard currency. From this date, all export taxes, transit taxes, surcharges, and various donations, which were previously collected in customs silver taels, will be calculated in this new currency. The value of local goods used for statistics, etc., should also be clearly stated in the newly minted silver standard currency. Before this new silver currency is widely circulated, the currently circulating silver dollars of other types, such as the Sun Yat-sen silver dollar, which are of equal value, will continue to be accepted as substitutes for the newly minted silver standard currency. Other types of silver dollars will be accepted at the market price. However, import taxes and other taxes collected in gold units should continue to be handled as before. This order should be implemented immediately. All merchants are hereby notified.

Two Organizations Sent Letters to the Chamber of Commerce to Pay Attention to Inferior Goods Passing Off as Domestic Goods 243

Regularly Review Production and Sales Volumes

The Nanjing Road Businessmen's Association and the First District Branch of the Citizens Association jointly sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, requesting attention to inferior goods passing off as domestic goods. The original letter stated: "To whom it may concern, according to the discussion at the members' congress of our association [on how to determine national salvation methods and implement them effectively], a majority of the attending members proposed that recently, some domestic goods manufacturers have been using the certificates of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and domestic goods organizations to secretly replace trademarks with inferior goods, especially printing and dyeing factories and cotton yarn merchants. Therefore, it was resolved that we should immediately send letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and domestic goods organizations, requesting that they pay close attention to whether the production volume of domestic goods manufacturers matches the sales volume, and review them regularly." The matter concerns the fundamental plan for national salvation and should be approved. We are sending you the records and ask that you investigate and implement them.

Chiang Kai-shek and Kong Xiangxi Will Go to Nanjing Tonight 244

Chiang Tso-pin and Kong Xiangxi returned to the country and arrived in Shanghai one after another. After a tiring journey, they rested for a day or two and are scheduled to take the night train to Nanjing tonight to report to the Central Government on the diplomatic and inspection situation.

The Plummeting of European and American Export Goods 245

Since the outbreak of the hot war, North China has become tense, and transportation has mostly stopped. In addition, the recent intense financial turmoil has had a greater impact on export businesses. The investigation and report are as follows:

Within this week in Europe, the cargo volume of Shanghai's European liners has sharply declined. The Great British Mail Steamer, which usually has the most business, also only carried 220 bundles of Huzhou silk and 50 tons of Chinese tea on its latest voyage. This is only about 20% of its usual capacity. French mail steamers leaving port had no goods to carry at all, only oriental silk and cloth were shipped to Europe. The Italian mail steamer leaving port only carried a few samples. According to shipping industry insiders, the market has been stagnant since the hot war, and nobody is shipping goods. This level of decline is rarely seen.

There are too many Sino-American liners and an overabundance of tonnage on the American route. The Pacific Mail Steamship Company's ships have carried no more than 100 tons of cargo each time in the past ten days. The export cargo of the Japan Mail Company (NYK) is even less. For example, the over 20,000-ton Ryuyo Maru to America only carried 30 or 40 tons of cargo. Other ships such as the Standatol and Shelver are only loaded with incoming goods and have no outgoing cargo. The Sino-American New Company's ships have a small amount of freight because they are not part of the conference.

Germany to Change National Flag 246

German Residents in this City Prefer the Old National Flag

The "North China Daily News" reports: Will Germany adopt the black, red, and gold tricolor flag as its national flag, or will it change back to the old black, white, and red tricolor flag? This is a question that Germany will solve. German residents in this city are calmly awaiting the decision. According to German telegrams, the National Socialist Party has already lowered the black, red, and gold republican flag and raised the old black, white, and red flag, with the National Socialist Party swastika emblem in the center. However, Shanghai has not yet changed it. When the German Consulate General in Shanghai was asked about this matter yesterday, they replied that the black, red, and gold tricolor flag is stipulated in the constitution of the German Republic. If the new parliament resolves to amend the clause on the national flag in the constitution, or if the president issues a special order to change the national flag, Shanghai will immediately change it. As for the feelings of the German residents in this city regarding the change to the old flag, a respected figure told a "North China Daily News" representative that the German residents in this city have always been dissatisfied with the replacement of the black, white, and red national flag with the black, red, and gold tricolor, but as law-abiding citizens, they have no choice but to comply. He also said that Germans feel a certain significance in being under the black, white, and red tricolor flag, because Germany was a world power when this flag was used, so everyone respected it. Although it is uncertain whether Germany will be able to regain its status as a major power in the future, the restoration of the flag of its former glorious era is welcomed by the Germans in Shanghai.

Today is Japanese Army Memorial Day 247

Today's Japanese-language "Shanghai Daily News" states that today is the 28th Japanese Army Memorial Day, which commemorates the defeat of the Russian army near Fengtian by the Japanese army during the Russo-Japanese War in the Meiji 37th and 38th years (1904-1905), and the defeat of the Russian Baltic Fleet by the Japanese navy in the naval battle of the Sea of Japan. This memorial day is celebrated together with the Navy Memorial Day on May 27th. The Japanese military attache in this city will be fully mobilized to hold commemorative lectures. Talking Points

Siam 256

— Geng

For eighteen long months, the national crisis has yet to come to an end. On one hand, our country has to grit its teeth and endure the various wounds that the violent Japan constantly inflicts upon us, and on the other hand, we have to put on a forced smile and wait quietly for the League of Nations to make a decision. At this time of hardship and devastation, any ray of hope is enough to bring some comfort. This is especially true when multiple small countries can speak out for justice at each League of Nations meeting. Unexpectedly, recent events have brought a flood of bad news. Siam, our small neighbor, has suddenly become known for its [flattery of Japan] and [anti-Chinese sentiment].

Siam and China are both small and weak Asian countries. Due to the long history and close geographical relationship, there are more than two million Chinese and mixed-race people in Siam's population of over nine million, and its royal family is also of Chinese descent. Therefore, their international relations should be interdependent and mutually supportive. However, Siam, for some unknown reason, is taking advantage of our crisis to vigorously stir up trouble for us, acting like a [dog kicking a rabbit downhill]. First, it abstained from voting on the League of Nations report, which clearly fueled the flames of the violent Japan. Then, it purchased large quantities of military supplies from Europe and resold them to Japan. Most recently, it promulgated a law requiring primary schools to teach Siamese for at least 25 hours per week, clearly aiming to restrict the Chinese schools run by our overseas Chinese from having time to teach Chinese. Why is Siam willing to act as a pawn for the violent Japan and act like a tiger?

According to Article 16, Paragraph 1 of the Covenant of the League of Nations, [Should any Member of the League resort to war in disregard of its covenants under Article 12, 13 or 15, it shall ipso facto be deemed to have committed an act of war against all other Members of the League, which hereby undertake immediately to subject it to the severance of all trade or financial relations]. The violent Japan is a country that violates the Covenant of the League of Nations, and Siam is a member state that has the [obligation to sever relations with countries that violate the Covenant]. However, not only does it not sever relations with the violent Japan, but it also goes against its conscience and engages in [flattering Japan] and [anti-Chinese] activities. Is this not going against the tide to the extreme?

Moreover, even Western powers are deeply uneasy about Japan's continental policy of [To conquer the world, first conquer China]. Siam, a small country in the near east, does not seem to realize the vital importance of [The strength of your neighbor is the weakness of yours], [If the lips are gone, the teeth will be cold], and to recognize early on who will be my strong enemy and who will be my best friend. Is this not greatly perplexing?

As for yesterday's report denying Siam's sale of military supplies, it further demonstrates the Siamese people's deliberately ambiguous attitude to confuse the world. Those who bear the great responsibility of diplomatic negotiation must pay close attention to this!

Small Poems on Current Affairs 257

A futile effort to act as a bulwark is like lukewarm water; When enemy soldiers invade, they panic in disarray. What comes of losing soldiers and land? Abandoning our border is truly heartbreaking.

The fall of Liaoning and Jilin was already lamentable; The loss of Rehe is even more alarming and disconcerting. The shrinking territory still fails to awaken them; When will they rise up and recover the lost lands?

Science

Aerial Surveying 258

— Yan Jin

The development of modern science has truly been advancing at a rapid pace. Furthermore, in order to increase the effectiveness of lethal weapons, many astonishing new techniques have been discovered in the implementation of military science. The recent aerial surveying is one of these thousands of techniques.

The trajectory of a shell fired into the air is an arc-shaped parabola. The distances calculated on the most detailed military maps using a scale are horizontal distances. This is something that anyone with basic knowledge knows. However, the ground is never completely flat. The elevation differences between locations A and B can never be said to be completely on the same horizontal line. Therefore, many artillerymen, despite having extremely precise machinery and subtle calculations, still fail to hit their targets with their bullets. For this reason, the need for aerial surveying has arisen spontaneously.

The personnel required for aerial surveying are not ordinary land surveyors. What is needed are aviation personnel who can also take photographs. The method of surveying is extremely simple. It only requires using a specially made camera (like those used for filming movies) to continuously photograph the ground from a height of about two hundred feet.

After the photography is completed, the negatives are developed and printed like photographs. Because only one side of each negative is usable and clear, to have a completely usable topographic map, considerable editing is required. Once everything is ready, it can be printed on a flat sheet of blueprint paper.

The elevation in the photograph can be determined by the depth of the color. The topographic photograph that has been taken can be used by the draftsman to draw many perspective lines from it, and from this, the accurate elevation of the terrain can be calculated. By understanding the horizontal and vertical distances between the two locations, it is not difficult for the soldiers firing the artillery to calculate the exact distance at which they should fire the bullet. This allows every shot to hit its target, with no wasted shots. This is truly an astonishing event.

It is said that the Japanese military aircraft that appeared daily over the Rehe border several weeks ago without firing any bullets were their survey aircraft.

Half a Dozen Unexpected Things 259

— Sun Choucheng

The country with the largest army in the world was unexpectedly invaded by troops from a small country of three islands, who rampaged through the territory without any effective resistance. This is truly unexpected.

Having tens of thousands of soldiers defending key passes, while 128 enemy soldiers effortlessly occupy Chengde, is truly unexpected.

Despite declarations of resisting to the last soldier and the last gun, they fled with a brigade and a regiment while still far from the enemy. This is truly unexpected.

Holding a doctrine of non-resistance, handing over the three northeastern provinces, and then expressing great rage and demanding strict punishment upon hearing that subordinates fled without a fight, is truly unexpected.

Three thousand rickshaws, pulled by soldiers to transport supplies to the battlefield, happened to arrive at Gubeikou when Chengde fell, and refugees from outside the pass fled into the pass, competing to hire vehicles, resulting in a threefold increase in market profits. This is truly unexpected.

The dignified head of the Executive Yuan personally went north to inspect and knew that Rehe could only be defended for one week to ten days. At the time, he did not think of remedies but made flippant remarks afterward. This is truly unexpected.

Special National Crisis Donation 260

— Bo Ping

In front of a large building off a busy street, suddenly came four middle school students in the same color uniforms, wearing school badges. Two of them were holding white bamboo cloth flags, one was carrying a large bundle of flyers, and one was carrying a black leather bag. Their faces all had solemn and heroic expressions, and their steps were neat and clear.

Suddenly, they stopped in front of the building and went up a few stone steps, looking into the gatehouse. A middle-aged man in a coarse cloth shirt came out. They did not wait for him to ask and explained that they wanted to see the owner here. After hearing this, the middle-aged man frowned, but seeing that they were all civilized people, he reluctantly led them in. After passing through several winding doors, they sat down in a magnificent reception room. They thought: [With such a grand setting, today's donation will be at least one hundred or fifty at the lowest.] So they all held their breath and listened quietly as the man in the coarse cloth shirt announced:

[Master: There are several students from洋 school (modern style school) here asking to see you.]

[Damn it, is your rice bowl full? Always bringing these little devils to make fun of me. Get out! Humph....]

[Um, um! Master, take a deep breath and smoke a pipe.]

It seemed that something had been stuffed into the master's mouth, and there was a real silence for a while, with only the opium smoke permeating the inner room.

[Mr. Wang: You really don't know my troubles these past few days. The little devils keep talking about the national crisis. Do you think I have the heart for that? My eldest son has lung disease and is lying in the hospital, and my youngest son has contracted the spring epidemic and needs to see a doctor. Your mistress also has a relapse of her old illness, and my daughter is getting married next month, and she is making a fuss about getting a dowry every day. National crisis, national crisis, I can't even take care of my family's troubles! It's really hateful! Sigh!]

[Um, um! Master, take a deep breath again. Are you still standing there waiting to be scolded? Go quickly and reply to the little devils and don't bring them in here again in the future.]

[Yes, yes, thank you, Master Wang.] The man came out with a long face and glared at the students.

The four young people who were running for the country could not help but be filled with anger. They quickly left the reception room, but they could hear the conversation inside again.

[Wang Xingkuang: Think about it for me, how can my sons' illnesses be resolved? Alas!]

[Yes, yes, Master, I will definitely go to the Dabei Temple tomorrow and ask the head to send a few monks to perform the Star宿 ritual for the young masters. It's okay, Master: spend a few more repentance coins, and it will surely make the young masters lively and energetic again. Okay, Master, have another pipe.]

[Mr. Wang, you must be tired, have a pipe too!][Oh! Thank you, Master.]

Alas! A long sigh spread from the mouths of the four young people full of patriotism into the air.

Conversational Haiku 261

Flew Away Without Wings 262

— Geng

This was on a particularly fast second-class train in the morning.

[Sir, excuse me, can I borrow your lighter?] A middle-aged man with a well-trimmed mustache, his face full of smiles, came over to the young man who was gleaming, dressed in a Western suit, and leaning against the window smoking a cigar.

[The porter has lighters!] The young man quickly moved a new leather bag, which looked quite plump, on the tea table closer to the train wall, and even put a hand on it as if afraid it would fly away. Then, he exhaled two smoke rings, ignoring the middle-aged man.

In less than three minutes, a pretty Peace (brand cigarettes) modern girl, stylishly dressed, rushed over. Her ears and slender玉指 were decorated with glittering ornaments. Looking at an empty seat near a sitting armed comrade, she seemed ashamed to be with them, and in a flash, she shifted her gaze to the young man's face and gasped, [What bad luck, one step too late and there are no seats!]

[Uh!] The young man seemed to have been electrified. He only moved his臀部 and precisely gave up a seat.

[Thank you!] She smiled and sat down.

[You are welcome!]

[Sir, you are so kind. What is your honorable name? Where did you make your fortune?]

[My surname is Jin. I just returned from Belgium and am now doing a small job in the Budget Bureau of the National Government.]

[Oh, Mr. Jin is going to Nanjing. I am also going to Nanjing. However, I have never been to Nanjing. Near the Ministry of Education, I don't know if there are any beautiful hotels?]

[The Central Hotel is extremely beautiful! Perhaps the lady wants to be promoted in the Ministry of Education?]

[It's just a plan. If it doesn't succeed, I will have to ask you for a strong introduction!]

[How dare I!] Mr. Jin was overjoyed.

[Kunshan is here! Kunshan is here!] The porter shouted loudly; the train also stopped.

[The spring scenery is more beautiful than a painting, it's so lovely! Mr. Jin, would you like to take a look?] The lady leaned her head in from the train window, seeming to want to invite her companion to enjoy the beautiful scenery together. She only slightly tilted her head, but her left ear brushed against the train window, and she cried out [Ah! Mr.! What to do? My diamond earring fell off!]

Mr. Jin realized that the train was about to leave, so he quickly stretched out his head and looked down, and sure enough, he saw a golden shimmering earring shining beside the train tracks. So he volunteered to be quick on his feet, took big steps out of the train to pick up the earring for her. When he returned to his original seat, he exclaimed in surprise, [Ah! Did I get on the wrong train? Why can't I see the lady's beautiful figure and my leather bag containing 5,000 yuan in cash?]

Only the [Woo woo woo] sound of the train was heard, and the young man, who was holding the gold-plated and glass-like "precious" earring, his eyes dazed and fascinated, only saw the electric poles and the fields of ditches and furrows gradually moving, fleeting, and disappearing into the thick smoke and mist in the rear!

Shop Clerk Correspondence

Making an Appearance 263

— Lao Shaozhou

Mr. Editor:

A relative of mine, let's call him Jia, partnered with a friend in his hometown to open a money shop, with Jia acting as the manager. This year, the shop's shareholders underwent some changes. A new shareholder, Yi, couldn't appear publicly due to family reasons. Since Jia had no other shareholders he could rely on, he consulted me, asking me to make a public appearance on his behalf. Considering our family ties, I couldn't bear to see his endeavor, about to succeed, fail in an instant, so I readily agreed. All formal documents were to be signed and sealed by me publicly. However, Yi and I signed a separate private agreement, with Jia as a witness, using the shop's letterhead and Jia's personal seal. It stated that Yi alone would enjoy all profits and bear all losses of the shop in the future, without any involvement on my part. Looking back, I realize I was a bit hasty at the time. Now, I have some questions:

(1) Is this private agreement legally binding?

(2) If the shop fails and incurs losses exceeding its capital, and Yi is unable to bear the responsibility, will I be held liable?

Your wisdom is highly regarded, I hope you can provide an answer. (omitted below)

Respectfully, Lao Shaozhou

XXXX

Editor's Note: This kind of acting as a front for someone else is very common in society, and many disputes arise from it. Here are the answers to Mr. Lao's two questions: The first is "of course it is effective." Although contracts are said to require formalities, sometimes even if the formalities are not complete, as long as they are sufficient to "express intent," they are considered valid in law. The answer to the second question is more complex. If the amount of the loss is within Yi's capacity to bear, then unless he is a minor or legally incapacitated, he cannot escape this responsibility. If the amount of the loss exceeds Yi's capacity, then you will be responsible. In short, the private agreement you and Yi signed is, of course, somewhat confidential and not public. Legal regulations stipulate that this type of contract is only effective between the parties involved and cannot be used against unknowing third parties. Therefore, in the unfortunate event that the loss exceeds the capital, Mr. Lao is primarily responsible, and Yi is only responsible to Mr. Lao.

Fiction

Coal Mountain (Continued) 264

— by Ep Falkowski, Abridged Translation by Zhixiang

[Doesn't the contract clearly state that we must cooperate with the mining factory? To enable the development of the entire mine and restore the old position of the anthracite industry in the market, we must fulfill all the provisions of the contract.]

[I would like to advise you: the executive committee absolutely cannot help actions that violate the contract. Or do you want to continue the strike! But, within the scope of our power, we will not help you. Such illegal actions cannot receive economic assistance. If you want to strike, then other misfortunes will befall you. You have work to do, food to eat, and you won't starve to death, you should be satisfied!]

He then said to the last speaker: [I know you, you are a Red radical! A special envoy from the Central Coal Miners Union, here to disrupt our American coal mines. I will seek the consent of the Executive Committee to deport such extremists. In my opinion, what he said tonight is the culmination of everything.]

The meeting place became even more tense and uneasy. [Hit him!] [Expel him!] Various voices rang out.

Stroebel used his monkey eyes to stare at the audience, trying to identify the criminals.

[I have a proposal,] someone shouted amidst the chaos.

[Order, brothers!] The chairman shouted into the noisy wave, [Someone has a proposal!]

[Starting tomorrow, we will go on strike until our working conditions improve.]

[Seconded!]

[This proposal is illegal,] the executive committee member's face changed color, clenching his fists and shouting.

[Call for a vote, call for a vote!] A shout swept in like a hurricane.

[All in favor, say [Aye]!] The chairman said into the clamor.

[Aye]. It erupted from the entire hall. The loud sound shook the photo of the founding union hanging on the wall, but his face showed an indifferent look.

[I don't care anymore,] Stroebel shouted loudly, then grabbed his hat and pipe and angrily walked out the door. [Wait! You'll see what victory you can get.] He said angrily as he left.

His escape caused the miners in the entire place to laugh sarcastically. Now they all left their seats and continued the meeting more fiercely. After Stroebel left, their unity became even stronger.

Standing in the back, Peter felt his blood flowing quickly, his blood vessels seemed about to burst.

Peter's tone also gradually swelled and shouted [Strike!]. He knew why! He deeply felt the pain and wounds accumulated over thousands of years! He also recalled the various situations he had experienced when he first entered the mine.

[Several of us will be expelled from the union.] Tim said.

[They will also expel the rest of us.]

[In this way, we must have a new organization to bravely attack the union that deceived us, and not be abused by those union officials who are afraid of losing their positions.]

Outside the meeting place, a line of light like red hair hung in the dark sky, and the cold wind blew the lamps on the street corners. The street was also calm at this time. The rich people in the city were leisurely indulging in sweet dreams. In such silence, only the sound of the coal mine's water pump kept coming. Peter, dressed in thin clothes, shivered. He wondered what his wife would think of this. Should he wake her up and tell her? No, it wouldn't be too late to tell her tomorrow, unless she was waiting for him to return… he used to wait for him to return, listening to the sound of the door…

Tomorrow, in this old mine, major changes will begin… Tomorrow, that evil place will begin to change…! (The End)

Film Supplement

Jeanne Crain After the Divorce 265

— Zhongqin

After the news of Jeanne Crain's divorce from her husband was announced, newspapers in various countries published it in prominent positions. But what was the inside story of Jeanne Crain's divorce? What was Jeanne's intention in divorcing? There are many speculations from the outside world, and the rumors are divergent. Now, let's talk about the important points from the conversations published by her mother and her attorney, and we will have a conclusion.

Jeanne's attorney said; Jeanne entrusted him and Lee Dudelbeck to file for divorce a total of three times. The previous two times were conducted secretly, and the results were reconciliations. Therefore, very few outsiders knew about it. The reasons why Jeanne wanted a divorce were not very sufficient. The first time was because Jeanne was building a villa by the sea for summer vacations. She advocated building a delicate promenade on the beach, like a pier, while Lee Dudelbeck was vehemently opposed, advocating building a garden. The two quarreled because of this, and Jeanne used this as a reason for divorce. The second time was because Jeanne danced with a man at a banquet, and Lee Dudelbeck made a big scene with Jeanne because of this, almost resorting to violence. After these two incidents occurred, Jeanne went to Honolulu to live, and Lee Dudelbeck followed her both times to apologize to Jeanne. So she withdrew the lawsuit. The third time was this time, and there was no reason at all, just a disagreement between the two sides.

Jeanne's mother said; [There is nothing I disagree with my son-in-law about. He treats me like his own mother. Jeanne filed for divorce with him a total of three times, but in fact, there were five disagreements before and after. Every time they quarreled, Jeanne became ill because of it, and the reasons for the quarrels were not very sufficient. Once, they even quarreled about eating vegetables. I asked Jeanne carefully, but she couldn't tell me any reason.

Judging from the conversations of the two people, it can be seen that the marriage between Jeanne and Lee Dudelbeck was not entirely out of her own will, otherwise, without any sufficient reason, why would she have filed for divorce three times? Therefore, the saying that Jeanne married Lee Dudelbeck to spite Claire Farrell can be further confirmed. Now Farrell has resolutely resigned, indicating his farewell to Jeanne, but Jeanne has already fallen in love with Farrell and cannot stay with Lee Dudelbeck for the rest of her life. Now that Farrell is gone, Jeanne cannot recover, so she filed for divorce to show that she has not forgotten Farrell.

Jeanne's intention is like this, but what will Farrell do about it? According to reliable news, after Jeanne announced her divorce, the telephone at Claire Farrell's house rang non-stop. His friends all reported to him and inquired about how he would express himself. He received more than 20,000 letters in one week asking if he and Jeanne would reconcile. Although he stated that his relationship with his wife, Virginia, would not be affected by Jeanne, people in Hollywood do not believe that he is telling the truth. It is expected that the divorce between Farrell and Virginia is also a matter of time.

Film Review

Review of A Bill of Divorcement 266

— Linghe

Anyone who has seen John Barrymore's performance, I think, will admire the depth of his acting. Although not every work is very successful, he will never disappoint us in any way. Just take this film as an example, compared to the role he played in Grand Hotel, it is a stunning success. Of course, this has a close relationship with the script, and the plot of [A Bill of Divorcement] can enable him to maximize his performance.

In order to make a more rigorous review of this play, it is necessary to briefly describe the story of this film.

During the First World War, how many happy families were separated because of it? There was a Hilary (played by John Barrymore), who was injured in his nerves due to the war and was admitted to a mental hospital for more than ten years. When he recovered and returned home, he fully expected to receive his wife's love and comfort. But he knew that his wife had already remarried because she did not want to live a widowed life, and the wedding date was imminent. At this time, Hilary's grief was naturally reasonable, and his wife was also trapped in the contradiction of love because of this. As a result, the madman Hilary realized the sincerity of his wife's love for her new husband, so he resolutely took his daughter and lived his miserable life. At that time, Hilary's daughter was also in love, but she knew that she must have a hereditary mental illness and was afraid of harming her children in the future, so she resolutely broke away from her lover and served her poor old father for the rest of her life.

In such a story, it can be said that there is no character in it that we can criticize. Although Hilary's actions are unbearable, they are also very reasonable for the sake of love and for her future. Of course, Hilary's daughter's resolute solitary life is also very admirable for her strength of reason. However, the most bitter thing is this mentally ill Hilary. If so, all the characters are so good, then it is indeed not easy to achieve success in the performance, because it is not easy to make the audience sympathize with all the people, but this is achieved in this film, so this is the success of this film.

The entire play is performed, of course, with Barrymore bearing the most strenuous role, therefore, the director of this film also specially focuses on Barrymore. But he also paid special attention to the madman's daughter (Katharine Hepburn). He is unremitting in the progress of the entire painting. They are used simply and powerfully. Especially for the inner performance of each character, he fully gives the actors the opportunity to play. Especially in the last scene, he completely entrusted the important and difficult plot to the tone of Peana, so that the audience received his powerful stimulation. This point makes us have to admire the strength of his methods. At the beginning, in order to introduce the plot, it has a stage play tone, which is always somewhat unexciting.

The use of lighting makes this play even more colorful, which makes us believe that a soft light is very suitable for tragedy, but if it can also be dim and clear (such as the light in [A Farewell to Arms]), it should be more beautiful and increase the power of this play. There is a lot of dialogue, but it is all necessary, the sound recording has reached a perfect state, and the scenery is also very suitable.

Finally, regarding the skills of the actors, in addition to John's profound and detailed performance as mentioned above, the newcomer actress who plays the daughter is also very worthy of our attention. Her face and movements are similar to Greta Garbo, perhaps because she is trying her best to imitate Garbo. The rest of the people are not brilliant, but they do not destroy the plot.

Modern Film Publication 267

[Modern Film] monthly magazine, was founded by Liu Na'ou, Chen Binghong, Wu Yunmeng, Huang Tianshi, Huang Jiamo, and Zong Weigeng. After a long period of preparation, it has already been published a few days ago. The content aims to promote high-level taste and develop film art, with equal emphasis on pictures and texts, exquisite printing, and the writers are all famous figures in the film industry. The inaugural issue contains works by Sun Yu, Cai Chusheng, Cheng Bugao, Shen Xiling, Ai Xia, and Lu Xiaoluo, and can be called a film publication that stands out. Audiences who love film art can directly subscribe to the Modern Film Magazine at No. 64 Beijing Road, 5th Floor.

Audience Opinions

Review of City Nights 268

— Pingying

In this city of magnificent buildings and brilliant lights, all that meets the eye are wine, meat, cars… things like enjoyment. However, although the appearance is like this, the underground is buried with tens of thousands of people who have been exploited by the rich until their flesh and blood are exhausted, and they still have to work hard all day and all night, selling their physical strength. Lianhua Company's [City Nights] is aimed at depicting the evils of the city, exposing the dark curtain of the city, and instructing promising young people not to be anesthetized by the nature of the city of drunken gold and paper fans. What a meaningful film this is!

The screenwriter's skills are superb, which really makes us praise him. He never relaxes in revealing the disparity between classes and the contrast between rich and poor, especially when the female worker sees that her father's illness is critical, she is fired from the factory, and there is almost no money or rice at home, she makes the greatest determination to endure the pain and do what she disdains to do 丨丨 to throw her own body into the world of demons. And her father's indignation and determination after discovering her behavior. This truly demonstrates the consciousness and identity of a true worker.

The director's skills are also really good, he can command the actors as he pleases in the plot.

In terms of actors, Jin Yan and the child star Li Keng are just right. Ruan Lingyu is the most successful one in this film. Her movements and expressions make it impossible to find a single flaw from beginning to end. The rest of Wang Guilin and Li Junpan are also okay. Liu Jiqun plays the little celebrity in the film, and his identity is very suitable. Although the supporting roles of Zhang Meimei and Tang Tianyu are not very natural, they cannot reduce the color of this film.

The camera is still flexible, and the scenery is not bad, but it is redundant to explain in the subtitles which volume is finished, and it is unnecessary.

All in all; this film can be called a masterpiece among domestic products.

Talking about [City Nights] 269

— Sheng Hong

After watching [City Nights], which exposes the sins of special classes and calls for the oppressed masses, we deeply feel that Lianhua Film Company has achieved great success.

The sincerity of this film has grasped the current era in China, depicting the enjoyment of the rich and the suffering of the proletariat, which is truly incisive. Of course, this [City Nights] is also a film that the public needs and is also a contribution that closely follows the times?

We extremely admire the director's intelligence in the interweaving of the film. He contrasts the families of the wealthy with the families of the coolies, so that the audience can understand the happiness and suffering of the wealthy and the coolies. [So many people are homeless, what home am I going back to!] can be said to be the most powerful words in the whole film. The comparison between the cats of the rich and the cats of the coolies has great significance, making the audience's emotions more tense. When Ruan Lingyu played the old father who had to sell his body because of illness, it really made the audience's heartstrings tense and shocked with the heart of the people in the play.

When it comes to actors, Ruan Lingyu is the most successful. In the scenes of looking for her old father in the torrential rain, she shed tears, which made people… made the audience shed a few tears of sympathy. Jin…'s performance did not show his genius, but his suave and unrestrained appearance… quite helped the development of the plot.

The director's credit accounts for half of the success of [City Nights]. In addition to the interweaving that makes the audience admire, he also has high opinions on the actors' matching and pairing.

Joan Crawford Has a Good Year to Live 270

— Luofen

When Joan Crawford traveled to Europe with Little Van Banks last year, she met a doctor who determined that Joan Crawford was suffering from chronic inflammation of the central nervous system and would have a risk of cerebral congestion. He advised Joan Crawford to take a temporary rest and not work on the screen. Crawford smiled and ignored it. … After returning to the United States, she still lived on the screen. Now Joan Crawford suddenly suffered from headaches. Little Van Banks did not forget what happened last year and immediately hired a famous doctor to diagnose her. It is said that Joan's nerves have reached a dangerous state due to excessive thinking. If she continues to appear on the screen, she will definitely die after a year. Little Van Banks heard this terrible diagnosis and planned to order Joan Crawford to resign. Joan still planned to finish filming the new film [Turnabout] before deciding. Little Van Banks has been… very worried and is still trying to persuade her,

Movie novel

Rasputin (13) 271

— Time

She wanted to warn the queen, but this queen mother was too superstitious about Rasputin and was too deeply poisoned. She would never listen to her warning. And Paul was no longer by the emperor's side to help her. Her distrust of him had forced him away alive.

One night, Rasputin went to the palace, … entered her boudoir, wanting to … comfort her, wanting to indulge in her arms, Nita … angrily resisted his insult, and her … small delicate body was there his opponent. Rasputin laughed and pushed her down. When she was unable to do anything, his eyes stared deeply at her.

[Sleep, my little baby,] he ordered.

So, as obedient as the little prince, as submissive as the other noble ladies, Nitaga was also subdued by him. She immediately fell into a deep sleep. Rasputin smiled and looked at her.

His … fire suddenly went out. He didn't want her because she had resisted him like this. There were more valuable prizes to be had. The emperor's eldest daughter, … Lina, had grown up, and she was sleeping in the next room.

He eagerly walked into the door. He inadvertently … knocked a candlestick … to the ground. There was a sudden … rapid sound of footsteps outside. He waited furtively. When the door opened, the queen was standing there.

[Father, you scared me to death!] she gasped. After a while, she said: [Why is this candlestick on the ground?]

Rasputin smiled cunningly and said: [In our Siberia, on St. John's Night, we burn fires in the woods, and people jump over the fires… to make our blessings rise to the sky in the fire. I was just demonstrating it to Nitaga.]

The queen seemed lost in thought. She suddenly … looked at the room over there. [But Nitaga is already asleep… You… What are you doing in the … Lina's room?] She didn't wait for a reply and hurried to Nitaga's room. [What's wrong with her… Is she sick?] she … shouted. [Her eyes are open….]

[I was just talking to her,] Rasputin defended. [She was very tired. So I put her to sleep.]

The girl was awakened by them, and with a slight groan, she struggled to break free from the shackles that bound her. The queen ran over and hugged her in her arms, asking her why this was happening.

Nitaga moved tiredly, Nitaga wanted to struggle to stand up. She said [Rasputin charmed me! He wanted to insult me, and in the end, I saw him go to … Lina's room… He wants her too. I … saw him in a daze, but … I didn't have the strength to call for help.] (To be continued)
